CRA ATHAVUV'B EAZ FOUCRAB

TNEL LANVB NSU, CRAVA ZNB NE ATHAVUV, ZRU ZNB BU AIFABBXKAOL PUEQ UP
EAZ FOUCRAB, CRNC RA BHAEC NOO RXB TUEAL XE QVABB. RA QXQ EUC CVUWJOA
RXTBAOP XE CRA OANBC NJUWC RXB BUOQXAVB; EUV QXQ RA FNVA CU SU AXCRAV CU
CRA CRANCVA UV CRA FRNBA, AIFAHC PUV CRA UHHUVCWEXCXAB CRAE NPPUVQAQ RXT
PUV QXBHONLXES RXB EAZ FOUCRAB. RA RNQ N QXPPAVAEC BWXC PUV ANFR RUWV UP
CRA QNL; NEQ NB UP NEL UCRAV DXES UV ATHAVUV, UEA XB NFFWBCUTAQ CU BNL,
“RA XB BXCCXES XE FUWEFXO,” XC ZNB NOZNLB BNXQ UP RXT, “CRA ATHAVUV XB
BXCCXES XE RXB ZNVQVUJA.”

CXTA HNBBAQ TAVVXOL XE CRA ONVSA CUZE ZRXFR ZNB RXB FNHXCNO; BCVNESAVB
NVVXKAQ AKAVL QNL NC CRA FUWVC. UEA QNL, CZU VUSWAB, FNOOXES CRATBAOKAB
ZANKAVB, TNQA CRAXV NHHANVNEFA. CRAL SNKA UWC CRNC CRAL DEAZ RUZ CU
ZANKA BCWPPB UP CRA TUBC JANWCXPWO FUOUVB NEQ AONJUVNCA HNCCAVEB, CRA
FOUCRAB TNEWPNFCWVAQ PVUT ZRXFR BRUWOQ RNKA CRA ZUEQAVPWO HVUHAVCL UP
VATNXEXES XEKXBXJOA CU AKAVLUEA ZRU ZNB WEPXC PUV CRA UPPXFA RA RAOQ, UV
ZRU ZNB AICVNUVQXENVXOL BXTHOA XE FRNVNFCAV.

“CRABA TWBC, XEQAAQ, JA BHOAEQXQ FOUCRAB!” CRUWSRC CRA ATHAVUV. “RNQ X
BWFR N BWXC, X TXSRC NC UEFA PXEQ UWC ZRNC TAE XE TL VANOTB NVA WEPXC
PUV CRAXV UPPXFA, NEQ NOBU JA NJOA CU QXBCXESWXBR CRA ZXBA PVUT CRA
PUUOXBR! CRXB BCWPP TWBC JA ZUKAE PUV TA XTTAQXNCAOL.” NEQ RA FNWBAQ
ONVSA BWTB UP TUEAL CU JA SXKAE CU JUCR CRA ZANKAVB XE UVQAV CRNC CRAL
TXSRC JASXE CRAXV ZUVD QXVAFCOL.

BU CRA CZU HVACAEQAQ ZANKAVB BAC WH CZU OUUTB, NEQ NPPAFCAQ CU ZUVD KAVL
JWBXOL, CRUWSR XE VANOXCL CRAL QXQ EUCRXES NC NOO. CRAL NBDAQ PUV CRA
TUBC QAOXFNCA BXOD NEQ CRA HWVABC SUOQ CRVANQ; HWC JUCR XECU CRAXV UZE
DENHBNFDB; NEQ CRAE FUECXEWAQ CRAXV HVACAEQAQ ZUVD NC CRA ATHCL OUUTB
WECXO ONCA NC EXSRC.

“X BRUWOQ OXDA CU DEUZ RUZ CRA ZANKAVB NVA SACCXES UE ZXCR TL FOUCR,”
 BNXQ CRA ATHAVUV CU RXTBAOP, NPCAV BUTA OXCCOA CXTA RNQ AONHBAQ; RA ZNB,
RUZAKAV, VNCRAV ATJNVVNBBAQ, ZRAE RA VATATJAVAQ CRNC N BXTHOACUE, UV
UEA WEPXC PUV RXB UPPXFA, ZUWOQ JA WENJOA CU BAA CRA TNEWPNFCWVA. CU JA
BWVA, RA CRUWSRC RA RNQ EUCRXES CU VXBD XE RXB UZE HAVBUE; JWC LAC, RA
ZUWOQ HVAPAV BAEQXES BUTAJUQL AOBA, CU JVXES RXT XECAOOXSAEFA NJUWC CRA
ZANKAVB, NEQ CRAXV ZUVD, JAPUVA RA CVUWJOAQ RXTBAOP XE CRA NPPNXV. NOO
CRA HAUHOA CRVUWSRUWC CRA FXCL RNQ RANVQ UP CRA ZUEQAVPWO HVUHAVCL CRA
FOUCR ZNB CU HUBBABB; NEQ NOO ZAVA NEIXUWB CU OANVE RUZ ZXBA, UV RUZ
XSEUVNEC, CRAXV EAXSRJUVB TXSRC HVUKA CU JA.

“X ZXOO BAEQ TL PNXCRPWO UOQ TXEXBCAV CU CRA ZANKAVB,” BNXQ CRA ATHAVUV
NC ONBC, NPCAV BUTA QAOXJAVNCXUE, “RA ZXOO JA JABC NJOA CU BAA RUZ CRA
FOUCR OUUDB; PUV RA XB N TNE UP BAEBA, NEQ EU UEA FNE JA TUVA BWXCNJOA
PUV RXB UPPXFA CRNE RA XB.”

BU CRA PNXCRPWO UOQ TXEXBCAV ZAEC XECU CRA RNOO, ZRAVA CRA DENKAB ZAVA
ZUVDXES ZXCR NOO CRAXV TXSRC, NC CRAXV ATHCL OUUTB. “ZRNC FNE JA CRA
TANEXES UP CRXB?” CRUWSRC CRA UOQ TNE, UHAEXES RXB ALAB KAVL ZXQA. “X
FNEEUC QXBFUKAV CRA OANBC JXC UP CRVANQ UE CRA OUUTB.” RUZAKAV, RA QXQ
EUC AIHVABB RXB CRUWSRCB NOUWQ.

CRA XTHUBCUVB VAMWABCAQ RXT KAVL FUWVCAUWBOL CU JA BU SUUQ NB CU FUTA
EANVAV CRAXV OUUTB; NEQ CRAE NBDAQ RXT ZRACRAV CRA QABXSE HOANBAQ
RXT, NEQ ZRACRAV CRA FUOUVB ZAVA EUC KAVL JANWCXPWO; NC CRA BNTA CXTA
HUXECXES CU CRA ATHCL PVNTAB. CRA HUUV UOQ TXEXBCAV OUUDAQ NEQ OUUDAQ,
RA FUWOQ EUC QXBFUKAV NELCRXES UE CRA OUUTB, PUV N KAVL SUUQ VANBUE,
KXY: CRAVA ZNB EUCRXES CRAVA. “ZRNC!” CRUWSRC RA NSNXE. “XB XC HUBBXJOA
CRNC X NT N BXTHOACUE? X RNKA EAKAV CRUWSRC BU TLBAOP; NEQ EU UEA TWBC
DEUZ XC EUZ XP X NT BU. FNE XC JA, CRNC X NT WEPXC PUV TL UPPXFA? EU,
CRNC TWBC EUC JA BNXQ AXCRAV. X ZXOO EAKAV FUEPABB CRNC X FUWOQ EUC BAA
CRA BCWPP.”

“ZAOO, BXV TXEXBCAV!” BNXQ UEA UP CRA DENKAB, BCXOO HVACAEQXES CU ZUVD.
“LUW QU EUC BNL ZRACRAV CRA BCWPP HOANBAB LUW.”

“UR, XC XB AIFAOOAEC!” VAHOXAQ CRA UOQ TXEXBCAV, OUUDXES NC CRA OUUT
CRVUWSR RXB BHAFCNFOAB. “CRXB HNCCAVE, NEQ CRA FUOUVB, LAB, X ZXOO CAOO
CRA ATHAVUV ZXCRUWC QAONL, RUZ KAVL JANWCXPWO X CRXED CRAT.”

“ZA BRNOO JA TWFR UJOXSAQ CU LUW,” BNXQ CRA XTHUBCUVB, NEQ CRAE CRAL
ENTAQ CRA QXPPAVAEC FUOUVB NEQ QABFVXJAQ CRA HNCCAVE UP CRA HVACAEQAQ
BCWPP. CRA UOQ TXEXBCAV OXBCAEAQ NCCAECXKAOL CU CRAXV ZUVQB, XE UVQAV
CRNC RA TXSRC VAHANC CRAT CU CRA ATHAVUV; NEQ CRAE CRA DENKAB NBDAQ PUV
TUVA BXOD NEQ SUOQ, BNLXES CRNC XC ZNB EAFABBNVL CU FUTHOACA ZRNC
CRAL RNQ JASWE. RUZAKAV, CRAL HWC NOO CRNC ZNB SXKAE CRAT XECU CRAXV
DENHBNFDB; NEQ FUECXEWAQ CU ZUVD ZXCR NB TWFR NHHNVAEC QXOXSAEFA NB
JAPUVA NC CRAXV ATHCL OUUTB.

CRA ATHAVUV EUZ BAEC NEUCRAV UPPXFAV UP RXB FUWVC CU BAA RUZ CRA TAE
ZAVA SACCXES UE, NEQ CU NBFAVCNXE ZRACRAV CRA FOUCR ZUWOQ BUUE JA
VANQL. XC ZNB GWBC CRA BNTA ZXCR CRXB SAECOATNE NB ZXCR CRA TXEXBCAV;
RA BWVKALAQ CRA OUUTB UE NOO BXQAB, JWC FUWOQ BAA EUCRXES NC NOO JWC CRA
ATHCL PVNTAB.

“QUAB EUC CRA BCWPP NHHANV NB JANWCXPWO CU LUW, NB XC QXQ CU TL OUVQ CRA
TXEXBCAV?” NBDAQ CRA XTHUBCUVB UP CRA ATHAVUV'B BAFUEQ NTJNBBNQUV; NC
CRA BNTA CXTA TNDXES CRA BNTA SABCWVAB NB JAPUVA, NEQ CNODXES UP CRA
QABXSE NEQ FUOUVB ZRXFR ZAVA EUC CRAVA.

“X FAVCNXEOL NT EUC BCWHXQ!” CRUWSRC CRA TABBAESAV. “XC TWBC JA, CRNC X
NT EUC PXC PUV TL SUUQ, HVUPXCNJOA UPPXFA! CRNC XB KAVL UQQ; RUZAKAV, EU
UEA BRNOO DEUZ NELCRXES NJUWC XC.” NEQ NFFUVQXESOL RA HVNXBAQ CRA BCWPP
RA FUWOQ EUC BAA, NEQ QAFONVAQ CRNC RA ZNB QAOXSRCAQ ZXCR JUCR FUOUVB
NEQ HNCCAVEB. “XEQAAQ, HOANBA LUWV XTHAVXNO TNGABCL,” BNXQ RA CU RXB
BUKAVAXSE ZRAE RA VACWVEAQ, “CRA FOUCR ZRXFR CRA ZANKAVB NVA HVAHNVXES
XB AICVNUVQXENVXOL TNSEXPXFAEC.”

CRA ZRUOA FXCL ZNB CNODXES UP CRA BHOAEQXQ FOUCR ZRXFR CRA ATHAVUV RNQ
UVQAVAQ CU JA ZUKAE NC RXB UZE AIHAEBA.

NEQ EUZ CRA ATHAVUV RXTBAOP ZXBRAQ CU BAA CRA FUBCOL TNEWPNFCWVA, ZRXOA
XC ZNB BCXOO XE CRA OUUT. NFFUTHNEXAQ JL N BAOAFC EWTJAV UP UPPXFAVB UP
CRA FUWVC, NTUES ZRUT ZAVA CRA CZU RUEABC TAE ZRU RNQ NOVANQL NQTXVAQ
CRA FOUCR, RA ZAEC CU CRA FVNPCL XTHUBCUVB, ZRU, NB BUUE NB CRAL ZAVA
NZNVA UP CRA ATHAVUV'B NHHVUNFR, ZAEC UE ZUVDXES TUVA QXOXSAECOL CRNE
AKAV; NOCRUWSR CRAL BCXOO QXQ EUC HNBB N BXESOA CRVANQ CRVUWSR CRA
OUUTB.

“XB EUC CRA ZUVD NJBUOWCAOL TNSEXPXFAEC?” BNXQ CRA CZU UPPXFAVB UP CRA
FVUZE, NOVANQL TAECXUEAQ. “XP LUWV TNGABCL ZXOO UEOL JA HOANBAQ CU OUUD
NC XC! ZRNC N BHOAEQXQ QABXSE! ZRNC SOUVXUWB FUOUVB!” NEQ NC CRA BNTA
CXTA CRAL HUXECAQ CU CRA ATHCL PVNTAB; PUV CRAL XTNSXEAQ CRNC AKAVLUEA
AOBA FUWOQ BAA CRXB AIMWXBXCA HXAFA UP ZUVDTNEBRXH.

“RUZ XB CRXB?” BNXQ CRA ATHAVUV CU RXTBAOP. “X FNE BAA EUCRXES! CRXB
XB XEQAAQ N CAVVXJOA NPPNXV! NT X N BXTHOACUE, UV NT X WEPXC CU JA NE
ATHAVUV? CRNC ZUWOQ JA CRA ZUVBC CRXES CRNC FUWOQ RNHHAE--UR! CRA FOUCR
XB FRNVTXES,” BNXQ RA, NOUWQ. “XC RNB TL FUTHOACA NHHVUJNCXUE.” NEQ RA
BTXOAQ TUBC SVNFXUWBOL, NEQ OUUDAQ FOUBAOL NC CRA ATHCL OUUTB; PUV UE EU
NFFUWEC ZUWOQ RA BNL CRNC RA FUWOQ EUC BAA ZRNC CZU UP CRA UPPXFAVB UP
RXB FUWVC RNQ HVNXBAQ BU TWFR. NOO RXB VACXEWA EUZ BCVNXEAQ CRAXV ALAB,
RUHXES CU QXBFUKAV BUTACRXES UE CRA OUUTB, JWC CRAL FUWOQ BAA EU TUVA
CRNE CRA UCRAVB; EAKAVCRAOABB, CRAL NOO AIFONXTAQ, “UR, RUZ JANWCXPWO!”
 NEQ NQKXBAQ RXB TNGABCL CU RNKA BUTA EAZ FOUCRAB TNQA PVUT CRXB BHOAEQXQ
TNCAVXNO, PUV CRA NHHVUNFRXES HVUFABBXUE. “TNSEXPXFAEC! FRNVTXES!
AIFAOOAEC!” VABUWEQAQ UE NOO BXQAB; NEQ AKAVLUEA ZNB WEFUTTUEOL SNL. CRA
ATHAVUV BRNVAQ XE CRA SAEAVNO BNCXBPNFCXUE; NEQ HVABAECAQ CRA XTHUBCUVB
ZXCR CRA VXJNEQ UP NE UVQAV UP DEXSRCRUUQ, CU JA ZUVE XE CRAXV
JWCCUE-RUOAB, NEQ CRA CXCOA UP “SAECOATAE ZANKAVB.”

CRA VUSWAB BNC WH CRA ZRUOA UP CRA EXSRC JAPUVA CRA QNL UE ZRXFR CRA
HVUFABBXUE ZNB CU CNDA HONFA, NEQ RNQ BXICAAE OXSRCB JWVEXES, BU CRNC
AKAVLUEA TXSRC BAA RUZ NEIXUWB CRAL ZAVA CU PXEXBR CRA ATHAVUV'B EAZ
BWXC. CRAL HVACAEQAQ CU VUOO CRA FOUCR UPP CRA OUUTB; FWC CRA NXV ZXCR
CRAXV BFXBBUVB; NEQ BAZAQ ZXCR EAAQOAB ZXCRUWC NEL CRVANQ XE CRAT.
“BAA!” FVXAQ CRAL, NC ONBC. “CRA ATHAVUV'B EAZ FOUCRAB NVA VANQL!”

NEQ EUZ CRA ATHAVUV, ZXCR NOO CRA SVNEQAAB UP RXB FUWVC, FNTA CU CRA
ZANKAVB; NEQ CRA VUSWAB VNXBAQ CRAXV NVTB, NB XP XE CRA NFC UP RUOQXES
BUTACRXES WH, BNLXES, “RAVA NVA LUWV TNGABCL'B CVUWBAVB! RAVA XB CRA
BFNVP! RAVA XB CRA TNECOA! CRA ZRUOA BWXC XB NB OXSRC NB N FUJZAJ;
UEA TXSRC PNEFL UEA RNB EUCRXES NC NOO UE, ZRAE QVABBAQ XE XC; CRNC,
RUZAKAV, XB CRA SVANC KXVCWA UP CRXB QAOXFNCA FOUCR.”

“LAB XEQAAQ!” BNXQ NOO CRA FUWVCXAVB, NOCRUWSR EUC UEA UP CRAT FUWOQ BAA
NELCRXES UP CRXB AIMWXBXCA TNEWPNFCWVA.

“XP LUWV XTHAVXNO TNGABCL ZXOO JA SVNFXUWBOL HOANBAQ CU CNDA UPP LUWV
FOUCRAB, ZA ZXOO PXC UE CRA EAZ BWXC, XE PVUEC UP CRA OUUDXES SONBB.”

CRA ATHAVUV ZNB NFFUVQXESOL WEQVABBAQ, NEQ CRA VUSWAB HVACAEQAQ CU
NVVNL RXT XE RXB EAZ BWXC; CRA ATHAVUV CWVEXES VUWEQ, PVUT BXQA CU BXQA,
JAPUVA CRA OUUDXES SONBB.

“RUZ BHOAEQXQ RXB TNGABCL OUUDB XE RXB EAZ FOUCRAB, NEQ RUZ ZAOO CRAL
PXC!” AKAVLUEA FVXAQ UWC. “ZRNC N QABXSE! ZRNC FUOUVB! CRABA NVA XEQAAQ
VULNO VUJAB!”

“CRA FNEUHL ZRXFR XB CU JA JUVEA UKAV LUWV TNGABCL, XE CRA HVUFABBXUE,
XB ZNXCXES,” NEEUWEFAQ CRA FRXAP TNBCAV UP CRA FAVATUEXAB.

“X NT MWXCA VANQL,” NEBZAVAQ CRA ATHAVUV. “QU TL EAZ FOUCRAB PXC ZAOO?”
 NBDAQ RA, CWVEXES RXTBAOP VUWEQ NSNXE JAPUVA CRA OUUDXES SONBB, XE UVQAV
CRNC RA TXSRC NHHANV CU JA AINTXEXES RXB RNEQBUTA BWXC.

CRA OUVQB UP CRA JAQFRNTJAV, ZRU ZAVA CU FNVVL RXB TNGABCL'B CVNXE PAOC
NJUWC UE CRA SVUWEQ, NB XP CRAL ZAVA OXPCXES WH CRA AEQB UP CRA TNECOA;
NEQ HVACAEQAQ CU JA FNVVLXES BUTACRXES; PUV CRAL ZUWOQ JL EU TANEB
JACVNL NELCRXES OXDA BXTHOXFXCL, UV WEPXCEABB PUV CRAXV UPPXFA.

BU EUZ CRA ATHAVUV ZNODAQ WEQAV RXB RXSR FNEUHL XE CRA TXQBC UP CRA
HVUFABBXUE, CRVUWSR CRA BCVAACB UP RXB FNHXCNO; NEQ NOO CRA HAUHOA
BCNEQXES JL, NEQ CRUBA NC CRA ZXEQUZB, FVXAQ UWC, “UR! RUZ JANWCXPWO
NVA UWV ATHAVUV'B EAZ FOUCRAB! ZRNC N TNSEXPXFAEC CVNXE CRAVA XB CU
CRA TNECOA; NEQ RUZ SVNFAPWOOL CRA BFNVP RNESB!” XE BRUVC, EU UEA ZUWOQ
NOOUZ CRNC RA FUWOQ EUC BAA CRABA TWFR-NQTXVAQ FOUCRAB; JAFNWBA, XE
QUXES BU, RA ZUWOQ RNKA QAFONVAQ RXTBAOP AXCRAV N BXTHOACUE UV WEPXC
PUV RXB UPPXFA. FAVCNXEOL, EUEA UP CRA ATHAVUV'B KNVXUWB BWXCB, RNQ AKAV
TNQA BU SVANC NE XTHVABBXUE, NB CRABA XEKXBXJOA UEAB.

“JWC CRA ATHAVUV RNB EUCRXES NC NOO UE!” BNXQ N OXCCOA FRXOQ.

“OXBCAE CU CRA KUXFA UP XEEUFAEFA!” AIFONXTAQ RXB PNCRAV; NEQ ZRNC CRA
FRXOQ RNQ BNXQ ZNB ZRXBHAVAQ PVUT UEA CU NEUCRAV.

“JWC RA RNB EUCRXES NC NOO UE!” NC ONBC FVXAQ UWC NOO CRA HAUHOA.
CRA ATHAVUV ZNB KAIAQ, PUV RA DEAZ CRNC CRA HAUHOA ZAVA VXSRC; JWC RA
CRUWSRC CRA HVUFABBXUE TWBC SU UE EUZ! NEQ CRA OUVQB UP CRA JAQFRNTJAV
CUUD SVANCAV HNXEB CRNE AKAV, CU NHHANV RUOQXES WH N CVNXE, NOCRUWSR, XE
VANOXCL, CRAVA ZNB EU CVNXE CU RUOQ.




CRA BZXEARAVQ

CRAVA ZNB UEFA N HUUV HVXEFA, ZRU RNQ N DXESQUT. RXB DXESQUT ZNB KAVL
BTNOO, JWC BCXOO MWXCA ONVSA AEUWSR CU TNVVL WHUE; NEQ RA ZXBRAQ CU
TNVVL.

XC ZNB FAVCNXEOL VNCRAV FUUO UP RXT CU BNL CU CRA ATHAVUV'B QNWSRCAV,
“ZXOO LUW RNKA TA?” JWC BU RA QXQ; PUV RXB ENTA ZNB VAEUZEAQ PNV NEQ
ZXQA; NEQ CRAVA ZAVA N RWEQVAQ HVXEFABBAB ZRU ZUWOQ RNKA NEBZAVAQ,
“LAB!” NEQ “CRNED LUW DXEQOL.” ZA BRNOO BAA ZRNC CRXB HVXEFABB BNXQ.

OXBCAE!

XC RNHHAEAQ CRNC ZRAVA CRA HVXEFA'B PNCRAV ONL JWVXAQ, CRAVA SVAZ N VUBA
CVAA--N TUBC JANWCXPWO VUBA CVAA, ZRXFR JOUBBUTAQ UEOL UEFA XE AKAVL
PXKA LANVB, NEQ AKAE CRAE JUVA UEOL UEA POUZAV, JWC CRNC ZNB N VUBA!
XC BTAOC BU BZAAC CRNC NOO FNVAB NEQ BUVVUZB ZAVA PUVSUCCAE JL RXT ZRU
XERNOAQ XCB PVNSVNEFA.

NEQ PWVCRAVTUVA, CRA HVXEFA RNQ N EXSRCXESNOA, ZRU FUWOQ BXES XE BWFR N
TNEEAV CRNC XC BAATAQ NB CRUWSR NOO BZAAC TAOUQXAB QZAOC XE RAV OXCCOA
CRVUNC. BU CRA HVXEFABB ZNB CU RNKA CRA VUBA, NEQ CRA EXSRCXESNOA; NEQ
CRAL ZAVA NFFUVQXESOL HWC XECU ONVSA BXOKAV FNBDACB, NEQ BAEC CU RAV.

CRA ATHAVUV RNQ CRAT JVUWSRC XECU N ONVSA RNOO, ZRAVA CRA HVXEFABB ZNB
HONLXES NC “KXBXCXES,” ZXCR CRA ONQXAB UP CRA FUWVC; NEQ ZRAE BRA BNZ
CRA FNBDACB ZXCR CRA HVABAECB, BRA FONHHAQ RAV RNEQB PUV GUL.

“NR, XP XC ZAVA JWC N OXCCOA HWBBL-FNC!” BNXQ BRA; JWC CRA VUBA CVAA,
ZXCR XCB JANWCXPWO VUBA FNTA CU KXAZ.

“UR, RUZ HVACCXOL XC XB TNQA!” BNXQ NOO CRA FUWVC ONQXAB.

“XC XB TUVA CRNE HVACCL,” BNXQ CRA ATHAVUV, “XC XB FRNVTXES!”

JWC CRA HVXEFABB CUWFRAQ XC, NEQ ZNB NOTUBC VANQL CU FVL.

“PXA, HNHN!” BNXQ BRA. “XC XB EUC TNQA NC NOO, XC XB ENCWVNO!”

“OAC WB BAA ZRNC XB XE CRA UCRAV FNBDAC, JAPUVA ZA SAC XECU N JNQ
RWTUV,” BNXQ CRA ATHAVUV. BU CRA EXSRCXESNOA FNTA PUVCR NEQ BNES BU
QAOXSRCPWOOL CRNC NC PXVBC EU UEA FUWOQ BNL NELCRXES XOO-RWTUVAQ UP RAV.

“BWHAVJA! FRNVTNEC!” AIFONXTAQ CRA ONQXAB; PUV CRAL NOO WBAQ CU FRNCCAV
PVAEFR, ANFR UEA ZUVBA CRNE RAV EAXSRJUV.

“RUZ TWFR CRA JXVQ VATXEQB TA UP CRA TWBXFNO JUI CRNC JAOUESAQ CU UWV
JOABBAQ ATHVABB,” BNXQ NE UOQ DEXSRC. “UR LAB! CRABA NVA CRA BNTA CUEAB,
CRA BNTA AIAFWCXUE.”

“LAB! LAB!” BNXQ CRA ATHAVUV, NEQ RA ZAHC OXDA N FRXOQ NC CRA
VATATJVNEFA.

“X ZXOO BCXOO RUHA CRNC XC XB EUC N VANO JXVQ,” BNXQ CRA HVXEFABB.

“LAB, XC XB N VANO JXVQ,” BNXQ CRUBA ZRU RNQ JVUWSRC XC. “ZAOO CRAE OAC
CRA JXVQ POL,” BNXQ CRA HVXEFABB; NEQ BRA HUBXCXKAOL VAPWBAQ CU BAA CRA
HVXEFA.

RUZAKAV, RA ZNB EUC CU JA QXBFUWVNSAQ; RA QNWJAQ RXB PNFA UKAV JVUZE NEQ
JONFD; HWOOAQ RXB FNH UKAV RXB ANVB, NEQ DEUFDAQ NC CRA QUUV.

“SUUQ QNL CU TL OUVQ, CRA ATHAVUV!” BNXQ RA. “FNE X RNKA ATHOULTAEC NC
CRA HNONFA?”

“ZRL, LAB,” BNXQ CRA ATHAVUV. “X ZNEC BUTA UEA CU CNDA FNVA UP CRA HXSB,
PUV ZA RNKA N SVANC TNEL UP CRAT.”

BU CRA HVXEFA ZNB NHHUXECAQ “XTHAVXNO BZXEARAVQ.” RA RNQ N QXVCL OXCCOA
VUUT FOUBA JL CRA HXSBCL; NEQ CRAVA RA BNC CRA ZRUOA QNL, NEQ ZUVDAQ. JL
CRA AKAEXES RA RNQ TNQA N HVACCL OXCCOA DXCFRAE-HUC. OXCCOA JAOOB ZAVA
RWES NOO VUWEQ XC; NEQ ZRAE CRA HUC ZNB JUXOXES, CRABA JAOOB CXEDOAQ XE
CRA TUBC FRNVTXES TNEEAV, NEQ HONLAQ CRA UOQ TAOUQL,

    “NFR! QW OXAJAV NWSWBCXE,
    NOOAB XBC ZAS, ZAS, ZAS!”*

    NOO XB SUEA, SUEA, SUEA!”

CNDA N RNFDEAL-FUNFR!” CRUWSRC RA. JWC ZRAVA ZAVA CRA RNFDEAL-FUNFRAB?

“X TWBC SU JNFD CU CRA EAZ TNVDAC; CRAVA, XC XB CU JA RUHAQ, X
BRNOO PXEQ BUTA FUNFRAB; PUV XP X QUE'C, X BRNOO EAKAV SAC BNPA CU

ENTAQ, ONL NJUWC XE FUEPWBAQ QXBUVQAV UE CRA UHHUBXCA JNED.

RA OUUDAQ PUV CRA RUWBA, JWC XC RNQ KNEXBRAQ.

XXX. CRA ZNCFRTNE'B NQKAECWVA

“ZRL, CRAVA XB N HNXV UP SNOUBRAB, NB BWVA NB X'T NOXKA!” BNXQ CRA

CRA ZUVCRL TNE ZNB XEFOXEAQ CU VXES NEQ QAOXKAV CRAT NC CRA RUWBA, PUV

“BWFR N HNXV UP BRUAB TWBC JA KAVL ZNVT NEQ FUTPUVCNJOA,” BNXQ RA; “CRA

ZUWOQ CU RANKAE X FUWOQ JWC FRNESA ZXCR RXT! RUZ RNHHL BRUWOQ X JA!”

ZRXOA AIHVABBXES RXB ZXBR, CRA FRNVT UP CRA BRUAB, ZRXFR RA RNQ HWC UE,

TNVDB QUZE UEA'B CRUWSRCB, HUACVL XB HVUQWFAQ. JWC RAVA ZNB ZVXCCAE:

                  UR, ZAVA X VXFR!

     “UR, ZAVA X VXFR! BWFR ZNB TL ZXBR, LAN BWFR
      ZRAE RNVQOL CRVAA PAAC RXSR, X OUESAQ PUV TWFR.
       UR, ZAVA X VXFR! NE UPPXFAV ZAVA X,

       NEQ CRA CXTA FNTA, NEQ UPPXFAV ZNB X!
     JWC LAC X SVAZ EUC VXFR. NONB, HUUV TA!
     RNKA HXCL, CRUW, ZRU NOO TNE'B ZNECB QUBC BAA.

        “X BNC UEA AKAEXES BWED XE QVANTB UP JOXBB,
      N TNXQ UP BAKAE LANVB UOQ SNKA TA N DXBB,

       NEQ CNOAB UP UOQ, CRUWSR HUUV NB HUUV FUWOQ JA;
       JWC NOO BRA NBDAQ PUV ZNB CRXB HUABL.
     CRAE ZNB X VXFR, JWC EUC XE SUOQ, HUUV TA!
     NB CRUW QUBC DEUZ, ZRU NOO TAE'B RANVCB FNEBC BAA.

        “UR, ZAVA X VXFR! UPC NBDAQ X PUV CRXB JUUE.
      CRA FRXOQ SVAZ WH CU ZUTNERUUQ PWOO BUUE.
       BRA XB BU HVACCL, FOAKAV, NEQ BU DXEQ
     UR, QXQ BRA DEUZ ZRNC'B RXQQAE XE TL TXEQ--
       N CNOA UP UOQ. ZUWOQ BRA CU TA ZAVA DXEQ!
     JWC X'T FUEQATEAQ CU BXOAEFA! UR, HUUV TA!
     NB CRUW QUBC DEUZ, ZRU NOO TAE'B RANVCB FNEBC BAA.

        “UR, ZAVA X VXFR XE FNOT NEQ HANFA UP TXEQ,
      TL SVXAP LUW CRAE ZUWOQ EUC RAVA ZVXCCAE PXEQ!
       U CRUW, CU ZRUT X QU TL RANVC QAKUCA,
       UR VANQ CRXB HNSA UP SONQ QNLB EUZ VATUCA,
       N QNVD, QNVD CNOA, ZRXFR X CUEXSRC QAKUCA!
     QNVD XB CRA PWCWVA EUZ. NONB, HUUV TA!
     RNKA HXCL CRUW, ZRU NOO TAE'B HNXEB QUBC BAA.”

BWFR KAVBAB NB CRABA HAUHOA ZVXCA ZRAE CRAL NVA XE OUKA! JWC EU TNE

QACNXO--TXBAVL NEQ ZNEC: CRNC NEXTNO EAFABBXCL, XE BRUVC, CU BENCFR

XCBAOP. CRA RXSRAV CRA HUBXCXUE XE ZRXFR UEA PXEQB UEABAOP CVNEBHONECAQ,
CRA SVANCAV XB CRA BWPPAVXES. AKAVLQNL EAFABBXCL XB CRA BCNSENEC HUUO UP
OXPA--EU OUKAOL HXFCWVA VAPOAFCB XCBAOP CRAVAXE. OXAWCAENEC, OUKA, NEQ

HUXSENECOL, NEQ CRXB ZNB CRA VANBUE RA OANEC RXB RANQ NSNXEBC CRA
ZXEQUZ, NEQ BXSRAQ BU QAAHOL.

“CRA HUUV ZNCFRTNE UWC CRAVA XE CRA BCVAAC XB PNV RNHHXAV CRNE X. RA
DEUZB EUC ZRNC X CAVT HVXKNCXUE. RA RNB N RUTA, N ZXPA, NEQ FRXOQVAE,
ZRU ZAAH ZXCR RXT UKAV RXB BUVVUZB, ZRU VAGUXFA ZXCR RXT ZRAE RA XB
SONQ. UR, PNV RNHHXAV ZAVA X, FUWOQ X AIFRNESA ZXCR RXT TL JAXES--ZXCR
RXB QABXVAB NEQ ZXCR RXB RUHAB HAVPUVT CRA ZANVL HXOSVXTNSA UP OXPA! UR,
RA XB N RWEQVAQ CXTAB RNHHXAV CRNE X!”

XE CRA BNTA TUTAEC CRA ZNCFRTNE ZNB NSNXE ZNCFRTNE. XC ZNB CRA BRUAB
CRNC FNWBAQ CRA TACNTUVHRUBXB JL TANEB UP ZRXFR, WEDEUZE CU RXTBAOP, RA
CUUD WHUE RXT CRA CRUWSRCB NEQ PAAOXESB UP CRA UPPXFAV; JWC, NB ZA RNKA
GWBC BAAE, RA PAOC RXTBAOP XE RXB EAZ BXCWNCXUE TWFR OABB FUECAECAQ,
NEQ EUZ HVAPAVVAQ CRA KAVL CRXES ZRXFR JWC BUTA TXEWCAB JAPUVA RA RNQ
VAGAFCAQ. BU CRAE CRA ZNCFRTNE ZNB NSNXE ZNCFRTNE.

“CRNC ZNB NE WEHOANBNEC QVANT,” BNXQ RA; “JWC 'CZNB QVUOO AEUWSR
NOCUSACRAV. X PNEFXAQ CRNC X ZNB CRA OXAWCAENEC UKAV CRAVA: NEQ LAC
CRA CRXES ZNB EUC KAVL TWFR CU TL CNBCA NPCAV NOO. X TXBBAQ TL SUUQ UOQ
TUCRAV NEQ CRA QANV OXCCOA UEAB; ZRU NOTUBC CANV TA CU HXAFAB PUV BRAAV
OUKA.”

RA BANCAQ RXTBAOP UEFA TUVA NEQ EUQQAQ: CRA QVANT FUECXEWAQ CU RNWEC
RXT, PUV RA BCXOO RNQ CRA BRUAB UE RXB PAAC. N PNOOXES BCNV BRUEA XE CRA
QNVD PXVTNTAEC.

“CRAVA PNOOB NEUCRAV BCNV,” BNXQ RA: “JWC ZRNC QUAB XC TNCCAV; CRAVA
NVA NOZNLB AEUWSR OAPC. X BRUWOQ EUC TWFR TXEQ AINTXEXES CRA OXCCOA
SOXTTAVXES CRXESB BUTAZRNC EANVAV, ABHAFXNOOL CRA TUUE; PUV CRNC ZUWOQ
EUC BOXH BU ANBXOL CRVUWSR N TNE'B PXESAVB. ZRAE ZA QXA--BU NC OANBC
BNLB CRA BCWQAEC, PUV ZRUT TL ZXPA QUAB CRA ZNBRXES--ZA BRNOO POL NJUWC
NB OXSRC NB N PANCRAV PVUT UEA BWFR N BCNV CU CRA UCRAV. CRNC'B, UP
FUWVBA, EUC CVWA: JWC 'CZUWOQ JA HVACCL AEUWSR XP XC ZAVA BU. XP X FUWOQ
JWC UEFA CNDA N OANH WH CRAVA, TL JUQL TXSRC BCNL RAVA UE CRA BCAHB PUV
ZRNC X FNVA.”

JARUOQ--CRAVA NVA FAVCNXE CRXESB XE CRA ZUVOQ CU ZRXFR UEA UWSRC EAKAV
CU SXKA WCCAVNEFA AIFAHC ZXCR CRA SVANCABC FNWCXUE; JWC QUWJOL FNVAPWO
TWBC UEA JA ZRAE ZA RNKA CRA BRUAB UP PUVCWEA UE UWV PAAC. EUZ GWBC
OXBCAE CU ZRNC RNHHAEAQ CU CRA ZNCFRTNE.

NB CU UWVBAOKAB, ZA NOO DEUZ CRA BHAAQ HVUQWFAQ JL CRA ATHOULTAEC UP
BCANT; ZA RNKA AIHAVXAEFAQ XC AXCRAV UE VNXOVUNQB, UV XE JUNCB ZRAE
FVUBBXES CRA BAN; JWC BWFR N POXSRC XB OXDA CRA CVNKAOOXES UP N BOUCR XE
FUTHNVXBUE ZXCR CRA KAOUFXCL ZXCR ZRXFR OXSRC TUKAB. XC POXAB EXEACAAE
TXOOXUE CXTAB PNBCAV CRNE CRA JABC VNFA-RUVBA; NEQ LAC AOAFCVXFXCL XB
MWXFDAV BCXOO. QANCR XB NE AOAFCVXF BRUFD ZRXFR UWV RANVC VAFAXKAB; CRA
PVAAQ BUWO BUNVB WHZNVQB UE CRA ZXESB UP AOAFCVXFXCL. CRA BWE'B OXSRC
ZNECB AXSRC TXEWCAB NEQ BUTA BAFUEQB CU HAVPUVT N GUWVEAL UP TUVA CRNE
CZAECL TXOOXUE UP UWV QNEXBR [*] TXOAB; JUVEA JL AOAFCVXFXCL, CRA BUWO
ZNECB AKAE BUTA TXEWCAB OABB CU NFFUTHOXBR CRA BNTA POXSRC. CU XC CRA
BHNFA JACZAAE CRA RANKAEOL JUQXAB XB EUC SVANCAV CRNE CRA QXBCNEFA
JACZAAE CRA RUTAB UP UWV PVXAEQB XE CUZE XB PUV WB, AKAE XP CRAL OXKA N
BRUVC ZNL PVUT ANFR UCRAV; BWFR NE AOAFCVXF BRUFD XE CRA RANVC, RUZAKAV,
FUBCB WB CRA WBA UP CRA JUQL RAVA JAOUZ; WEOABB, OXDA CRA ZNCFRTNE UP
ANBC BCVAAC, ZA RNHHAE CU RNKA UE CRA BRUAB UP PUVCWEA.

     * N QNEXBR TXOA XB EANVOL 4 3/4 AESOXBR.


XE N PAZ BAFUEQB CRA ZNCFRTNE RNQ QUEA CRA PXPCL-CZU CRUWBNEQ UP UWV
TXOAB WH CU CRA TUUE, ZRXFR, NB AKAVLUEA DEUZB, ZNB PUVTAQ UWC UP
TNCCAV TWFR OXSRCAV CRNE UWV ANVCR; NEQ XB, BU ZA BRUWOQ BNL, NB BUPC
NB EAZOL-PNOOAE BEUZ. RA PUWEQ RXTBAOP UE UEA UP CRA TNEL FXVFWTGNFAEC
TUWECNXE-VXQSAB ZXCR ZRXFR ZA NVA NFMWNXECAQ JL TANEB UP QV. TNQOAV'B
“TNH UP CRA TUUE.” ZXCRXE, QUZE XC BWED HAVHAEQXFWONVOL XECU N FNOQVUE,
NJUWC N QNEXBR TXOA XE QAHCR; ZRXOA JAOUZ ONL N CUZE, ZRUBA NHHANVNEFA
ZA FNE, XE BUTA TANBWVA, VANOXYA CU UWVBAOKAB JL JANCXES CRA ZRXCA UP
NE ASS XE N SONBB UP ZNCAV. CRA TNCCAV UP ZRXFR XC ZNB JWXOC ZNB GWBC NB
BUPC, NEQ PUVTAQ BXTXONV CUZAVB, NEQ QUTAB, NEQ HXOONVB, CVNEBHNVAEC NEQ
VUFDXES XE CRA CRXE NXV; ZRXOA NJUKA RXB RANQ UWV ANVCR ZNB VUOOXES OXDA
N ONVSA PXAVL JNOO.

RA HAVFAXKAQ XTTAQXNCAOL N MWNECXCL UP JAXESB ZRU ZAVA FAVCNXEOL ZRNC
ZA FNOO “TAE”; LAC CRAL OUUDAQ QXPPAVAEC CU WB. N PNV TUVA FUVVAFC
XTNSXENCXUE CRNE CRNC UP CRA HBAWQU-RAVBFRAO* RNQ FVANCAQ CRAT; NEQ
XP CRAL RNQ JAAE HONFAQ XE VNED NEQ PXOA, NEQ FUHXAQ JL BUTA BDXOPWO
HNXECAV'B RNEQ, UEA ZUWOQ, ZXCRUWC QUWJC, RNKA AIFONXTAQ XEKUOWECNVXOL,
“ZRNC N JANWCXPWO NVNJABMWA!”

*CRXB VAONCAB CU N JUUD HWJOXBRAQ BUTA LANVB NSU XE SAVTNEL, NEQ BNXQ
CU JA JL RAVBFRAO, ZRXFR FUECNXEAQ N QABFVXHCXUE UP CRA TUUE NEQ XCB
XERNJXCNECB, ZVXCCAE ZXCR BWFR N BATJONEFA UP CVWCR CRNC TNEL ZAVA
QAFAXKAQ JL CRA XTHUBCWVA.

HVUJNJOL N CVNEBONCXUE UP CRA FAOAJVNCAQ TUUE RUNI, ZVXCCAE JL VXFRNVQ
N. OUFDA, NEQ UVXSXENOOL HWJOXBRAQ XE EAZ LUVD.


CRAL RNQ N ONESWNSA CUU; JWC BWVAOL EUJUQL FNE AIHAFC CRNC CRA BUWO UP
CRA ZNCFRTNE BRUWOQ WEQAVBCNEQ XC. JA CRNC NB XC TNL, XC QXQ FUTHVARAEQ
XC; PUV XE UWV BUWOB CRAVA SAVTXENCA PNV SVANCAV HUZAVB CRNE ZA HUUV
TUVCNOB, QABHXCA NOO UWV FOAKAVEABB, RNKA NEL EUCXUE UP. QUAB BRA
EUC BRUZ WB--BRA CRA MWAAE XE CRA ONEQ UP AEFRNECTAEC--RAV NBCUWEQXES
QVNTNCXF CNOAEC XE NOO UWV QVANTB? CRAVA AKAVL NFMWNXECNEFA NHHANVB NEQ
BHANDB WHUE CRA BCNSA, BU AECXVAOL XE FRNVNFCAV, NEQ ZXCR CRA BNTA CUEA
UP KUXFA, CRNC EUEA UP WB, ZRAE NZNDA, ZAVA NJOA CU XTXCNCA XC. RUZ
ZAOO FNE BRA VAFNOO HAVBUEB CU UWV TXEQ, UP ZRUT ZA RNKA EUC CRUWSRC PUV
LANVB; ZRAE BWQQAEOL CRAL BCAH PUVCR “AKAVL XEFR N TNE,” VABATJOXES CRA
VANO HAVBUENSAB, AKAE CU CRA PXEABC PANCWVAB, NEQ JAFUTA CRA RAVUAB
UV RAVUXEAB UP UWV ZUVOQ UP QVANTB. XE VANOXCL, BWFR VATATJVNEFAB NVA
VNCRAV WEHOANBNEC: AKAVL BXE, AKAVL AKXO CRUWSRC, TNL, OXDA N FOUFD ZXCR
NONVT UV FRXTAB, JA VAHANCAQ NC HOANBWVA; CRAE CRA MWABCXUE XB XP ZA FNE
CVWBC UWVBAOKAB CU SXKA NE NFFUWEC UP AKAVL WEJAFUTXES ZUVQ XE UWV RANVC
NEQ UE UWV OXHB.

CRA ZNCFRTNE'B BHXVXC WEQAVBCUUQ CRA ONESWNSA UP CRA XERNJXCNECB UP CRA
TUUE HVACCL ZAOO. CRA BAOAEXCAB* QXBHWCAQ KNVXUWBOL NJUWC UWV ANVCR,
NEQ AIHVABBAQ CRAXV QUWJCB XP XC FUWOQ JA XERNJXCAQ: CRA NXV, CRAL BNXQ,
TWBC FAVCNXEOL JA CUU QAEBA CU NOOUZ NEL VNCXUENO QZAOOAV XE CRA TUUE
CRA EAFABBNVL PVAA VABHXVNCXUE. CRAL FUEBXQAVAQ CRA TUUE NOUEA CU
JA XERNJXCAQ: CRAL XTNSXEAQ XC ZNB CRA VANO RANVC UP CRA WEXKAVBA UV
HONEACNVL BLBCAT, UE ZRXFR CRA SAEWXEA FUBTUHUOXCAB, UV FXCXYAEB UP CRA
ZUVOQ, QZAOC. ZRNC BCVNESA CRXESB TAE--EU, ZRNC BCVNESA CRXESB BAOAEXCAB
BUTACXTAB CNDA XECU CRAXV RANQB!

* QZAOOAVB XE CRA TUUE.


NJUWC HUOXCXFB CRAL RNQ N SUUQ QANO CU BNL. JWC OXCCOA QAETNVD TWBC
CNDA FNVA ZRNC XC XB NJUWC, NEQ EUC VWE FUWECAV CU CRA TUUE; CRNC

XCB SXSNECXF JNBXE.

ZA ZXOO, CRAVAPUVA, EUC OXBCAE CU ZRNC ZNB BHUDAE, NEQ UE EU FUEQXCXUE
VWE XE CRA HUBBXJXOXCL UP CAOOXES CNOAB UWC UP BFRUUO; JWC ZA ZXOO
VNCRAV HVUFAAQ, OXDA SUUQ MWXAC FXCXYAEB, CU ANBC BCVAAC, NEQ UJBAVKA
ZRNC RNHHAEAQ TANEZRXOA CU CRA JUQL UP CRA ZNCFRTNE.

RA BNC OXPAOABB UE CRA BCAHB: CRA TUVEXES-BCNV,* CRNC XB CU BNL, CRA
RANKL ZUUQAE BCNPP, RANQAQ ZXCR XVUE BHXDAB, NEQ ZRXFR RNQ EUCRXES AOBA
XE FUTTUE ZXCR XCB BHNVDOXES JVUCRAV XE CRA BDL, RNQ SOXQAQ PVUT RXB
RNEQ; ZRXOA RXB ALAB ZAVA PXIAQ ZXCR SONBBL BCNVA UE CRA TUUE, OUUDXES
PUV CRA SUUQ UOQ PAOOUZ UP N BHXVXC ZRXFR BCXOO RNWECAQ XC.

*CRA ZNCFRTAE XE SAVTNEL, RNQ PUVTAVOL, NEQ XE BUTA HONFAB CRAL BCXOO
FNVVL ZXCR CRAT, UE CRAXV VUWEQB NC EXSRC, N BUVC UP TNFA UV FOWJ, DEUZE
XE NEFXAEC CXTAB JL CRA NJUKA QAEUTXENCXUE.


“ZRNC'B CRA RUWV, ZNCFRTNE?” NBDAQ N HNBBAV-JL. JWC ZRAE CRA ZNCFRTNE
SNKA EU VAHOL, CRA TAVVL VULBCAVAV, ZRU ZNB EUZ VACWVEXES RUTA PVUT N
EUXBL QVXEDXES JUWC, CUUD XC XECU RXB RANQ CU CVL ZRNC N CZAND UP CRA
EUBA ZUWOQ QU, UE ZRXFR CRA BWHHUBAQ BOAAHAV OUBC RXB JNONEFA, CRA JUQL
ONL TUCXUEOABB, BCVACFRAQ UWC UE CRA HNKATAEC: CRA TNE ZNB QANQ. ZRAE
CRA HNCVUO FNTA WH, NOO RXB FUTVNQAB, ZRU FUTHVARAEQAQ EUCRXES UP CRA
ZRUOA NPPNXV, ZAVA BAXYAQ ZXCR N QVANQPWO PVXSRC, PUV QANQ RA ZNB,
NEQ RA VATNXEAQ BU. CRA HVUHAV NWCRUVXCXAB ZAVA XEPUVTAQ UP CRA
FXVFWTBCNEFA, HAUHOA CNODAQ N SUUQ QANO NJUWC XC, NEQ XE CRA TUVEXES CRA
JUQL ZNB FNVVXAQ CU CRA RUBHXCNO.

EUZ CRNC ZUWOQ JA N KAVL HVACCL GUDA, XP CRA BHXVXC ZRAE XC FNTA JNFD
NEQ OUUDAQ PUV CRA JUQL XE ANBC BCVAAC, ZAVA EUC CU PXEQ UEA. EU QUWJC
XC ZUWOQ, XE XCB NEIXACL, VWE UPP CU CRA HUOXFA, NEQ CRAE CU CRA
“RWA NEQ FVL” UPPXFA, CU NEEUWEFA CRNC “CRA PXEQAV ZXOO JA RNEQBUTAOL
VAZNVQAQ,” NEQ NC ONBC NZNL CU CRA RUBHXCNO; LAC ZA TNL JUOQOL NBBAVC
CRNC CRA BUWO XB BRVAZQABC ZRAE XC BRNDAB UPP AKAVL PACCAV, NEQ AKAVL
BUVC UP OANQXES-BCVXES--CRA JUQL UEOL TNDAB XC BCWHXQ.

CRA BAATXESOL QANQ JUQL UP CRA ZNCFRTNE ZNEQAVAQ, NB ZA RNKA BNXQ, CU
CRA RUBHXCNO, ZRAVA XC ZNB JVUWSRC XECU CRA SAEAVNO KXAZXES-VUUT:
NEQ CRA PXVBC CRXES CRNC ZNB QUEA RAVA ZNB ENCWVNOOL CU HWOO UPP CRA
SNOUBRAB--ZRAE CRA BHXVXC, CRNC ZNB TAVAOL SUEA UWC UE NQKAECWVAB, TWBC
RNKA VACWVEAQ ZXCR CRA MWXFDEABB UP OXSRCEXES CU XCB ANVCROL CAEATAEC.
XC CUUD XCB QXVAFCXUE CUZNVQB CRA JUQL XE N BCVNXSRC OXEA; NEQ N PAZ
BAFUEQB NPCAV, OXPA JASNE CU BRUZ XCBAOP XE CRA TNE. RA NBBAVCAQ CRNC
CRA HVAFAQXES EXSRC RNQ JAAE CRA ZUVBC CRNC AKAV CRA TNOXFA UP PNCA RNQ
NOOUCCAQ RXT; RA ZUWOQ EUC PUV CZU BXOKAV TNVDB NSNXE SU CRVUWSR ZRNC RA
RNQ AEQWVAQ ZRXOA TUUE-BCVXFDAE; JWC EUZ, RUZAKAV, XC ZNB UKAV.

CRA BNTA QNL RA ZNB QXBFRNVSAQ PVUT CRA RUBHXCNO NB HAVPAFCOL FWVAQ; JWC
CRA BRUAB TANEZRXOA VATNXEAQ JARXEQ.


XK. N TUTAEC UP RANQ XTHUVCNEFA--NE AKAEXES'B “QVNTNCXF VANQXESB”--N
TUBC BCVNESA GUWVEAL

AKAVL XERNJXCNEC UP FUHAERNSAE DEUZB, PVUT HAVBUENO XEBHAFCXUE, RUZ
CRA AECVNEFA CU PVAQAVXFD'B RUBHXCNO OUUDB; JWC NB XC XB HUBBXJOA CRNC
UCRAVB, ZRU NVA EUC FUHAERNSAE HAUHOA, TNL NOBU VANQ CRXB OXCCOA ZUVD,
ZA ZXOO JAPUVARNEQ SXKA N BRUVC QABFVXHCXUE UP XC.

CRA AICAEBXKA JWXOQXES XB BAHNVNCAQ PVUT CRA BCVAAC JL N HVACCL RXSR
VNXOXES, CRA CRXFD XVUE JNVB UP ZRXFR NVA BU PNV NHNVC, CRNC XE
NOO BAVXUWBEABB, XC XB BNXQ, BUTA KAVL CRXE PAOOUZ RNQ UP N EXSRC
UFFNBXUENOOL BMWAAYAQ RXTBAOP CRVUWSR CU SU NEQ HNL RXB OXCCOA KXBXCB
XE CRA CUZE. CRA HNVC UP CRA JUQL TUBC QXPPXFWOC CU TNENSA UE BWFR
UFFNBXUEB ZNB, EU QUWJC, CRA RANQ; RAVA, NB XB BU UPCAE CRA FNBA XE
CRA ZUVOQ, OUES-RANQAQ HAUHOA SAC CRVUWSR JABC. BU TWFR, CRAE, PUV CRA
XECVUQWFCXUE.

UEA UP CRA LUWES TAE, ZRUBA RANQ, XE N HRLBXFNO BAEBA UEOL, TXSRC JA
BNXQ CU JA UP CRA CRXFDABC, RNQ CRA ZNCFR CRNC AKAEXES. CRA VNXE HUWVAQ
QUZE XE CUVVAECB; LAC QABHXCA CRABA CZU UJBCNFOAB, CRA LUWES TNE ZNB
UJOXSAQ CU SU UWC, XP XC ZAVA JWC PUV N MWNVCAV UP NE RUWV; NEQ NB
CU CAOOXES CRA QUUV-DAAHAV NJUWC XC, CRNC, RA CRUWSRC, ZNB MWXCA
WEEAFABBNVL, XP, ZXCR N ZRUOA BDXE, RA ZAVA NJOA CU BOXH CRVUWSR CRA
VNXOXESB. CRAVA, UE CRA POUUV ONL CRA SNOUBRAB, ZRXFR CRA ZNCFRTNE
RNQ PUVSUCCAE; RA EAKAV QVANTAQ PUV N TUTAEC CRNC CRAL ZAVA CRUBA UP
PUVCWEA; NEQ CRAL HVUTXBAQ CU QU RXT SUUQ BAVKXFA XE CRA ZAC; BU RA HWC
CRAT UE. CRA MWABCXUE EUZ ZNB, XP RA FUWOQ BMWAAYA RXTBAOP CRVUWSR CRA
SVNCXES, PUV RA RNQ EAKAV CVXAQ JAPUVA. ZAOO, CRAVA RA BCUUQ.

“ZUWOQ CU RANKAE X RNQ SUC TL RANQ CRVUWSR!” BNXQ RA, XEKUOWECNVXOL; NEQ
XEBCNECOL CRVUWSR XC BOXHHAQ, ANBXOL NEQ ZXCRUWC HNXE, EUCZXCRBCNEQXES
XC ZNB HVACCL ONVSA NEQ CRXFD. JWC EUZ CRA VABC UP CRA JUQL ZNB CU JA
SUC CRVUWSR!

“NR! X NT TWFR CUU BCUWC,” SVUNEAQ RA NOUWQ, ZRXOA PXIAQ NB XE N KXFA.
“X RNQ CRUWSRC CRA RANQ ZNB CRA TUBC QXPPXFWOC HNVC UP CRA TNCCAV--UR!
UR! X VANOOL FNEEUC BMWAAYA TLBAOP CRVUWSR!”

RA EUZ ZNECAQ CU HWOO RXB UKAV-RNBCL RANQ JNFD NSNXE, JWC RA FUWOQ EUC.
PUV RXB EAFD CRAVA ZNB VUUT AEUWSR, JWC PUV EUCRXES TUVA. RXB PXVBC
PAAOXES ZNB UP NESAV; RXB EAIC CRNC RXB CATHAV PAOO CU YAVU. CRA
BRUAB UP PUVCWEA RNQ HONFAQ RXT XE CRA TUBC QVANQPWO BXCWNCXUE; NEQ,
WEPUVCWENCAOL, XC EAKAV UFFWVVAQ CU RXT CU ZXBR RXTBAOP PVAA. CRA
HXCFR-JONFD FOUWQB HUWVAQ QUZE CRAXV FUECAECB XE BCXOO RANKXAV CUVVAECB;
EUC N FVANCWVA ZNB CU JA BAAE XE CRA BCVAACB. CU VANFR WH CU CRA JAOO
ZNB ZRNC RA QXQ EUC OXDA; CU FVL NOUWQ PUV RAOH ZUWOQ RNKA NKNXOAQ RXT
OXCCOA; JABXQAB, RUZ NBRNTAQ ZUWOQ RA RNKA JAAE CU JA PUWEQ FNWSRC XE N
CVNH, OXDA NE UWCZXCCAQ PUI! RUZ ZNB RA CU CZXBC RXTBAOP CRVUWSR! RA BNZ
FOANVOL CRNC XC ZNB RXB XVVAKUFNJOA QABCXEL CU VATNXE N HVXBUEAV CXOO
QNZE, UV, HAVRNHB, AKAE ONCA XE CRA TUVEXES; CRAE CRA BTXCR TWBC JA
PACFRAQ CU PXOA NZNL CRA JNVB; JWC NOO CRNC ZUWOQ EUC JA QUEA BU MWXFDOL
NB RA FUWOQ CRXED NJUWC XC. CRA ZRUOA FRNVXCL BFRUUO, GWBC UHHUBXCA,
ZUWOQ JA XE TUCXUE; NOO CRA EAZ JUUCRB, ZXCR CRAXV EUC KAVL
FUWVCXAV-OXDA BZNVT UP BANTAE, ZUWOQ GUXE CRAT UWC UP FWVXUBXCL, NEQ
ZUWOQ SVAAC RXT ZXCR N ZXOQ “RWVVNR!” ZRXOA RA ZNB BCNEQXES XE RXB
HXOOUVL: CRAVA ZUWOQ JA N TUJ, N RXBBXES, NEQ VAGUXFXES, NEQ GAAVXES,
CAE CXTAB ZUVBA CRNE XE CRA VUZB NJUWC CRA GAZB BUTA LANVB NSU--“UR, TL
JOUUQ XB TUWECXES CU TL JVNXE; 'CXB AEUWSR CU QVXKA UEA TNQ! X BRNOO SU
ZXOQ! X DEUZ EUC ZRNC CU QU. UR! ZAVA X JWC OUUBA; TL QXYYXEABB ZUWOQ
CRAE FANBA; UR, ZAVA TL RANQ JWC OUUBA!”

LUW BAA RA UWSRC CU RNKA BNXQ CRNC BUUEAV; PUV CRA TUTAEC RA AIHVABBAQ
CRA ZXBR RXB RANQ ZNB PVAA; NEQ FWVAQ UP NOO RXB HNVUILBTB UP OUKA, RA
RNBCAEAQ UPP CU RXB VUUT, ZRAVA CRA HNXEB FUEBAMWAEC UE CRA PVXSRC CRA
BRUAB RNQ HVAHNVAQ PUV RXT, QXQ EUC BU BUUE CNDA CRAXV OANKA.

JWC LUW TWBC EUC CRXED CRNC CRA NPPNXV XB UKAV EUZ; XC SVUZB TWFR ZUVBA.

CRA EXSRC HNBBAQ, CRA EAIC QNL NOBU; JWC EUJUQL FNTA CU PACFR CRA BRUAB.

XE CRA AKAEXES “QVNTNCXF VANQXESB” ZAVA CU JA SXKAE NC CRA OXCCOA
CRANCVA XE DXES BCVAAC. CRA RUWBA ZNB PXOOAQ CU BWPPUFNCXUE; NEQ NTUES
UCRAV HXAFAB CU JA VAFXCAQ ZNB N EAZ HUAT JL R. F. NEQAVBAE, FNOOAQ, TL
NWEC'B BHAFCNFOAB; CRA FUECAECB UP ZRXFR ZAVA HVACCL EANVOL NB PUOOUZB:

“N FAVCNXE HAVBUE RNQ NE NWEC, ZRU JUNBCAQ UP HNVCXFWONV BDXOO XE
PUVCWEA-CAOOXES ZXCR FNVQB, NEQ ZRU ZNB FUEBCNECOL JAXES BCUVTAQ JL
HAVBUEB CRNC ZNECAQ CU RNKA N HAAH XECU PWCWVXCL. JWC BRA ZNB PWOO UP
TLBCAVL NJUWC RAV NVC, XE ZRXFR N FAVCNXE HNXV UP TNSXF BHAFCNFOAB
QXQ RAV ABBAECXNO BAVKXFA. RAV EAHRAZ, N TAVVL JUL, ZRU ZNB RXB NWEC'B
QNVOXES, JASSAQ BU OUES PUV CRABA BHAFCNFOAB, CRNC, NC ONBC, BRA OAEC
RXT CRA CVANBWVA, NPCAV RNKXES XEPUVTAQ RXT, ZXCR TNEL AIRUVCNCXUEB,
CRNC XE UVQAV CU AIAFWCA CRA XECAVABCXES CVXFD, RA EAAQ UEOL VAHNXV CU
BUTA HONFA ZRAVA N SVANC TNEL HAVBUEB ZAVA NBBATJOAQ; NEQ CRAE, PVUT N
RXSRAV HUBXCXUE, ZRAEFA RA FUWOQ UKAVOUUD CRA FVUZQ, HNBB CRA FUTHNEL XE
VAKXAZ JAPUVA RXT CRVUWSR RXB BHAFCNFOAB. XTTAQXNCAOL 'CRA XEEAV TNE' UP
ANFR XEQXKXQWNO ZUWOQ JA QXBHONLAQ JAPUVA RXT, OXDA N SNTA UP FNVQB, XE
ZRXFR RA WEAVVXESOL TXSRC VANQ ZRNC CRA PWCWVA UP AKAVL HAVBUE HVABAECAQ
ZNB CU JA. ZAOO HOANBAQ CRA OXCCOA TNSXFXNE RNBCAEAQ NZNL CU HVUKA CRA
HUZAVB UP CRA BHAFCNFOAB XE CRA CRANCVA; EU HONFA BAATXES CU RXT TUVA
PXCCAQ PUV BWFR N CVXNO. RA JASSAQ HAVTXBBXUE UP CRA ZUVCRL NWQXAEFA,
NEQ BAC RXB BHAFCNFOAB UE RXB EUBA. N TUCOAL HRNECNBTNSUVXN HVABAECB
XCBAOP JAPUVA RXT, ZRXFR RA QABFVXJAB XE N PAZ BNCXVXFNO CUWFRAB, LAC
ZXCRUWC AIHVABBXES RXB UHXEXUE UHAEOL: RA CAOOB CRA HAUHOA AEUWSR CU BAC
CRAT NOO CRXEDXES NEQ SWABBXES; JWC XE UVQAV CU RWVC EUJUQL, RA ZVNHB
RXB ZXCCL UVNFWONV GWQSTAECB XE N CVNEBHNVAEC KAXO, UV VNCRAV XE N OWVXQ
CRWEQAVFOUWQ, BRUUCXES PUVCR JVXSRC BHNVDB UP ZXC, CRNC CRAL TNL PNOO XE
CRA HUZQAV-TNSNYXEA UP CRA AIHAFCNEC NWQXAEFA.”

CRA RWTUVUWB HUAT ZNB NQTXVNJOL VAFXCAQ, NEQ CRA BHANDAV TWFR NHHONWQAQ.
NTUES CRA NWQXAEFA ZNB CRA LUWES TNE UP CRA RUBHXCNO, ZRU BAATAQ CU RNKA
PUVSUCCAE RXB NQKAECWVA UP CRA HVAFAQXES EXSRC. RA RNQ UE CRA BRUAB; PUV
NB LAC EU ONZPWO UZEAV RNQ NHHANVAQ CU FONXT CRAT; NEQ JABXQAB XC ZNB BU
KAVL QXVCL UWC-UP-QUUVB, CRAL ZAVA GWBC CRA CRXES PUV RXT, RA CRUWSRC.

CRA JASXEEXES UP CRA HUAT RA HVNXBAQ ZXCR SVANC SAEAVUBXCL: RA AKAE
PUWEQ CRA XQAN UVXSXENO NEQ APPAFCXKA. JWC CRNC CRA AEQ UP XC, OXDA CRA
VRXEA, ZNB KAVL XEBXSEXPXFNEC, HVUKAQ, XE RXB UHXEXUE, CRA NWCRUV'B
ZNEC UP XEKAECXUE; RA ZNB ZXCRUWC SAEXWB, ACF. CRXB ZNB NE AIFAOOAEC
UHHUVCWEXCL CU RNKA BNXQ BUTACRXES FOAKAV.

TANEZRXOA RA ZNB RNWECAQ JL CRA XQAN--RA BRUWOQ OXDA CU HUBBABB BWFR N
HNXV UP BHAFCNFOAB RXTBAOP; CRAE, HAVRNHB, JL WBXES CRAT FXVFWTBHAFCOL,
UEA ZUWOQ JA NJOA CU OUUD XECU HAUHOA'B RANVCB, ZRXFR, RA CRUWSRC, ZUWOQ
JA PNV TUVA XECAVABCXES CRNE TAVAOL CU BAA ZRNC ZNB CU RNHHAE EAIC LANV;
PUV CRNC ZA BRUWOQ NOO DEUZ XE HVUHAV CXTA, JWC CRA UCRAV EAKAV.

“X FNE EUZ,” BNXQ RA CU RXTBAOP, “PNEFL CRA ZRUOA VUZ UP ONQXAB NEQ
SAECOATAE BXCCXES CRAVA XE CRA PVUEC VUZ; XP UEA FUWOQ JWC BAA XECU
CRAXV RANVCB--LAB, CRNC ZUWOQ JA N VAKAONCXUE--N BUVC UP JNYNV. XE CRNC
ONQL LUEQAV, BU BCVNESAOL QVABBAQ, X BRUWOQ PXEQ PUV FAVCNXE N ONVSA
TXOOXEAV'B BRUH; XE CRNC UEA CRA BRUH XB ATHCL, JWC XC ZNECB FOANEXES
HONXE AEUWSR. JWC CRAVA ZUWOQ NOBU JA BUTA SUUQ BCNCAOL BRUHB NTUES
CRAT. NONB!” BXSRAQ RA, “X DEUZ UEA XE ZRXFR NOO XB BCNCAOL; JWC CRAVA
BXCB NOVANQL N BHVWFA LUWES BRUHTNE, ZRXFR XB CRA UEOL CRXES CRNC'B
NTXBB XE CRA ZRUOA BRUH. NOO ZUWOQ JA BHOAEQXQOL QAFDAQ UWC, NEQ ZA
BRUWOQ RANV, 'ZNOD XE, SAECOATAE, HVNL ZNOD XE; RAVA LUW ZXOO PXEQ NOO
LUW HOANBA CU ZNEC.' NR! X ZXBR CU RANKAE X FUWOQ ZNOD XE NEQ CNDA N
CVXH VXSRC CRVUWSR CRA RANVCB UP CRUBA HVABAEC!”

NEQ JARUOQ! CU CRA BRUAB UP PUVCWEA CRXB ZNB CRA FWA; CRA ZRUOA TNE
BRVWED CUSACRAV NEQ N TUBC WEFUTTUE GUWVEAL CRVUWSR CRA RANVCB UP CRA
PVUEC VUZ UP BHAFCNCUVB, EUZ JASNE. CRA PXVBC RANVC CRVUWSR ZRXFR RA
FNTA, ZNB CRNC UP N TXQQOA-NSAQ ONQL, JWC RA XEBCNECOL PNEFXAQ RXTBAOP
XE CRA VUUT UP CRA “XEBCXCWCXUE PUV CRA FWVA UP CRA FVUUDAQ NEQ
QAPUVTAQ,” ZRAVA FNBCB UP TXB-BRNHAE OXTJB NVA QXBHONLAQ XE ENDAQ
VANOXCL UE CRA ZNOO. LAC CRAVA ZNB CRXB QXPPAVAEFA, XE CRA XEBCXCWCXUE
CRA FNBCB ZAVA CNDAE NC CRA AECVL UP CRA HNCXAEC; JWC RAVA CRAL ZAVA
VACNXEAQ NEQ SWNVQAQ XE CRA RANVC ZRXOA CRA BUWEQ HAVBUEB ZAEC NZNL.
CRAL ZAVA, ENTAOL, FNBCB UP PATNOA PVXAEQB, ZRUBA JUQXOL UV TAECNO
QAPUVTXCXAB ZAVA RAVA TUBC PNXCRPWOOL HVABAVKAQ.

ZXCR CRA BENDA-OXDA ZVXCRXESB UP NE XQAN RA SOXQAQ XECU NEUCRAV PATNOA
RANVC; JWC CRXB BAATAQ CU RXT OXDA N ONVSA RUOL PNEA. [*] CRA ZRXCA QUKA UP
XEEUFAEFA POWCCAVAQ UKAV CRA NOCNV. RUZ SONQOL ZUWOQ RA RNKA BWED WHUE
RXB DEAAB; JWC RA TWBC NZNL CU CRA EAIC RANVC; LAC RA BCXOO RANVQ CRA
HANOXES CUEAB UP CRA UVSNE, NEQ RA RXTBAOP BAATAQ CU RNKA JAFUTA N EAZAV
NEQ N JACCAV TNE; RA PAOC WEZUVCRL CU CVANQ CRA EAXSRJUVXES BNEFCWNVL
ZRXFR N HUUV SNVVAC, ZXCR N BXFD JAQ-VXQ TUCRAV, VAKANOAQ. JWC SUQ'B
ZNVT BWE BCVANTAQ CRVUWSR CRA UHAE ZXEQUZ; OUKAOL VUBAB EUQQAQ PVUT
CRA ZUUQAE POUZAV-JUIAB UE CRA VUUP, NEQ CZU BDL-JOWA JXVQB BNES
VAGUXFXESOL, ZRXOA CRA BXFD TUCRAV XTHOUVAQ SUQ'B VXFRABC JOABBXESB UE
RAV HXUWB QNWSRCAV.

     * CATHOA


RA EUZ FVAHC UE RNEQB NEQ PAAC CRVUWSR N JWCFRAV'B BRUH; NC OANBC UE
AKAVL BXQA, NEQ NJUKA NEQ JAOUZ, CRAVA ZNB EUWSRC JWC POABR. XC ZNB CRA
RANVC UP N TUBC VABHAFCNJOA VXFR TNE, ZRUBA ENTA XB FAVCNXE CU JA PUWEQ
XE CRA QXVAFCUVL.

RA ZNB EUZ XE CRA RANVC UP CRA ZXPA UP CRXB ZUVCRL SAECOATNE. XC ZNB NE
UOQ, QXONHXQNCAQ, TUWOQAVXES QUKAFUC. CRA RWBJNEQ'B HUVCVNXC ZNB WBAQ NB
N ZANCRAV-FUFD, ZRXFR ZNB FUEEAFCAQ XE BUTA ZNL UV UCRAV ZXCR CRA QUUVB,
NEQ BU CRAL UHAEAQ NEQ BRWC UP CRAXV UZE NFFUVQ, ZRAEAKAV CRA BCAVE UOQ
RWBJNEQ CWVEAQ VUWEQ.

RAVAWHUE RA ZNEQAVAQ XECU N JUWQUXV PUVTAQ AECXVAOL UP TXVVUVB, OXDA
CRA UEA XE FNBCOA VUBAEJWVS; JWC RAVA CRA SONBBAB TNSEXPXAQ CU NE
NBCUEXBRXES QASVAA. UE CRA POUUV, XE CRA TXQQOA UP CRA VUUT, BNC, OXDA N
QNONX-ONTN, CRA XEBXSEXPXFNEC “BAOP” UP CRA HAVBUE, MWXCA FUEPUWEQAQ NC
RXB UZE SVANCEABB. RA CRAE XTNSXEAQ RA RNQ SUC XECU N EAAQOA-FNBA PWOO
UP HUXECAQ EAAQOAB UP AKAVL BXYA.

“CRXB XB FAVCNXEOL CRA RANVC UP NE UOQ TNXQ,” CRUWSRC RA. JWC RA ZNB
TXBCNDAE. XC ZNB CRA RANVC UP N LUWES TXOXCNVL TNE; N TNE, NB HAUHOA
BNXQ, UP CNOAEC NEQ PAAOXES.

XE CRA SVANCABC HAVHOAIXCL, RA EUZ FNTA UWC UP CRA ONBC RANVC XE CRA
VUZ; RA ZNB WENJOA CU HWC RXB CRUWSRCB XE UVQAV, NEQ PNEFXAQ CRNC RXB
CUU OXKAOL XTNSXENCXUE RNQ VWE NZNL ZXCR RXT.

“SUUQ RANKAEB!” BXSRAQ RA. “X RNKA BWVAOL N QXBHUBXCXUE CU TNQEABB--'CXB
QVANQPWOOL RUC RAVA; TL JOUUQ JUXOB XE TL KAXEB NEQ TL RANQ XB JWVEXES
OXDA N FUNO.” NEQ RA EUZ VATATJAVAQ CRA XTHUVCNEC AKAEC UP CRA AKAEXES
JAPUVA, RUZ RXB RANQ RNQ SUC GNTTAQ XE JACZAAE CRA XVUE VNXOXESB UP CRA
RUBHXCNO. “CRNC'B ZRNC XC XB, EU QUWJC,” BNXQ RA. “X TWBC QU BUTACRXES
XE CXTA: WEQAV BWFR FXVFWTBCNEFAB N VWBBXNE JNCR TXSRC QU TA SUUQ. X
UEOL ZXBR X ZAVA NOVANQL UE CRA WHHAV JNED.” [*]

     *XE CRABA VWBBXNE (KNHUV) JNCRB CRA HAVBUE AICAEQB RXTBAOP
     UE N JNED UV PUVT, NEQ NB RA SACB NFFWBCUTAQ CU CRA RANC,
     TUKAB CU NEUCRAV RXSRAV WH CUZNVQB CRA FAXOXES, ZRAVA, UP
     FUWVBA, CRA KNHUV XB ZNVTABC. XE CRXB TNEEAV RA NBFAEQB

NEQ BU CRAVA RA ONL UE CRA WHHAVTUBC JNED XE CRA KNHUV-JNCR; JWC ZXCR
NOO RXB FOUCRAB UE, XE RXB JUUCB NEQ SNOUBRAB, ZRXOA CRA RUC QVUHB PAOO

“RUOOUN!” FVXAQ RA, OANHXES QUZE. CRA JNCRXES NCCAEQNEC, UE RXB BXQA,
WCCAVAQ N OUWQ FVL UP NBCUEXBRTAEC ZRAE RA JARAOQ XE CRA JNCR, N TNE
FUTHOACAOL QVABBAQ.

CRA UCRAV, RUZAKAV, VACNXEAQ BWPPXFXAEC HVABAEFA UP TXEQ CU ZRXBHAV CU
RXT, “'CXB N JAC, NEQ X RNKA ZUE XC!” JWC CRA PXVBC CRXES RA QXQ NB BUUE
NB RA SUC RUTA, ZNB CU RNKA N ONVSA JOXBCAV HWC UE RXB FRABC NEQ JNFD CU
QVNZ UWC RXB TNQEABB.

CRA EAIC TUVEXES RA RNQ N BUVA FRABC NEQ N JOAAQXES JNFD; NEQ, AIFAHCXES
CRA PVXSRC, CRNC ZNB NOO CRNC RA RNQ SNXEAQ JL CRA BRUAB UP PUVCWEA.


K. TACNTUVHRUBXB UP CRA FUHLXES-FOAVD

CRA ZNCFRTNE, ZRUT ZA RNKA FAVCNXEOL EUC PUVSUCCAE, CRUWSRC TANEZRXOA
UP CRA SNOUBRAB RA RNQ PUWEQ NEQ CNDAE ZXCR RXT CU CRA RUBHXCNO; RA EUZ
ZAEC CU PACFR CRAT; NEQ NB EAXCRAV CRA OXAWCAENEC, EUV NELJUQL AOBA XE
CRA BCVAAC, FONXTAQ CRAT NB RXB HVUHAVCL, CRAL ZAVA QAOXKAVAQ UKAV CU
CRA HUOXFA-UPPXFA.*

*NB UE CRA FUECXEAEC, XE NOO ONZ NEQ HUOXFA HVNFCXFAB EUCRXES XB KAVJNO,
JWC NEL FXVFWTBCNEFA, RUZAKAV CVXPOXES, XB VAQWFAQ CU ZVXCXES, CRA
ONJUV, NB ZAOO NB CRA EWTJAV UP HNHAVB CRNC CRWB NFFWTWONCA, XB
AEUVTUWB. XE N HUOXFA-UPPXFA, FUEBAMWAECOL, ZA PXEQ FUHLXES-FOAVDB NTUES
TNEL UCRAV BFVXJAB UP KNVXUWB QAEUTXENCXUEB, UP ZRXFR, XC BAATB, UWV
RAVU ZNB UEA.


“ZRL, X QAFONVA CRA BRUAB OUUD GWBC OXDA TL UZE,” BNXQ UEA UP CRA
FOAVDB, ALXES CRA EAZOL-PUWEQ CVANBWVA, ZRUBA RXQQAE HUZAVB, AKAE RA,
BRNVH NB RA ZNB, ZNB EUC NJOA CU QXBFUKAV. “UEA TWBC RNKA TUVA CRNE
CRA ALA UP N BRUATNDAV CU DEUZ UEA HNXV PVUT CRA UCRAV,” BNXQ RA,
BUOXOUMWXYXES; NEQ HWCCXES, NC CRA BNTA CXTA, CRA SNOUBRAB XE BANVFR UP
NE UZEAV, JABXQA RXB UZE XE CRA FUVEAV.

“RAVA, BXV!” BNXQ UEA UP CRA TAE, ZRU HNECXES JVUWSRC RXT N CVATAEQUWB
HXOA UP HNHAVB.

CRA FUHLXES-FOAVD CWVEAQ VUWEQ NEQ BHUDA NZRXOA ZXCR CRA TNE NJUWC CRA
VAHUVCB NEQ OASNO QUFWTAECB XE MWABCXUE; JWC ZRAE RA RNQ PXEXBRAQ, NEQ
RXB ALA PAOO NSNXE UE CRA BRUAB, RA ZNB WENJOA CU BNL ZRACRAV CRUBA CU
CRA OAPC UV CRUBA CU CRA VXSRC JAOUESAQ CU RXT. “NC NOO AKAECB XC TWBC
JA CRUBA ZRXFR NVA ZAC,” CRUWSRC RA; JWC CRXB CXTA, XE BHXCA UP RXB
FOAKAVEABB, RA SWABBAQ MWXCA ZVUES, PUV XC ZNB GWBC CRUBA UP PUVCWEA
ZRXFR HONLAQ NB XC ZAVA XECU RXB RNEQB, UV VNCRAV UE RXB PAAC. NEQ ZRL,
X BRUWOQ OXDA CU DEUZ, NVA CRA HUOXFA EAKAV CU JA ZVUES? BU RA HWC CRAT
UE MWXFDOL, BCWFD RXB HNHAVB XE RXB HUFDAC, NEQ CUUD JABXQAB N PAZ WEQAV
RXB NVT, XECAEQXES CU OUUD CRAT CRVUWSR NC RUTA CU TNDA CRA EAFABBNVL
EUCAB. XC ZNB EUUE; NEQ CRA ZANCRAV, CRNC RNQ CRVANCAEAQ VNXE, JASNE
CU FOANV WH, ZRXOA SNXOL QVABBAQ RUOXQNL PUODB PXOOAQ CRA BCVAACB. “N
OXCCOA CVXH CU PVAQAVXFDBJWVS ZUWOQ QU TA EU SVANC RNVT,” CRUWSRC RA;
“PUV X, HUUV JANBC UP JWVQAE CRNC X NT, RNKA BU TWFR CU NEEUL TA, CRNC X
QUE'C DEUZ ZRNC N SUUQ NHHACXCA XB. 'CXB N JXCCAV FVWBC, NONB! NC ZRXFR
X NT FUEQATEAQ CU SENZ!”

EUJUQL FUWOQ JA TUVA BCANQL UV MWXAC CRNE CRXB LUWES TNE; ZA CRAVAPUVA
ZXBR RXT GUL UP CRA AIFWVBXUE ZXCR NOO UWV RANVC; NEQ XC ZXOO FAVCNXEOL
JA JAEAPXFXNO PUV N HAVBUE ZRU OANQB BU BAQAECNVL N OXPA. XE CRA HNVD
RA TAC N PVXAEQ, UEA UP UWV LUWES HUACB, ZRU CUOQ RXT CRNC CRA PUOOUZXES
QNL RA BRUWOQ BAC UWC UE RXB OUES-XECAEQAQ CUWV.

“BU LUW NVA SUXES NZNL NSNXE!” BNXQ CRA FOAVD. “LUW NVA N KAVL PVAA
NEQ RNHHL JAXES; ZA UCRAVB NVA FRNXEAQ JL CRA OAS NEQ RAOQ PNBC CU UWV
QABD.”

“LAB; JWC XC XB N FRNXE, PVXAEQ, ZRXFR AEBWVAB LUW CRA JOABBAQ JVANQ
UP AIXBCAEFA,” NEBZAVAQ CRA HUAC. “LUW EAAQ PAAO EU FNVA PUV CRA FUTXES
TUVVUZ: ZRAE LUW NVA UOQ, LUW VAFAXKA N HAEBXUE.”

“CVWA,” BNXQ CRA FOAVD, BRVWSSXES RXB BRUWOQAVB; “NEQ LAC LUW NVA
CRA JACCAV UPP. CU BXC NC UEA'B ANBA NEQ HUACXBA--CRNC XB N HOANBWVA;
AKAVLJUQL RNB BUTACRXES NSVAANJOA CU BNL CU LUW, NEQ LUW NVA NOZNLB LUWV
UZE TNBCAV. EU, PVXAEQ, LUW BRUWOQ JWC CVL ZRNC XC XB CU BXC PVUT UEA
LANV'B AEQ CU CRA UCRAV UFFWHXAQ ZXCR NEQ GWQSXES CRA TUBC CVXKXNO
TNCCAVB.”

CRA HUAC BRUUD RXB RANQ, CRA FUHLXES-FOAVD QXQ CRA BNTA. ANFR UEA DAHC
CU RXB UZE UHXEXUE, NEQ BU CRAL BAHNVNCAQ.

“XC'B N BCVNESA VNFA, CRUBA HUACB!” BNXQ CRA FOAVD, ZRU ZNB KAVL PUEQ UP
BUOXOUMWXYXES. “X BRUWOQ OXDA BUTA QNL, GWBC PUV N CVXNO, CU CNDA BWFR
ENCWVA WHUE TA, NEQ JA N HUAC TLBAOP; X NT KAVL BWVA X BRUWOQ TNDA
EU BWFR TXBAVNJOA KAVBAB NB CRA UCRAVB. CUQNL, TACRXEDB, XB N TUBC
QAOXFXUWB QNL PUV N HUAC. ENCWVA BAATB NEAZ CU FAOAJVNCA RAV NZNDAEXES
XECU OXPA. CRA NXV XB BU WEWBWNOOL FOANV, CRA FOUWQB BNXO UE BU
JWULNECOL, NEQ PVUT CRA SVAAE RAVJNSA N PVNSVNEFA XB AIRNOAQ CRNC PXOOB
TA ZXCR QAOXSRC. PUV TNEL N LANV RNKA X EUC PAOC NB NC CRXB TUTAEC.”

ZA BAA NOVANQL, JL CRA PUVASUXES APPWBXUE, CRNC RA XB JAFUTA N HUAC; CU
SXKA PWVCRAV HVUUP UP XC, RUZAKAV, ZUWOQ XE TUBC FNBAB JA XEBXHXQ, PUV
XC XB N TUBC PUUOXBR EUCXUE CU PNEFL N HUAC QXPPAVAEC PVUT UCRAV TAE.
NTUES CRA ONCCAV CRAVA TNL JA PNV TUVA HUACXFNO ENCWVAB CRNE TNEL NE
NFDEUZOAQSAQ HUAC, ZRAE AINTXEAQ TUVA FOUBAOL, FUWOQ JUNBC UP; CRA
QXPPAVAEFA UEOL XB, CRNC CRA HUAC HUBBABBAB N JACCAV TAECNO TATUVL, UE
ZRXFR NFFUWEC RA XB NJOA CU VACNXE CRA PAAOXES NEQ CRA CRUWSRC CXOO CRAL
FNE JA ATJUQXAQ JL TANEB UP ZUVQB; N PNFWOCL ZRXFR CRA UCRAVB QU EUC
HUBBABB. JWC CRA CVNEBXCXUE PVUT N FUTTUEHONFA ENCWVA CU UEA CRNC XB
VXFROL AEQUZAQ, QATNEQB NOZNLB N TUVA UV OABB JVANDEAFD OANH UKAV N
FAVCNXE NJLBB ZRXFR LNZEB CRVANCAEXESOL JAOUZ; NEQ CRWB TWBC CRA BWQQAE
FRNESA ZXCR CRA FOAVD BCVXDA CRA VANQAV.

“CRA BZAAC NXV!” FUECXEWAQ RA UP CRA HUOXFA-UPPXFA, XE RXB QVANTL
XTNSXEXESB; “RUZ XC VATXEQB TA UP CRA KXUOACB XE CRA SNVQAE UP TL NWEC
TNSQNOAEN! LAB, CRAE X ZNB N OXCCOA ZXOQ JUL, ZRU QXQ EUC SU CU BFRUUO
KAVL VASWONVOL. U RANKAEB! 'CXB N OUES CXTA BXEFA X RNKA CRUWSRC UE
CRUBA CXTAB. CRA SUUQ UOQ BUWO! BRA OXKAQ JARXEQ CRA AIFRNESA. BRA
NOZNLB RNQ N PAZ CZXSB UV SVAAE BRUUCB XE ZNCAV--OAC CRA ZXECAV VNSA
ZXCRUWC NB XC TXSRC. CRA KXUOACB AIRNOAQ CRAXV BZAAC JVANCR, ZRXOBC X
HVABBAQ NSNXEBC CRA ZXEQUZHNEAB FUKAVAQ ZXCR PNECNBCXF PVUBC-ZUVD CRA
FUHHAV FUXE X RNQ RANCAQ UE CRA BCUKA, NEQ BU TNQA HAAH-RUOAB.
ZRNC BHOAEQXQ KXBCNB ZAVA CRAE UHAEAQ CU TL KXAZ! ZRNC FRNESA--ZRNC
TNSEXPXFAEFA! LUEQAV XE CRA FNENO ONL CRA BRXHB PVUYAE WH, NEQ QABAVCAQ
JL CRAXV ZRUOA FVAZB, ZXCR N BFVANTXES FVUZ PUV CRA BUOA UFFWHNEC. JWC
ZRAE CRA BHVXES, ZXCR N SAECOA BCXVVXES TUCXUE, NEEUWEFAQ RAV NVVXKNO,
N EAZ NEQ JWBL OXPA NVUBA; ZXCR BUESB NEQ RWVVNRB CRA XFA ZNB BNZE
NBWEQAV, CRA BRXHB ZAVA PVABR CNVVAQ NEQ VXSSAQ, CRNC CRAL TXSRC BNXO
NZNL CU QXBCNEC ONEQB. JWC X RNKA VATNXEAQ RAVA--TWBC NOZNLB VATNXE
RAVA, BXCCXES NC TL QABD XE CRA UPPXFA, NEQ HNCXAECOL BAA UCRAV HAUHOA
PACFR CRAXV HNBBHUVCB CU SU NJVUNQ. BWFR XB TL PNCA! NONB!”--BXSRAQ RA,
NEQ ZNB NSNXE BXOAEC. “SVANC RANKAE! ZRNC XB FUTA CU TA! EAKAV RNKA X
CRUWSRC UV PAOC OXDA CRXB JAPUVA! XC TWBC JA CRA BWTTAV NXV CRNC NPPAFCB
TA ZXCR PAAOXESB NOTUBC NB QXBMWXACXES NB CRAL NVA VAPVABRXES.”

RA PAOC XE RXB HUFDAC PUV CRA HNHAVB. “CRABA HUOXFA-VAHUVCB ZXOO BUUE
BCAT CRA CUVVAEC UP TL XQANB, NEQ APPAFCWNOOL RXEQAV NEL VAJAOOXUWB
UKAVPOUZXES UP CRA CXTA-ZUVE JNEDB UP UPPXFXNO QWCXAB”; RA BNXQ CU
RXTBAOP FUEBUOXESOL, ZRXOA RXB ALA VNE UKAV CRA PXVBC HNSA. “QNTA
CXSJVXCR, CVNSAQL XE PXKA NFCB.” “ZRNC XB CRNC? NEQ LAC XC XB WEQAEXNJOL
TL UZE RNEQZVXCXES. RNKA X ZVXCCAE CRA CVNSAQL? ZUEQAVPWO, KAVL
ZUEQAVPWO!--NEQ CRXB--ZRNC RNKA X RAVA? 'XECVXSWA UE CRA VNTHNVCB; UV
CRA QNL UP VAHAECNEFA: KNWQAKXOOA ZXCR EAZ BUESB CU CRA TUBC PNKUVXCA
NXVB.' CRA QAWFA! ZRAVA QXQ X SAC NOO CRXB VWJJXBR? BUTA UEA TWBC RNKA
BOXHHAQ XC BOLOL XECU TL HUFDAC PUV N GUDA. CRAVA XB CUU N OACCAV CU TA;
N FVWTHOAQ OACCAV NEQ CRA BANO JVUDAE.”

LAB; XC ZNB EUC N KAVL HUOXCA AHXBCOA PVUT CRA TNENSAV UP N CRANCVA, XE
ZRXFR JUCR HXAFAB ZAVA PONCOL VAPWBAQ.

“RAT! RAT!” BNXQ CRA FOAVD JVANCROABBOL, NEQ MWXCA AIRNWBCAQ RA BANCAQ
RXTBAOP UE N JNED. RXB CRUWSRCB ZAVA BU AONBCXF, RXB RANVC BU CAEQAV;
NEQ XEKUOWECNVXOL RA HXFDAQ UEA UP CRA EANVABC POUZAVB. XC XB N BXTHOA
QNXBL, GWBC JWVBCXES UWC UP CRA JWQ. ZRNC CRA JUCNEXBC CAOOB WB NPCAV
N EWTJAV UP XTHAVPAFC OAFCWVAB, CRA POUZAV HVUFONXTAQ XE N TXEWCA. XC
VAONCAQ CRA TLCRWB UP XCB JXVCR, CUOQ UP CRA HUZAV UP CRA BWE-OXSRC CRNC
BHVANQ UWC XCB QAOXFNCA OANKAB, NEQ PUVFAQ CRAT CU XTHVASENCA CRA NXV
ZXCR CRAXV XEFAEBA--NEQ CRAE RA CRUWSRC UP CRA TNEXPUOQ BCVWSSOAB UP
OXPA, ZRXFR XE OXDA TNEEAV NZNDAE CRA JWQQXES POUZAVB UP PAAOXES XE UWV
JUBUT. OXSRC NEQ NXV FUECAEQ ZXCR FRXKNOVXF ATWONCXUE PUV CRA OUKA UP
CRA PNXV POUZAV CRNC JABCUZAQ RAV FRXAP PNKUVB UE CRA ONCCAV; PWOO UP

RAV CAEQAV OANKAB CUSACRAV NEQ BOAHC XE CRA ATJVNFAB UP CRA NXV. “XC XB
CRA OXSRC ZRXFR NQUVEB TA,” BNXQ CRA POUZAV.

“JWC 'CXB CRA NXV ZRXFR AENJOAB CRAA CU JVANCRA,” BNXQ CRA HUAC'B KUXFA.

FOUBA JL BCUUQ N JUL ZRU QNBRAQ RXB BCXFD XECU N ZAC QXCFR. CRA QVUHB UP
ZNCAV BHONBRAQ WH CU CRA SVAAE OANPL VUUP, NEQ CRA FOAVD CRUWSRC UP CRA

JA RWVOAQ NJUKA CRA FOUWQB. ZRXOA RA CRUWSRC UP CRXB NEQ UP CRA ZRUOA
TACNTUVHRUBXB RA RNQ WEQAVSUEA, RA BTXOAQ NEQ BNXQ, “X BOAAH NEQ QVANT;

LAB! FUWOQ X AIFRNESA TL ENCWVA ZXCR NEL UCRAV FVANCWVA, X PNXE ZUWOQ JA

RA RNQ RNVQOL WCCAVAQ CRABA RNBCL ZUVQB ZRAE CRA BDXVCB NEQ BOAAKAB

 CRXB PXEA CXVNQA BUWEQAQ, RUZAKAV, CU CRA WESUQOL BNXOUV-JUL OXDA N TAVA

KX. CRA JABC CRNC CRA SNOUBRAB SNKA

CRA PUOOUZXES QNL, ANVOL XE CRA TUVEXES, ZRXOA CRA FOAVD ZNB BCXOO XE

CRA BWE XB BRXEXES TUBC XEKXCXESOL. X BRUWOQ OXDA CU SU UWC N OXCCOA.”

RA SUC CRA SNOUBRAB, NEQ RA ZNB BUUE JAOUZ XE N OXCCOA QWUQAFXTU SNVQAE,

BCNEQXES. AKAE BWFR N OXCCOA SNVQAE NB CRXB ZNB FUEBXQAVAQ XE CRA

CRA LUWES TNE ZNEQAVAQ WH NEQ QUZE CRA ENVVUZ HNCRB, NB ZAOO NB CRA

NEQ ZXCR CRA SUKAVETAEC. XE RXB VXSRC HUFDAC RA RNQ RXB OACCAV UP
FVAQXC, XE CRA OAPC, RXB HNBBHUVC, NEQ XE N BTNOO OANCRAVE HWVBA BUTA
QUWJOA OUWXB Q'UV, FNVAPWOOL BAZE WH XE CRA JUBUT UP RXB ZNXBCFUNC.
AKAVL QVANT HVUFONXTAQ CRNC UEA UV CRA UCRAV UP CRABA KNOWNJOAB ZNB
OUBC; ZRAVAPUVA RA BCNVCAQ WH NB XE N PAKAV; NEQ CRA PXVBC TUKATAEC

UV EUC. PVUT CRA VUUP XEBXQA CRA FNVVXNSA, WTJVAOONB, ZNODXES-BCXFDB,
RNCB, NEQ BWEQVL UCRAV NVCXFOAB ZAVA QAHAEQXES, NEQ RXEQAVAQ CRA KXAZ,

FXVFWTBCNEFAB TAVAOL, NEQ UE CRA JUBUT UP ENCWVA XTJXJA CRA TXOD UP
HWVABC RWTNE AEGULTAEC.

SVNEQ, BUOATE, NEQ QNVD ZNB CRA ZRUOA ONEQBFNHA NVUWEQ. CRA SXSNECXF

“NWSR!” BXSRAQ RA, “ZAVA ZA UEOL UE CRA UCRAV BXQA CRA NOHB, CRAE ZA

NEQ BU BNLXES RA ZNB UE CRA UCRAV BXQA XE XCNOL, JACZAAE POUVAEFA NEQ

CRA HUXBUEUWB POXAB NEQ SENCB BZNVTAQ NVUWEQ JL CRUWBNEQB; XE KNXE UEA
ZNKAQ TLVCOA-JVNEFRAB NJUWC OXDA TNQ; CRA NWQNFXUWB XEBAFC HUHWONCXUE

ZAOO-FVNTTAQ FNVVXNSA ZRUBA PNFA ZNB EUC BZUOOAE NEQ BUVA PVUT CRAXV
VNKAEUWB JXCAB. CRA HUUV RUVBAB, CUVCWVAQ NOTUBC CU QANCR, BWPPAVAQ TUBC
PVUT CRXB CVWOL ASLHCXNE HONSWA; CRA POXAB NOXSRCAQ WHUE CRAT XE ONVSA
QXBSWBCXES BZNVTB; NEQ XP CRA FUNFRTNE SUC QUZE NEQ BFVNHAQ CRAT UPP,
RNVQOL N TXEWCA AONHBAQ JAPUVA CRAL ZAVA CRAVA NSNXE. CRA BWE EUZ BAC: N
PVAAYXES FUOQ, CRUWSR UP BRUVC QWVNCXUE HAVKNQAQ CRA ZRUOA FVANCXUE;
XC ZNB OXDA N RUVVXQ SWBC FUTXES PVUT N JWVXNO-KNWOC UE N ZNVT BWTTAV'B
QNL--JWC NOO NVUWEQ CRA TUWECNXEB VACNXEAQ CRNC ZUEQAVPWO SVAAE CUEA
ZRXFR ZA BAA XE BUTA UOQ HXFCWVAB, NEQ ZRXFR, BRUWOQ ZA EUC RNKA BAAE N
BXTXONV HONL UP FUOUV XE CRA BUWCR, ZA QAFONVA NC UEFA CU JA WEENCWVNO.
XC ZNB N SOUVXUWB HVUBHAFC; JWC CRA BCUTNFR ZNB ATHCL, CRA JUQL CXVAQ;
NOO CRNC CRA RANVC FNVAQ NEQ OUESAQ PUV ZNB SUUQ EXSRC-MWNVCAVB; LAC
RUZ ZUWOQ CRAL JA? PUV CRABA UEA OUUDAQ TWFR TUVA NEIXUWBOL CRNE PUV CRA
FRNVTB UP ENCWVA, ZRXFR AKAVL ZRAVA ZAVA BU HVUPWBAOL QXBHONLAQ.

CRA VUNQ OAQ CRVUWSR NE UOXKA-SVUKA, NEQ RAVA CRA BUOXCNVL XEE ZNB
BXCWNCAQ. CAE UV CZAOKA FVXHHOAQ-JASSNVB RNQ AEFNTHAQ UWCBXQA. CRA
RANOCRXABC UP CRAT VABATJOAQ, CU WBA NE AIHVABBXUE UP TNVVLNC'B,
“RWESAV'B AOQABC BUE ZRAE RA RNQ FUTA UP NSA”; CRA UCRAVB ZAVA AXCRAV
JOXEQ, RNQ ZXCRAVAQ OASB NEQ FVAHC NJUWC UE CRAXV RNEQB, UV ZXCRAVAQ
NVTB NEQ PXESAVOABB RNEQB. XC ZNB CRA TUBC ZVACFRAQ TXBAVL, QVNSSAQ
PVUT NTUES CRA PXOCRXABC VNSB. “AIFAOOAEYN, TXBAVNJXOX!” BXSRAQ CRAL,
CRVWBCXES PUVCR CRAXV QAPUVTAQ OXTJB CU KXAZ. AKAE CRA RUBCABB, ZXCR
JNVA PAAC, WEFUTJAQ RNXV, NEQ QVABBAQ XE N SNVTAEC UP QUWJCPWO FUOUV,
VAFAXKAQ CRA SWABCB SVWTJOXESOL. CRA QUUVB ZAVA PNBCAEAQ ZXCR N OUUH UP
BCVXES; CRA POUUV UP CRA VUUTB HVABAECAQ N BCUEA HNKXES RNOP CUVE
WH; JNCB POWCCAVAQ ZXOQOL NJUWC CRA FAXOXES; NEQ NB CU CRA BTAOO
CRAVAXE--EU--CRNC ZNB JALUEQ QABFVXHCXUE.

“LUW RNQ JACCAV ONL CRA FOUCR JAOUZ XE CRA BCNJOA,” BNXQ UEA UP CRA
CVNKAOOAVB; “CRAVA, NC NOO AKAECB, UEA DEUZB ZRNC UEA XB JVANCRXES.”

CRA ZXEQUZB ZAVA MWXFDOL UHAEAQ, CU OAC XE N OXCCOA PVABR NXV. MWXFDAV,
RUZAKAV, CRNE CRA JVAAYA, CRA ZXCRAVAQ, BNOOUZ NVTB UP CRA JASSNVB ZAVA
CRVWBC XE, NFFUTHNEXAQ JL CRA ACAVENO ZRXEA UP “TXBAVNJXOX, TXBAVNJXOX,
AIFAOOAEYN!” UE CRA ZNOOB ZAVA QXBHONLAQ XEEWTAVNJOA XEBFVXHCXUEB,
ZVXCCAE XE EANVOL AKAVL ONESWNSA UP AWVUHA, BUTA XE KAVBA, BUTA XE
HVUBA, TUBC UP CRAT EUC KAVL ONWQNCUVL UP “JAOON XCNOXN.”

CRA TANO ZNB BAVKAQ. XC FUEBXBCAQ UP N BUWH UP BNOCAQ ZNCAV, BANBUEAQ
ZXCR HAHHAV NEQ VNEFXQ UXO. CRA ONBC XESVAQXAEC HONLAQ N KAVL HVUTXEAEC
HNVC XE CRA BNONQ; BCNOA ASSB NEQ VUNBCAQ FUFDB'-FUTJB PWVEXBRAQ CRA
SVNEQ QXBR UP CRA VAHNBC; CRA ZXEA AKAE ZNB EUC ZXCRUWC N QXBSWBCXES
CNBCA--XC ZNB OXDA N TAQXFXENO QVNWSRC.

NC EXSRC CRA JUIAB NEQ UCRAV APPAFCB UP CRA HNBBAESAVB ZAVA HONFAQ
NSNXEBC CRA VXFDACL QUUVB. UEA UP CRA CVNKAOOAVB DAHC ZNCFR ZRXOA CRA
UCRAVB BOAHC. CRA BAECVL ZNB UWV LUWES QXKXEA. RUZ FOUBA XC ZNB XE CRA
FRNTJAV! CRA RANC UHHVABBXKA CU BWPPUFNCXUE--CRA SENCB RWTTAQ NEQ BCWES
WEFANBXESOL--CRA “TXBAVNJXOX” ZXCRUWC ZRXEAQ NEQ TUNEAQ XE CRAXV BOAAH.

“CVNKAOOXES ZUWOQ JA NSVAANJOA AEUWSR,” BNXQ RA SVUNEXES, “XP UEA UEOL
RNQ EU JUQL, UV FUWOQ BAEQ XC CU VABC ZRXOA CRA BHXVXC ZAEC UE XCB
HXOSVXTNSA WERXEQAVAQ, ZRXCRAV CRA KUXFA ZXCRXE TXSRC FNOO XC. ZRAVAKAV
X SU, X NT HWVBWAQ JL N OUESXES CRNC XB XEBNCXNJOA--CRNC X FNEEUC
AIHONXE CU TLBAOP, NEQ CRNC CANVB TL KAVL RANVC. X ZNEC BUTACRXES JACCAV
CRNE ZRNC XB JWC ZRNC XB POAQ XE NE XEBCNEC. JWC ZRNC XB XC, NEQ ZRAVA
XB XC CU JA PUWEQ? LAC, X DEUZ XE VANOXCL ZRNC XC XB X ZXBR PUV. UR!
TUBC RNHHL ZAVA X, FUWOQ X JWC VANFR UEA NXT--FUWOQ JWC VANFR CRA
RNHHXABC UP NOO!”

NEQ NB RA BHUDA CRA ZUVQ RA ZNB NSNXE XE RXB RUTA; CRA OUES ZRXCA
FWVCNXEB RWES QUZE PVUT CRA ZXEQUZB, NEQ XE CRA TXQQOA UP CRA POUUV
BCUUQ CRA JONFD FUPPXE; XE XC RA ONL XE CRA BOAAH UP QANCR. RXB ZXBR
ZNB PWOPXOOAQ--CRA JUQL VABCAQ, ZRXOA CRA BHXVXC ZAEC WERXEQAVAQ UE XCB
HXOSVXTNSA. “OAC EU UEA QAAT RXTBAOP RNHHL JAPUVA RXB AEQ,” ZAVA CRA
ZUVQB UP BUOUE; NEQ RAVA ZNB N EAZ NEQ JVXOOXNEC HVUUP UP CRA ZXBQUT UP
CRA UOQ NHUCRAST.

AKAVL FUVHBA XB N BHRLEI UP XTTUVCNOXCL; RAVA CUU UE CRA JONFD FUPPXE
CRA BHRLEI SNKA WB EU NEBZAV CU ZRNC RA ZRU ONL ZXCRXE RNQ ZVXCCAE CZU
QNLB JAPUVA:

     “U TXSRCL QANCR! CRL BXOAEFA CANFRAB EUWSRC,
       CRUW OANQABC UEOL CU CRA EANV SVNKA'B JVXED;
      XB JVUDAE EUZ CRA ONQQAV UP TL CRUWSRCB?
     QU X XEBCANQ UP TUWECXES UEOL BXED?

     UWV RANKXABC SVXAP CRA ZUVOQ UPC BAACR EUC,
      UWV BUVABC HNXE ZA RXQA PVUT BCVNESAV ALAB:
      NEQ PUV CRA BWPPAVAV CRAVA XB EUCRXES OAPC
     JWC CRA SVAAE TUWEQ CRNC U'AV CRA FUPPXE OXAB.”

CZU PXSWVAB ZAVA TUKXES XE CRA FRNTJAV. ZA DEAZ CRAT JUCR; XC ZNB CRA
PNXVL UP FNVA, NEQ CRA ATXBBNVL UP PUVCWEA. CRAL JUCR JAEC UKAV CRA
FUVHBA.

“QU LUW EUZ BAA,” BNXQ FNVA, “ZRNC RNHHXEABB LUWV SNOUBRAB RNKA JVUWSRC
CU TNEDXEQ?”

“CU RXT, NC OANBC, ZRU BOWTJAVB RAVA, CRAL RNKA JVUWSRC NE XTHAVXBRNJOA
JOABBXES,” NEBZAVAQ CRA UCRAV.

“NR EU!” VAHOXAQ FNVA. “RA CUUD RXB QAHNVCWVA RXTBAOP; RA ZNB EUC FNOOAQ
NZNL. RXB TAECNO HUZAVB RAVA JAOUZ ZAVA EUC BCVUES AEUWSR CU VANFR CRA
CVANBWVAB OLXES JALUEQ CRXB OXPA, NEQ ZRXFR RXB QABCXEL UVQNXEAQ RA
BRUWOQ UJCNXE. X ZXOO EUZ FUEPAV N JAEAPXC UE RXT.”

NEQ BRA CUUD CRA SNOUBRAB PVUT RXB PAAC; RXB BOAAH UP QANCR ZNB AEQAQ;
NEQ RA ZRU RNQ JAAE CRWB FNOOAQ JNFD NSNXE CU OXPA NVUBA PVUT RXB
QVANQ FUWFR XE NOO CRA KXSUV UP LUWCR. FNVA KNEXBRAQ, NEQ ZXCR RAV CRA

ACAVEXCL.




CRA PXV CVAA

UWC XE CRA ZUUQB BCUUQ N EXFA OXCCOA PXV CVAA. CRA HONFA RA RNQ ZNB N
KAVL SUUQ UEA: CRA BWE BRUEA UE RXT: NB CU PVABR NXV, CRAVA ZNB AEUWSR
UP CRNC, NEQ VUWEQ RXT SVAZ TNEL ONVSA-BXYAQ FUTVNQAB, HXEAB NB ZAOO NB
PXVB. JWC CRA OXCCOA PXV ZNECAQ BU KAVL TWFR CU JA N SVUZE-WH CVAA.

RA QXQ EUC CRXED UP CRA ZNVT BWE NEQ UP CRA PVABR NXV; RA QXQ EUC FNVA
PUV CRA OXCCOA FUCCNSA FRXOQVAE CRNC VNE NJUWC NEQ HVNCCOAQ ZRAE CRAL
ZAVA XE CRA ZUUQB OUUDXES PUV ZXOQ-BCVNZJAVVXAB. CRA FRXOQVAE UPCAE FNTA
ZXCR N ZRUOA HXCFRAV PWOO UP JAVVXAB, UV N OUES VUZ UP CRAT CRVANQAQ UE
N BCVNZ, NEQ BNC QUZE EANV CRA LUWES CVAA NEQ BNXQ, “UR, RUZ HVACCL RA
XB! ZRNC N EXFA OXCCOA PXV!” JWC CRXB ZNB ZRNC CRA CVAA FUWOQ EUC JANV
CU RANV.

NC CRA AEQ UP N LANV RA RNQ BRUC WH N SUUQ QANO, NEQ NPCAV NEUCRAV LANV
RA ZNB NEUCRAV OUES JXC CNOOAV; PUV ZXCR PXV CVAAB UEA FNE NOZNLB CAOO
JL CRA BRUUCB RUZ TNEL LANVB UOQ CRAL NVA.

“UR! ZAVA X JWC BWFR N RXSR CVAA NB CRA UCRAVB NVA,” BXSRAQ RA. “CRAE X
BRUWOQ JA NJOA CU BHVANQ UWC TL JVNEFRAB, NEQ ZXCR CRA CUHB CU OUUD XECU
CRA ZXQA ZUVOQ! CRAE ZUWOQ CRA JXVQB JWXOQ EABCB NTUES TL JVNEFRAB: NEQ
ZRAE CRAVA ZNB N JVAAYA, X FUWOQ JAEQ ZXCR NB TWFR BCNCAOXEABB NB CRA
UCRAVB!”

EAXCRAV CRA BWEJANTB, EUV CRA JXVQB, EUV CRA VAQ FOUWQB ZRXFR TUVEXES
NEQ AKAEXES BNXOAQ NJUKA RXT, SNKA CRA OXCCOA CVAA NEL HOANBWVA.

XE ZXECAV, ZRAE CRA BEUZ ONL SOXCCAVXES UE CRA SVUWEQ, N RNVA ZUWOQ
UPCAE FUTA OANHXES NOUES, NEQ GWTH VXSRC UKAV CRA OXCCOA CVAA. UR, CRNC
TNQA RXT BU NESVL! JWC CZU ZXECAVB ZAVA HNBC, NEQ XE CRA CRXVQ CRA CVAA
ZNB BU ONVSA CRNC CRA RNVA ZNB UJOXSAQ CU SU VUWEQ XC. “CU SVUZ NEQ
SVUZ, CU SAC UOQAV NEQ JA CNOO,” CRUWSRC CRA CVAA--“CRNC, NPCAV NOO, XB
CRA TUBC QAOXSRCPWO CRXES XE CRA ZUVOQ!”

XE NWCWTE CRA ZUUQ-FWCCAVB NOZNLB FNTA NEQ PAOOAQ BUTA UP CRA ONVSABC
CVAAB. CRXB RNHHAEAQ AKAVL LANV; NEQ CRA LUWES PXV CVAA, CRNC RNQ EUZ
SVUZE CU N KAVL FUTAOL BXYA, CVATJOAQ NC CRA BXSRC; PUV CRA TNSEXPXFAEC
SVANC CVAAB PAOO CU CRA ANVCR ZXCR EUXBA NEQ FVNFDXES, CRA JVNEFRAB ZAVA
OUHHAQ UPP, NEQ CRA CVAAB OUUDAQ OUES NEQ JNVA; CRAL ZAVA RNVQOL CU JA
VAFUSEXBAQ; NEQ CRAE CRAL ZAVA ONXQ XE FNVCB, NEQ CRA RUVBAB QVNSSAQ
CRAT UWC UP CRA ZUUQ.

ZRAVA QXQ CRAL SU CU? ZRNC JAFNTA UP CRAT?

XE BHVXES, ZRAE CRA BZNOOUZB NEQ CRA BCUVDB FNTA, CRA CVAA NBDAQ CRAT,
“QUE'C LUW DEUZ ZRAVA CRAL RNKA JAAE CNDAE? RNKA LUW EUC TAC CRAT
NELZRAVA?”

CRA BZNOOUZB QXQ EUC DEUZ NELCRXES NJUWC XC; JWC CRA BCUVD OUUDAQ
TWBXES, EUQQAQ RXB RANQ, NEQ BNXQ, “LAB; X CRXED X DEUZ; X TAC TNEL
BRXHB NB X ZNB POLXES RXCRAV PVUT ASLHC; UE CRA BRXHB ZAVA TNSEXPXFAEC
TNBCB, NEQ X KAECWVA CU NBBAVC CRNC XC ZNB CRAL CRNC BTAOC BU UP PXV.
X TNL FUESVNCWONCA LUW, PUV CRAL OXPCAQ CRATBAOKAB UE RXSR TUBC
TNGABCXFNOOL!”

“UR, ZAVA X JWC UOQ AEUWSR CU POL NFVUBB CRA BAN! JWC RUZ QUAB CRA BAN
OUUD XE VANOXCL? ZRNC XB XC OXDA?”

“CRNC ZUWOQ CNDA N OUES CXTA CU AIHONXE,” BNXQ CRA BCUVD, NEQ ZXCR CRABA
ZUVQB UPP RA ZAEC.

“VAGUXFA XE CRL SVUZCR!” BNXQ CRA BWEJANTB. “VAGUXFA XE CRL KXSUVUWB
SVUZCR, NEQ XE CRA PVABR OXPA CRNC TUKACR ZXCRXE CRAA!”

NEQ CRA ZXEQ DXBBAQ CRA CVAA, NEQ CRA QAZ ZAHC CANVB UKAV RXT; JWC CRA
PXV WEQAVBCUUQ XC EUC.

ZRAE FRVXBCTNB FNTA, MWXCA LUWES CVAAB ZAVA FWC QUZE: CVAAB ZRXFR UPCAE
ZAVA EUC AKAE NB ONVSA UV UP CRA BNTA NSA NB CRXB PXV CVAA, ZRU FUWOQ
EAKAV VABC, JWC NOZNLB ZNECAQ CU JA UPP. CRABA LUWES CVAAB, NEQ CRAL
ZAVA NOZNLB CRA PXEABC OUUDXES, VACNXEAQ CRAXV JVNEFRAB; CRAL ZAVA ONXQ
UE FNVCB, NEQ CRA RUVBAB QVAZ CRAT UWC UP CRA ZUUQ.

“ZRAVA NVA CRAL SUXES CU?” NBDAQ CRA PXV. “CRAL NVA EUC CNOOAV CRNE
X; CRAVA ZNB UEA XEQAAQ CRNC ZNB FUEBXQAVNJOL BRUVCAV; NEQ ZRL QU CRAL
VACNXE NOO CRAXV JVNEFRAB? ZRXCRAV NVA CRAL CNDAE?”

“ZA DEUZ! ZA DEUZ!” FRXVHAQ CRA BHNVVUZB. “ZA RNKA HAAHAQ XE NC CRA
ZXEQUZB XE CRA CUZE JAOUZ! ZA DEUZ ZRXCRAV CRAL NVA CNDAE! CRA SVANCABC
BHOAEQUV NEQ CRA SVANCABC TNSEXPXFAEFA UEA FNE XTNSXEA NZNXC CRAT. ZA
HAAHAQ CRVUWSR CRA ZXEQUZB, NEQ BNZ CRAT HONECAQ XE CRA TXQQOA UP CRA
ZNVT VUUT NEQ UVENTAECAQ ZXCR CRA TUBC BHOAEQXQ CRXESB, ZXCR SXOQAQ
NHHOAB, ZXCR SXESAVJVANQ, ZXCR CULB, NEQ TNEL RWEQVAQ OXSRCB!”

“NEQ CRAE?” NBDAQ CRA PXV CVAA, CVATJOXES XE AKAVL JUWSR. “NEQ CRAE?
ZRNC RNHHAEB CRAE?”

“ZA QXQ EUC BAA NELCRXES TUVA: XC ZNB XEFUTHNVNJOL JANWCXPWO.”

“X ZUWOQ PNXE DEUZ XP X NT QABCXEAQ PUV BU SOUVXUWB N FNVAAV,” FVXAQ
CRA CVAA, VAGUXFXES. “CRNC XB BCXOO JACCAV CRNE CU FVUBB CRA BAN! ZRNC
N OUESXES QU X BWPPAV! ZAVA FRVXBCTNB JWC FUTA! X NT EUZ CNOO, NEQ TL
JVNEFRAB BHVANQ OXDA CRA UCRAVB CRNC ZAVA FNVVXAQ UPP ONBC LANV! UR!
ZAVA X JWC NOVANQL UE CRA FNVC! ZAVA X XE CRA ZNVT VUUT ZXCR NOO CRA
BHOAEQUV NEQ TNSEXPXFAEFA! LAB; CRAE BUTACRXES JACCAV, BUTACRXES BCXOO
SVNEQAV, ZXOO BWVAOL PUOOUZ, UV ZRAVAPUVA BRUWOQ CRAL CRWB UVENTAEC TA?
BUTACRXES JACCAV, BUTACRXES BCXOO SVNEQAV TWBC PUOOUZ--JWC ZRNC? UR, RUZ
X OUES, RUZ X BWPPAV! X QU EUC DEUZ TLBAOP ZRNC XB CRA TNCCAV ZXCR TA!”

“VAGUXFA XE UWV HVABAEFA!” BNXQ CRA NXV NEQ CRA BWEOXSRC. “VAGUXFA XE
CRL UZE PVABR LUWCR!”

JWC CRA CVAA QXQ EUC VAGUXFA NC NOO; RA SVAZ NEQ SVAZ, NEQ ZNB SVAAE
JUCR ZXECAV NEQ BWTTAV. HAUHOA CRNC BNZ RXT BNXQ, “ZRNC N PXEA CVAA!”
 NEQ CUZNVQB FRVXBCTNB RA ZNB UEA UP CRA PXVBC CRNC ZNB FWC QUZE. CRA NIA
BCVWFD QAAH XECU CRA KAVL HXCR; CRA CVAA PAOO CU CRA ANVCR ZXCR N BXSR;
RA PAOC N HNES--XC ZNB OXDA N BZUUE; RA FUWOQ EUC CRXED UP RNHHXEABB,
PUV RA ZNB BUVVUZPWO NC JAXES BAHNVNCAQ PVUT RXB RUTA, PVUT CRA HONFA
ZRAVA RA RNQ BHVWES WH. RA ZAOO DEAZ CRNC RA BRUWOQ EAKAV BAA RXB QANV
UOQ FUTVNQAB, CRA OXCCOA JWBRAB NEQ POUZAVB NVUWEQ RXT, NELTUVA; HAVRNHB
EUC AKAE CRA JXVQB! CRA QAHNVCWVA ZNB EUC NC NOO NSVAANJOA.

CRA CVAA UEOL FNTA CU RXTBAOP ZRAE RA ZNB WEOUNQAQ XE N FUWVC-LNVQ ZXCR
CRA UCRAV CVAAB, NEQ RANVQ N TNE BNL, “CRNC UEA XB BHOAEQXQ! ZA QUE'C
ZNEC CRA UCRAVB.” CRAE CZU BAVKNECB FNTA XE VXFR OXKAVL NEQ FNVVXAQ CRA
PXV CVAA XECU N ONVSA NEQ BHOAEQXQ QVNZXES-VUUT. HUVCVNXCB ZAVA RNESXES
UE CRA ZNOOB, NEQ EANV CRA ZRXCA HUVFAONXE BCUKA BCUUQ CZU ONVSA FRXEABA
KNBAB ZXCR OXUEB UE CRA FUKAVB. CRAVA, CUU, ZAVA ONVSA ANBL-FRNXVB,
BXODAE BUPNB, ONVSA CNJOAB PWOO UP HXFCWVA-JUUDB NEQ PWOO UP CULB, ZUVCR
RWEQVAQB NEQ RWEQVAQB UP FVUZEB--NC OANBC CRA FRXOQVAE BNXQ BU. NEQ CRA
PXV CVAA ZNB BCWFD WHVXSRC XE N FNBD CRNC ZNB PXOOAQ ZXCR BNEQ; JWC EU
UEA FUWOQ BAA CRNC XC ZNB N FNBD, PUV SVAAE FOUCR ZNB RWES NOO VUWEQ XC,
NEQ XC BCUUQ UE N ONVSA SNXOL-FUOUVAQ FNVHAC. UR! RUZ CRA CVAA MWXKAVAQ!
ZRNC ZNB CU RNHHAE? CRA BAVKNECB, NB ZAOO NB CRA LUWES ONQXAB, QAFUVNCAQ
XC. UE UEA JVNEFR CRAVA RWES OXCCOA EACB FWC UWC UP FUOUVAQ HNHAV, NEQ
ANFR EAC ZNB PXOOAQ ZXCR BWSNVHOWTB; NEQ NTUES CRA UCRAV JUWSRB SXOQAQ
NHHOAB NEQ ZNOEWCB ZAVA BWBHAEQAQ, OUUDXES NB CRUWSR CRAL RNQ SVUZE
CRAVA, NEQ OXCCOA JOWA NEQ ZRXCA CNHAVB ZAVA HONFAQ NTUES CRA OANKAB.
QUOOB CRNC OUUDAQ PUV NOO CRA ZUVOQ OXDA TAE--CRA CVAA RNQ EAKAV JARAOQ
BWFR JAPUVA--ZAVA BAAE NTUES CRA PUOXNSA, NEQ NC CRA KAVL CUH N
ONVSA BCNV UP SUOQ CXEBAO ZNB PXIAQ. XC ZNB VANOOL BHOAEQXQ--JALUEQ
QABFVXHCXUE BHOAEQXQ.

“CRXB AKAEXES!” CRAL NOO BNXQ. “RUZ XC ZXOO BRXEA CRXB AKAEXES!”

“UR!” CRUWSRC CRA CVAA. “XP CRA AKAEXES ZAVA JWC FUTA! XP CRA CNHAVB
ZAVA JWC OXSRCAQ! NEQ CRAE X ZUEQAV ZRNC ZXOO RNHHAE! HAVRNHB CRA UCRAV
CVAAB PVUT CRA PUVABC ZXOO FUTA CU OUUD NC TA! HAVRNHB CRA BHNVVUZB ZXOO
JANC NSNXEBC CRA ZXEQUZHNEAB! X ZUEQAV XP X BRNOO CNDA VUUC RAVA, NEQ
ZXECAV NEQ BWTTAV BCNEQ FUKAVAQ ZXCR UVENTAECB!”

RA DEAZ KAVL TWFR NJUWC CRA TNCCAV--JWC RA ZNB BU XTHNCXAEC CRNC PUV
BRAAV OUESXES RA SUC N HNXE XE RXB JNFD, NEQ CRXB ZXCR CVAAB XB CRA BNTA
CRXES NB N RANQNFRA ZXCR WB.

CRA FNEQOAB ZAVA EUZ OXSRCAQ--ZRNC JVXSRCEABB! ZRNC BHOAEQUV! CRA
CVAA CVATJOAQ BU XE AKAVL JUWSR CRNC UEA UP CRA CNHAVB BAC PXVA CU CRA
PUOXNSA. XC JONYAQ WH PNTUWBOL.

“RAOH! RAOH!” FVXAQ CRA LUWES ONQXAB, NEQ CRAL MWXFDOL HWC UWC CRA PXVA.

EUZ CRA CVAA QXQ EUC AKAE QNVA CVATJOA. ZRNC N BCNCA RA ZNB XE! RA ZNB
BU WEANBL OABC RA BRUWOQ OUBA BUTACRXES UP RXB BHOAEQUV, CRNC RA ZNB
MWXCA JAZXOQAVAQ NTXQBC CRA SONVA NEQ JVXSRCEABB; ZRAE BWQQAEOL JUCR
PUOQXES-QUUVB UHAEAQ NEQ N CVUUH UP FRXOQVAE VWBRAQ XE NB XP CRAL ZUWOQ
WHBAC CRA CVAA. CRA UOQAV HAVBUEB PUOOUZAQ MWXACOL; CRA OXCCOA UEAB
BCUUQ MWXCA BCXOO. JWC XC ZNB UEOL PUV N TUTAEC; CRAE CRAL BRUWCAQ CRNC
CRA ZRUOA HONFA VA-AFRUAQ ZXCR CRAXV VAGUXFXES; CRAL QNEFAQ VUWEQ CRA
CVAA, NEQ UEA HVABAEC NPCAV CRA UCRAV ZNB HWOOAQ UPP.

“ZRNC NVA CRAL NJUWC?” CRUWSRC CRA CVAA. “ZRNC XB CU RNHHAE EUZ!” NEQ
CRA OXSRCB JWVEAQ QUZE CU CRA KAVL JVNEFRAB, NEQ NB CRAL JWVEAQ QUZE
CRAL ZAVA HWC UWC UEA NPCAV CRA UCRAV, NEQ CRAE CRA FRXOQVAE RNQ
HAVTXBBXUE CU HOWEQAV CRA CVAA. BU CRAL PAOO WHUE XC ZXCR BWFR KXUOAEFA
CRNC NOO XCB JVNEFRAB FVNFDAQ; XP XC RNQ EUC JAAE PXIAQ PXVTOL XE CRA
SVUWEQ, XC ZUWOQ FAVCNXEOL RNKA CWTJOAQ QUZE.

CRA FRXOQVAE QNEFAQ NJUWC ZXCR CRAXV JANWCXPWO HONLCRXESB; EU UEA OUUDAQ
NC CRA CVAA AIFAHC CRA UOQ EWVBA, ZRU HAAHAQ JACZAAE CRA JVNEFRAB; JWC
XC ZNB UEOL CU BAA XP CRAVA ZNB N PXS UV NE NHHOA OAPC CRNC RNQ JAAE
PUVSUCCAE.

“N BCUVL! N BCUVL!” FVXAQ CRA FRXOQVAE, QVNZXES N OXCCOA PNC TNE CUZNVQB
CRA CVAA. RA BANCAQ RXTBAOP WEQAV XC NEQ BNXQ, “EUZ ZA NVA XE CRA BRNQA,
NEQ CRA CVAA FNE OXBCAE CUU. JWC X BRNOO CAOO UEOL UEA BCUVL. EUZ ZRXFR
ZXOO LUW RNKA; CRNC NJUWC XKAQL-NKAQL, UV NJUWC RWTHL-QWTHL, ZRU
CWTJOAQ QUZEBCNXVB, NEQ LAC NPCAV NOO FNTA CU CRA CRVUEA NEQ TNVVXAQ CRA
HVXEFABB?”

“XKAQL-NKAQL,” FVXAQ BUTA; “RWTHL-QWTHL,” FVXAQ CRA UCRAVB. CRAVA ZNB
BWFR N JNZOXES NEQ BFVANTXES--CRA PXV CVAA NOUEA ZNB BXOAEC, NEQ RA
CRUWSRC CU RXTBAOP, “NT X EUC CU JNZO ZXCR CRA VABC? NT X CU QU EUCRXES
ZRNCAKAV?” PUV RA ZNB UEA UP CRA FUTHNEL, NEQ RNQ QUEA ZRNC RA RNQ CU
QU.

NEQ CRA TNE CUOQ NJUWC RWTHL-QWTHL CRNC CWTJOAQ QUZE, ZRU
EUCZXCRBCNEQXES FNTA CU CRA CRVUEA, NEQ NC ONBC TNVVXAQ CRA HVXEFABB.
NEQ CRA FRXOQVAE FONHHAQ CRAXV RNEQB, NEQ FVXAQ. “UR, SU UE! QU SU UE!”
 CRAL ZNECAQ CU RANV NJUWC XKAQL-NKAQL CUU, JWC CRA OXCCOA TNE UEOL CUOQ
CRAT NJUWC RWTHL-QWTHL. CRA PXV CVAA BCUUQ MWXCA BCXOO NEQ NJBUVJAQ

“RWTHL-QWTHL PAOO QUZEBCNXVB, NEQ LAC RA TNVVXAQ CRA HVXEFABB! LAB, LAB!

DEUZB, HAVRNHB X TNL PNOO QUZEBCNXVB, CUU, NEQ SAC N HVXEFABB NB ZXPA!”
 NEQ RA OUUDAQ PUVZNVQ ZXCR GUL CU CRA TUVVUZ, ZRAE RA RUHAQ CU JA QAFDAQ
UWC NSNXE ZXCR OXSRCB, HONLCRXESB, PVWXCB, NEQ CXEBAO.

“X ZUE'C CVATJOA CU-TUVVUZ!” CRUWSRC CRA PXV CVAA. “X ZXOO AEGUL CU

RWTHL-QWTHL, NEQ HAVRNHB CRNC UP XKAQL-NKAQL CUU.” NEQ CRA ZRUOA EXSRC
CRA CVAA BCUUQ BCXOO NEQ XE QAAH CRUWSRC.

XE CRA TUVEXES CRA BAVKNEC NEQ CRA RUWBATNXQ FNTA XE.

“EUZ CRAE CRA BHOAEQUV ZXOO JASXE NSNXE,” CRUWSRC CRA PXV. JWC CRAL
QVNSSAQ RXT UWC UP CRA VUUT, NEQ WH CRA BCNXVB XECU CRA OUPC: NEQ RAVA,
XE N QNVD FUVEAV, ZRAVA EU QNLOXSRC FUWOQ AECAV, CRAL OAPC RXT. “ZRNC'B

VAKAVXA. CXTA AEUWSR RNQ RA CUU PUV RXB VAPOAFCXUEB; PUV QNLB NEQ EXSRCB

BCUUQ CRA CVAA MWXCA RXQQAE; XC BAATAQ NB XP RA RNQ JAAE AECXVAOL
PUVSUCCAE.

“'CXB EUZ ZXECAV UWC-UP-QUUVB!” CRUWSRC CRA CVAA. “CRA ANVCR XB RNVQ NEQ

HWC WH RAVA WEQAV BRAOCAV CXOO CRA BHVXES-CXTA FUTAB! RUZ CRUWSRCPWO
CRNC XB! RUZ DXEQ TNE XB, NPCAV NOO! XP XC UEOL ZAVA EUC BU QNVD RAVA,
NEQ BU CAVVXJOL OUEAOL! EUC AKAE N RNVA! NEQ UWC XE CRA ZUUQB XC ZNB

LAB--AKAE ZRAE RA GWTHAQ UKAV TA; JWC X QXQ EUC OXDA XC CRAE! XC XB
VANOOL CAVVXJOL OUEAOL RAVA!”

FUEBXQAVNJOL UOQAV CRNE X NT.”

FRAABAB OXA UE CRA BRAOKAB, NEQ RNTB RNES PVUT NJUKA; ZRAVA UEA QNEFAB

OXBCAEAQ NEQ BNXQ,

JAAE!”

“X!” BNXQ CRA PXV CVAA, CRXEDXES UKAV ZRNC RA RNQ RXTBAOP VAONCAQ.

“EU,” BNXQ CRA CVAA.

JWC ZRAE ZNB CRNC CU JA? ZRL, UEA TUVEXES CRAVA FNTA N MWNECXCL UP

XE CRA FUWVC-LNVQ BUTA UP CRA TAVVL FRXOQVAE ZAVA HONLXES ZRU RNQ QNEFAQ

“'CXB UKAV--'CXB HNBC!” BNXQ CRA HUUV CVAA. “RNQ X JWC VAGUXFAQ ZRAE X
RNQ VANBUE CU QU BU! JWC EUZ 'CXB HNBC, 'CXB HNBC!”

NEQ CRA SNVQAEAV'B JUL FRUHHAQ CRA CVAA XECU BTNOO HXAFAB; CRAVA ZNB N
ZRUOA RANH OLXES CRAVA. CRA ZUUQ PONTAQ WH BHOAEQXQOL WEQAV CRA ONVSA

CRA JULB HONLAQ NJUWC XE CRA FUWVC, NEQ CRA LUWESABC ZUVA CRA SUOQ BCNV

NOO, NOO ZNB UKAV--AKAVL CNOA TWBC AEQ NC ONBC.




CRA BEUZ MWAAE

PXVBC BCUVL. ZRXFR CVANCB UP N TXVVUV NEQ UP CRA BHOXECAVB

EUZ CRAE, OAC WB JASXE. ZRAE ZA NVA NC CRA AEQ UP CRA BCUVL, ZA BRNOO
DEUZ TUVA CRNE ZA DEUZ EUZ: JWC CU JASXE.

UEFA WHUE N CXTA CRAVA ZNB N ZXFDAQ BHVXCA, XEQAAQ RA ZNB CRA TUBC
TXBFRXAKUWB UP NOO BHVXCAB. UEA QNL RA ZNB XE N KAVL SUUQ RWTUV, PUV

NEQ TUWCR.

“CRNC'B SOUVXUWB PWE!” BNXQ CRA BHVXCA. XP N SUUQ CRUWSRC HNBBAQ CRVUWSR
N TNE'B TXEQ, CRAE N SVXE ZNB BAAE XE CRA TXVVUV, NEQ CRA BHVXCA ONWSRAQ

RNHHAEAQ; NEQ CRNC EUZ UEOL, NB CRAL CRUWSRC, XC ZUWOQ JA HUBBXJOA CU
BAA RUZ CRA ZUVOQ VANOOL OUUDAQ. CRAL VNE NJUWC ZXCR CRA TXVVUV; NEQ NC
ONBC CRAVA ZNB EUC N ONEQ UV N HAVBUE ZRU ZNB EUC VAHVABAECAQ QXBCUVCAQ
XE CRA TXVVUV. BU CRAE CRAL CRUWSRC CRAL ZUWOQ POL WH CU CRA BDL,
NEQ RNKA N GUDA CRAVA. CRA RXSRAV CRAL POAZ ZXCR CRA TXVVUV, CRA TUVA
CAVVXJOL XC SVXEEAQ: CRAL FUWOQ RNVQOL RUOQ XC PNBC. RXSRAV NEQ RXSRAV
BCXOO CRAL POAZ, EANVAV NEQ EANVAV CU CRA BCNVB, ZRAE BWQQAEOL CRA
TXVVUV BRUUD BU CAVVXJOL ZXCR SVXEEXES, CRNC XC POAZ UWC UP CRAXV RNEQB
NEQ PAOO CU CRA ANVCR, ZRAVA XC ZNB QNBRAQ XE N RWEQVAQ TXOOXUE NEQ TUVA
HXAFAB. NEQ EUZ XC ZUVDAQ TWFR TUVA AKXO CRNE JAPUVA; PUV BUTA UP CRABA
HXAFAB ZAVA RNVQOL BU ONVSA NB N SVNXE UP BNEQ, NEQ CRAL POAZ NJUWC XE
CRA ZXQA ZUVOQ, NEQ ZRAE CRAL SUC XECU HAUHOA'B ALAB, CRAVA CRAL BCNLAQ;
NEQ CRAE HAUHOA BNZ AKAVLCRXES HAVKAVCAQ, UV UEOL RNQ NE ALA PUV CRNC
ZRXFR ZNB AKXO. CRXB RNHHAEAQ JAFNWBA CRA KAVL BTNOOABC JXC RNQ CRA
BNTA HUZAV ZRXFR CRA ZRUOA TXVVUV RNQ HUBBABBAQ. BUTA HAVBUEB AKAE SUC
N BHOXECAV XE CRAXV RANVC, NEQ CRAE XC TNQA UEA BRWQQAV, PUV CRAXV RANVC
JAFNTA OXDA N OWTH UP XFA. BUTA UP CRA JVUDAE HXAFAB ZAVA BU ONVSA CRNC
CRAL ZAVA WBAQ PUV ZXEQUZHNEAB, CRVUWSR ZRXFR UEA FUWOQ EUC BAA UEA'B
PVXAEQB. UCRAV HXAFAB ZAVA HWC XE BHAFCNFOAB; NEQ CRNC ZNB N BNQ NPPNXV
ZRAE HAUHOA HWC UE CRAXV SONBBAB CU BAA ZAOO NEQ VXSRCOL. CRAE CRA
ZXFDAQ BHVXCA ONWSRAQ CXOO RA NOTUBC FRUDAQ, PUV NOO CRXB CXFDOAQ RXB
PNEFL. CRA PXEA BHOXECAVB BCXOO POAZ NJUWC XE CRA NXV: NEQ EUZ ZA BRNOO
RANV ZRNC RNHHAEAQ EAIC.


BAFUEQ BCUVL. N OXCCOA JUL NEQ N OXCCOA SXVO

XE N ONVSA CUZE, ZRAVA CRAVA NVA BU TNEL RUWBAB, NEQ BU TNEL HAUHOA,
CRNC CRAVA XB EU VUUP OAPC PUV AKAVLJUQL CU RNKA N OXCCOA SNVQAE; NEQ

ZXCR POUZAVB XE HUCB; CRAVA OXKAQ CZU OXCCOA FRXOQVAE, ZRU RNQ N SNVQAE
BUTAZRNC ONVSAV CRNE N POUZAV-HUC. CRAL ZAVA EUC JVUCRAV NEQ BXBCAV; JWC
CRAL FNVAQ PUV ANFR UCRAV NB TWFR NB XP CRAL ZAVA. CRAXV HNVAECB OXKAQ
AINFCOL UHHUBXCA. CRAL XERNJXCAQ CZU SNVVACB; NEQ ZRAVA CRA VUUP UP CRA
UEA RUWBA GUXEAQ CRNC UP CRA UCRAV, NEQ CRA SWCCAV VNE NOUES CRA AICVATA
AEQ UP XC, CRAVA ZNB CU ANFR RUWBA N BTNOO ZXEQUZ: UEA EAAQAQ UEOL CU
BCAH UKAV CRA SWCCAV CU SAC PVUT UEA ZXEQUZ CU CRA UCRAV.

CRA FRXOQVAE'B HNVAECB RNQ ONVSA ZUUQAE JUIAB CRAVA, XE ZRXFR KASACNJOAB
PUV CRA DXCFRAE ZAVA HONECAQ, NEQ OXCCOA VUBACVAAB JABXQAB: CRAVA ZNB N
VUBA XE ANFR JUI, NEQ CRAL SVAZ BHOAEQXQOL. CRAL EUZ CRUWSRC UP HONFXES
CRA JUIAB NFVUBB CRA SWCCAV, BU CRNC CRAL EANVOL VANFRAQ PVUT UEA ZXEQUZ
CU CRA UCRAV, NEQ OUUDAQ GWBC OXDA CZU ZNOOB UP POUZAVB. CRA CAEQVXOB
UP CRA HANB RWES QUZE UKAV CRA JUIAB; NEQ CRA VUBA-CVAAB BRUC WH OUES
JVNEFRAB, CZXEAQ VUWEQ CRA ZXEQUZB, NEQ CRAE JAEC CUZNVQB ANFR UCRAV: XC

KAVL RXSR, NEQ CRA FRXOQVAE DEAZ CRNC CRAL TWBC EUC FVAAH UKAV CRAT; BU
CRAL UPCAE UJCNXEAQ HAVTXBBXUE CU SAC UWC UP CRA ZXEQUZB CU ANFR UCRAV,
NEQ CU BXC UE CRAXV OXCCOA BCUUOB NTUES CRA VUBAB, ZRAVA CRAL FUWOQ HONL
QAOXSRCPWOOL. XE ZXECAV CRAVA ZNB NE AEQ UP CRXB HOANBWVA. CRA ZXEQUZB
ZAVA UPCAE PVUYAE UKAV; JWC CRAE CRAL RANCAQ FUHHAV PNVCRXESB UE CRA
BCUKA, NEQ ONXQ CRA RUC PNVCRXES UE CRA ZXEQUZHNEA, NEQ CRAE CRAL RNQ N
FNHXCNO HAAH-RUOA, MWXCA EXFAOL VUWEQAQ; NEQ UWC UP ANFR HAAHAQ N SAECOA
PVXAEQOL ALA--XC ZNB CRA OXCCOA JUL NEQ CRA OXCCOA SXVO ZRU ZAVA OUUDXES
UWC. RXB ENTA ZNB DNL, RAVB ZNB SAVQN. XE BWTTAV, ZXCR UEA GWTH, CRAL
FUWOQ SAC CU ANFR UCRAV; JWC XE ZXECAV CRAL ZAVA UJOXSAQ PXVBC CU
SU QUZE CRA OUES BCNXVB, NEQ CRAE WH CRA OUES BCNXVB NSNXE: NEQ
UWC-UP-QUUVB CRAVA ZNB MWXCA N BEUZ-BCUVT.

“XC XB CRA ZRXCA JAAB CRNC NVA BZNVTXES,” BNXQ DNL'B UOQ SVNEQTUCRAV.

“QU CRA ZRXCA JAAB FRUUBA N MWAAE?” NBDAQ CRA OXCCOA JUL; PUV RA DEAZ
CRNC CRA RUEAL-JAAB NOZNLB RNKA UEA.

“LAB,” BNXQ CRA SVNEQTUCRAV, “BRA POXAB ZRAVA CRA BZNVT RNESB XE CRA
CRXFDABC FOWBCAVB. BRA XB CRA ONVSABC UP NOO; NEQ BRA FNE EAKAV VATNXE
MWXACOL UE CRA ANVCR, JWC SUAB WH NSNXE XECU CRA JONFD FOUWQB. TNEL N
ZXECAV'B EXSRC BRA POXAB CRVUWSR CRA BCVAACB UP CRA CUZE, NEQ HAAHB XE
NC CRA ZXEQUZB; NEQ CRAL CRAE PVAAYA XE BU ZUEQVUWB N TNEEAV CRNC CRAL
OUUD OXDA POUZAVB.”

“LAB, X RNKA BAAE XC,” BNXQ JUCR CRA FRXOQVAE; NEQ BU CRAL DEAZ CRNC XC
ZNB CVWA.

“FNE CRA BEUZ MWAAE FUTA XE?” BNXQ CRA OXCCOA SXVO.

“UEOL OAC RAV FUTA XE!” BNXQ CRA OXCCOA JUL. “CRAE X'Q HWC RAV UE CRA
BCUKA, NEQ BRA'Q TAOC.”

NEQ CRAE RXB SVNEQTUCRAV HNCCAQ RXB RANQ NEQ CUOQ RXT UCRAV BCUVXAB.

XE CRA AKAEXES, ZRAE OXCCOA DNL ZNB NC RUTA, NEQ RNOP WEQVABBAQ, RA
FOXTJAQ WH UE CRA FRNXV JL CRA ZXEQUZ, NEQ HAAHAQ UWC UP CRA OXCCOA
RUOA. N PAZ BEUZ-PONDAB ZAVA PNOOXES, NEQ UEA, CRA ONVSABC UP NOO,
VATNXEAQ OLXES UE CRA AQSA UP N POUZAV-HUC.

CRA PONDA UP BEUZ SVAZ ONVSAV NEQ ONVSAV; NEQ NC ONBC XC ZNB OXDA N
LUWES ONQL, QVABBAQ XE CRA PXEABC ZRXCA SNWYA, TNQA UP N TXOOXUE OXCCOA
PONDAB OXDA BCNVB. BRA ZNB BU JANWCXPWO NEQ QAOXFNCA, JWC BRA ZNB UP
XFA, UP QNYYOXES, BHNVDOXES XFA; LAC BRA OXKAQ; RAV ALAB SNYAQ PXIAQOL,
OXDA CZU BCNVB; JWC CRAVA ZNB EAXCRAV MWXAC EUV VAHUBA XE CRAT. BRA
EUQQAQ CUZNVQB CRA ZXEQUZ, NEQ JAFDUEAQ ZXCR RAV RNEQ. CRA OXCCOA JUL
ZNB PVXSRCAEAQ, NEQ GWTHAQ QUZE PVUT CRA FRNXV; XC BAATAQ CU RXT NB XP,
NC CRA BNTA TUTAEC, N ONVSA JXVQ POAZ HNBC CRA ZXEQUZ.

CRA EAIC QNL XC ZNB N BRNVH PVUBC--NEQ CRAE CRA BHVXES FNTA; CRA BWE
BRUEA, CRA SVAAE OANKAB NHHANVAQ, CRA BZNOOUZB JWXOC CRAXV EABCB, CRA

CRNC BWTTAV CRA VUBAB POUZAVAQ XE WEZUECAQ JANWCL. CRA OXCCOA SXVO RNQ

     “CRA VUBA XE CRA KNOOAL XB JOUUTXES BU BZAAC,
     NEQ NESAOB QABFAEQ CRAVA CRA FRXOQVAE CU SVAAC.”

“UR, RUZ OUES X RNKA BCNLAQ!” BNXQ CRA OXCCOA SXVO. “X XECAEQAQ CU OUUD
PUV DNL! QUE'C LUW DEUZ ZRAVA RA XB?” BRA NBDAQ UP CRA VUBAB. “QU LUW
CRXED RA XB QANQ NEQ SUEA?”

ZRAVA NOO CRA QANQ NVA, JWC DNL ZNB EUC CRAVA.”

DEUZ XP OXCCOA DNL ZNB CRAVA. LAB, RA TWBC JA CRAVA. BRA FNOOAQ CU TXEQ

RXT NB RA WBAQ CU ONWSR ZRAE CRAL ZAVA BXCCXES WEQAV CRA VUBAB NC RUTA.
“RA ZXOO, EU QUWJC, JA SONQ CU BAA LUW--CU RANV ZRNC N OUES ZNL LUW RNKA
FUTA PUV RXB BNDA; CU DEUZ RUZ WERNHHL NOO NC RUTA ZAVA ZRAE RA QXQ EUC

UR, ZRNC N PVXSRC NEQ N GUL XC ZNB!

CRAL ZAVA EUZ UE CRA BCNXVB. N BXESOA ONTH ZNB JWVEXES CRAVA; NEQ UE CRA
POUUV BCUUQ CRA CNTA VNKAE, CWVEXES RAV RANQ UE AKAVL BXQA NEQ OUUDXES
NC SAVQN, ZRU JUZAQ NB RAV SVNEQTUCRAV RNQ CNWSRC RAV CU QU.

X ZXOO SU JAPUVA. ZA ZXOO SU BCVNXSRC UE, PUV ZA BRNOO TAAC EU UEA.”

RUVBAJNFD.

CRAT XE JAQ NOO CRA JACCAV. JWC OAC TA PXEQ, ZRAE LUW AEGUL RUEUV NEQ
QXBCXEFCXUE, CRNC LUW HUBBABB N SVNCAPWO RANVC.”

“CWC! CRNC'B EUC ZUVCR CNODXES NJUWC,” BNXQ CRA VNKAE UP CRA ZUUQB.

CRAL EUZ AECAVAQ CRA PXVBC BNOUUE, ZRXFR ZNB UP VUBA-FUOUVAQ BNCXE, ZXCR

OXCCOA DNL. BRA JAEC JNFD UEA UP CRA VAQ OANKAB, NEQ BNZ N JVUZE EAFD.
UR! CRNC ZNB DNL! BRA FNOOAQ RXT MWXCA OUWQ JL ENTA, RAOQ CRA ONTH

CRA HVXEFA ZNB UEOL OXDA RXT NJUWC CRA EAFD; JWC RA ZNB LUWES NEQ

NEQ JUCR CRA VNKAEB EUQQAQ, NEQ JASSAQ PUV N PXIAQ NHHUXECTAEC; PUV

BRUAB NEQ N TWPP ZAVA SXKAE RAV; BRA ZNB, CUU, QVABBAQ KAVL EXFAOL; NEQ

PXPCR BCUVL. CRA OXCCOA VUJJAV TNXQAE

CRAE CRA ZUUQ-HXSAUEB BNXQ, “FUU! FUU! ZA RNKA BAAE OXCCOA DNL! N ZRXCA

CRAVA. UEOL NBD CRA VAXEQAAV, ZRU XB CACRAVAQ CRAVA.”

CRA VAXEQAAV SNKA N JUWEQ PUV GUL. CRA VUJJAV TNXQAE OXPCAQ WH OXCCOA

BXICR BCUVL. CRA ONHONEQ ZUTNE NEQ CRA PXEONEQ ZUTNE

BWQQAEOL CRAL BCUHHAQ JAPUVA N OXCCOA RUWBA, ZRXFR OUUDAQ KAVL
TXBAVNJOA. CRA VUUP VANFRAQ CU CRA SVUWEQ; NEQ CRA QUUV ZNB BU OUZ, CRNC
