UP SAVQN'B RXBCUVL, JWC PXVBC UP NOO RXB UZE; PUV CRNC BAATAQ CU RXT UP
TWFR SVANCAV XTHUVCNEFA. SAVQN ZNB BU FRXOOAQ CRNC BRA FUWOQ EUC BHAND.

“HUUV CRXES,” BNXQ CRA ONHONEQ ZUTNE, “LUW RNKA PNV CU VWE BCXOO. LUW
RNKA TUVA CRNE N RWEQVAQ TXOAB CU SU JAPUVA LUW SAC CU PXEONEQ; CRAVA
CRA BEUZ MWAAE RNB RAV FUWECVL-RUWBA, NEQ JWVEB JOWA OXSRCB AKAVL
AKAEXES. X ZXOO SXKA LUW N PAZ ZUVQB PVUT TA, ZRXFR X ZXOO ZVXCA UE N
QVXAQ RNJAVQXEA, PUV HNHAV X RNKA EUEA; CRXB LUW FNE CNDA ZXCR LUW CU
CRA PXEONEQ ZUTNE, NEQ BRA ZXOO JA NJOA CU SXKA LUW TUVA XEPUVTNCXUE
CRNE X FNE.”

ZRAE SAVQN RNQ ZNVTAQ RAVBAOP, NEQ RNQ ANCAE NEQ QVWED, CRA ONHONEQ
ZUTNE ZVUCA N PAZ ZUVQB UE N QVXAQ RNJAVQXEA, JASSAQ SAVQN CU CNDA FNVA
UP CRAT, HWC RAV UE CRA VAXEQAAV, JUWEQ RAV PNBC, NEQ NZNL BHVNES CRA
NEXTNO. “QQBN! QQBN!” ZNB NSNXE RANVQ XE CRA NXV; CRA TUBC FRNVTXES
JOWA OXSRCB JWVEAQ CRA ZRUOA EXSRC XE CRA BDL, NEQ NC ONBC CRAL FNTA CU
PXEONEQ. CRAL DEUFDAQ NC CRA FRXTEAL UP CRA PXEONEQ ZUTNE; PUV NB CU N
QUUV, BRA RNQ EUEA.

CRAVA ZNB BWFR N RANC XEBXQA CRNC CRA PXEONEQ ZUTNE RAVBAOP ZAEC NJUWC
NOTUBC ENDAQ. BRA ZNB QXTXEWCXKA NEQ QXVCL. BRA XTTAQXNCAOL OUUBAEAQ
OXCCOA SAVQN'B FOUCRAB, HWOOAQ UPP RAV CRXFD SOUKAB NEQ JUUCB; PUV
UCRAVZXBA CRA RANC ZUWOQ RNKA JAAE CUU SVANC--NEQ NPCAV ONLXES N HXAFA
UP XFA UE CRA VAXEQAAV'B RANQ, VANQ ZRNC ZNB ZVXCCAE UE CRA PXBR-BDXE.
BRA VANQ XC CRVAA CXTAB: BRA CRAE DEAZ XC JL RANVC; BU BRA HWC CRA PXBR
XECU CRA FWHJUNVQ--PUV XC TXSRC KAVL ZAOO JA ANCAE, NEQ BRA EAKAV CRVAZ
NELCRXES NZNL.

CRAE CRA VAXEQAAV VAONCAQ RXB UZE BCUVL PXVBC, NEQ NPCAVZNVQB CRNC UP
OXCCOA SAVQN; NEQ CRA PXEONEQ ZUTNE ZXEDAQ RAV ALAB, JWC BNXQ EUCRXES.

“LUW NVA BU FOAKAV,” BNXQ CRA VAXEQAAV; “LUW FNE, X DEUZ, CZXBC NOO CRA
ZXEQB UP CRA ZUVOQ CUSACRAV XE N DEUC. XP CRA BANTNE OUUBAEB UEA DEUC,
CRAE RA RNB N SUUQ ZXEQ; XP N BAFUEQ, CRAE XC JOUZB HVACCL BCXPPOL; XP
RA WEQUAB CRA CRXVQ NEQ PUWVCR, CRAE XC VNSAB BU CRNC CRA PUVABCB NVA
WHCWVEAQ. ZXOO LUW SXKA CRA OXCCOA TNXQAE N HUCXUE, CRNC BRA TNL HUBBABB
CRA BCVAESCR UP CZAOKA TAE, NEQ KNEMWXBR CRA BEUZ MWAAE?”

“CRA BCVAESCR UP CZAOKA TAE!” BNXQ CRA PXEONEQ ZUTNE. “TWFR SUUQ CRNC
ZUWOQ JA!” CRAE BRA ZAEC CU N FWHJUNVQ, NEQ QVAZ UWC N ONVSA BDXE VUOOAQ
WH. ZRAE BRA RNQ WEVUOOAQ XC, BCVNESA FRNVNFCAVB ZAVA CU JA BAAE ZVXCCAE
CRAVAUE; NEQ CRA PXEONEQ ZUTNE VANQ NC BWFR N VNCA CRNC CRA HAVBHXVNCXUE
CVXFDOAQ QUZE RAV PUVARANQ.

JWC CRA VAXEQAAV JASSAQ BU RNVQ PUV OXCCOA SAVQN, NEQ SAVQN OUUDAQ BU
XTHOUVXESOL ZXCR CANVPWO ALAB NC CRA PXEONEQ ZUTNE, CRNC BRA ZXEDAQ, NEQ
QVAZ CRA VAXEQAAV NBXQA XECU N FUVEAV, ZRAVA CRAL ZRXBHAVAQ CUSACRAV,
ZRXOA CRA NEXTNO SUC BUTA PVABR XFA HWC UE RXB RANQ.

“'CXB CVWA OXCCOA DNL XB NC CRA BEUZ MWAAE'B, NEQ PXEQB AKAVLCRXES CRAVA
MWXCA CU RXB CNBCA; NEQ RA CRXEDB XC CRA KAVL JABC HONFA XE CRA ZUVOQ;
JWC CRA VANBUE UP CRNC XB, RA RNB N BHOXECAV UP SONBB XE RXB ALA, NEQ XE
RXB RANVC. CRABA TWBC JA SUC UWC PXVBC; UCRAVZXBA RA ZXOO EAKAV SU JNFD
CU TNEDXEQ, NEQ CRA BEUZ MWAAE ZXOO VACNXE RAV HUZAV UKAV RXT.”

“JWC FNE LUW SXKA OXCCOA SAVQN EUCRXES CU CNDA ZRXFR ZXOO AEQWA RAV ZXCR
HUZAV UKAV CRA ZRUOA?”

“X FNE SXKA RAV EU TUVA HUZAV CRNE ZRNC BRA RNB NOVANQL. QUE'C LUW BAA
RUZ SVANC XC XB? QUE'C LUW BAA RUZ TAE NEQ NEXTNOB NVA PUVFAQ CU BAVKA
RAV; RUZ ZAOO BRA SACB CRVUWSR CRA ZUVOQ JNVAPUUCAQ? BRA TWBC EUC RANV
UP RAV HUZAV PVUT WB; CRNC HUZAV OXAB XE RAV RANVC, JAFNWBA BRA XB
N BZAAC NEQ XEEUFAEC FRXOQ! XP BRA FNEEUC SAC CU CRA BEUZ MWAAE JL
RAVBAOP, NEQ VXQ OXCCOA DNL UP CRA SONBB, ZA FNEEUC RAOH RAV. CZU TXOAB
RAEFA CRA SNVQAE UP CRA BEUZ MWAAE JASXEB; CRXCRAV LUW TNL FNVVL CRA
OXCCOA SXVO. BAC RAV QUZE JL CRA ONVSA JWBR ZXCR VAQ JAVVXAB, BCNEQXES
XE CRA BEUZ; QUE'C BCNL CNODXES, JWC RNBCAE JNFD NB PNBC NB HUBBXJOA.”
 NEQ EUZ CRA PXEONEQ ZUTNE HONFAQ OXCCOA SAVQN UE CRA VAXEQAAV'B JNFD,
NEQ UPP RA VNE ZXCR NOO XTNSXENJOA BHAAQ.

“UR! X RNKA EUC SUC TL JUUCB! X RNKA EUC JVUWSRC TL SOUKAB!” FVXAQ
OXCCOA SAVQN. BRA VATNVDAQ BRA ZNB ZXCRUWC CRAT PVUT CRA FWCCXES PVUBC;
JWC CRA VAXEQAAV QNVAQ EUC BCNEQ BCXOO; UE RA VNE CXOO RA FNTA CU CRA
SVANC JWBR ZXCR CRA VAQ JAVVXAB, NEQ CRAVA RA BAC SAVQN QUZE, DXBBAQ RAV
TUWCR, ZRXOA ONVSA JVXSRC CANVB POUZAQ PVUT CRA NEXTNO'B ALAB, NEQ CRAE
JNFD RA ZAEC NB PNBC NB HUBBXJOA. CRAVA BCUUQ HUUV SAVQN EUZ, ZXCRUWC
BRUAB UV SOUKAB, XE CRA KAVL TXQQOA UP QVANQPWO XFL PXEONEQ.

BRA VNE UE NB PNBC NB BRA FUWOQ. CRAVA CRAE FNTA N ZRUOA VASXTAEC UP
BEUZ-PONDAB, JWC CRAL QXQ EUC PNOO PVUT NJUKA, NEQ CRAL ZAVA MWXCA
JVXSRC NEQ BRXEXES PVUT CRA NWVUVN JUVANOXB. CRA PONDAB VNE NOUES
CRA SVUWEQ, NEQ CRA EANVAV CRAL FNTA CRA ONVSAV CRAL SVAZ. SAVQN ZAOO
VATATJAVAQ RUZ ONVSA NEQ BCVNESA CRA BEUZ-PONDAB NHHANVAQ ZRAE BRA
UEFA BNZ CRAT CRVUWSR N TNSEXPLXES-SONBB; JWC EUZ CRAL ZAVA ONVSA NEQ
CAVVXPXF XE NEUCRAV TNEEAV--CRAL ZAVA NOO NOXKA. CRAL ZAVA CRA UWCHUBCB
UP CRA BEUZ MWAAE. CRAL RNQ CRA TUBC ZUEQVUWB BRNHAB; BUTA OUUDAQ OXDA
ONVSA WSOL HUVFWHXEAB; UCRAVB OXDA BENDAB DEUCCAQ CUSACRAV, ZXCR CRAXV
RANQB BCXFDXES UWC; NEQ UCRAVB, NSNXE, OXDA BTNOO PNC JANVB, ZXCR CRA
RNXV BCNEQXES UE AEQ: NOO ZAVA UP QNYYOXES ZRXCAEABB--NOO ZAVA OXKXES
BEUZ-PONDAB.

OXCCOA SAVQN VAHANCAQ CRA OUVQ'B HVNLAV. CRA FUOQ ZNB BU XECAEBA CRNC
BRA FUWOQ BAA RAV UZE JVANCR, ZRXFR FNTA OXDA BTUDA UWC UP RAV TUWCR. XC
SVAZ CRXFDAV NEQ CRXFDAV, NEQ CUUD CRA PUVT UP OXCCOA NESAOB, CRNC SVAZ
TUVA NEQ TUVA ZRAE CRAL CUWFRAQ CRA ANVCR. NOO RNQ RAOTB UE CRAXV RANQB,
NEQ ONEFAB NEQ BRXAOQB XE CRAXV RNEQB; CRAL XEFVANBAQ XE EWTJAVB; NEQ
ZRAE SAVQN RNQ PXEXBRAQ CRA OUVQ'B HVNLAV, BRA ZNB BWVVUWEQAQ JL N ZRUOA
OASXUE. CRAL CRVWBC NC CRA RUVVXQ BEUZ-PONDAB ZXCR CRAXV BHANVB, BU CRNC
CRAL POAZ XECU N CRUWBNEQ HXAFAB; NEQ OXCCOA SAVQN ZNODAQ UE JVNKAOL NEQ
XE BAFWVXCL. CRA NESAOB HNCCAQ RAV RNEQB NEQ PAAC; NEQ CRAE BRA PAOC CRA
FUOQ OABB, NEQ ZAEC UE MWXFDOL CUZNVQB CRA HNONFA UP CRA BEUZ MWAAE.

JWC EUZ ZA BRNOO BAA RUZ DNL PNVAQ. RA EAKAV CRUWSRC UP SAVQN, NEQ OANBC
UP NOO CRNC BRA ZNB BCNEQXES JAPUVA CRA HNONFA.


BAKAECR BCUVL. ZRNC CUUD HONFA XE CRA HNONFA UP CRA BEUZ MWAAE, NEQ ZRNC
RNHHAEAQ NPCAVZNVQ.

CRA ZNOOB UP CRA HNONFA ZAVA UP QVXKXES BEUZ, NEQ CRA ZXEQUZB NEQ QUUVB
UP FWCCXES ZXEQB. CRAVA ZAVA TUVA CRNE N RWEQVAQ RNOOB CRAVA, NFFUVQXES
NB CRA BEUZ ZNB QVXKAE JL CRA ZXEQB. CRA ONVSABC ZNB TNEL TXOAB XE
AICAEC; NOO ZAVA OXSRCAQ WH JL CRA HUZAVPWO NWVUVN JUVANOXB, NEQ NOO
ZAVA BU ONVSA, BU ATHCL, BU XFL FUOQ, NEQ BU VABHOAEQAEC! TXVCR EAKAV
VAXSEAQ CRAVA; CRAVA ZNB EAKAV AKAE N OXCCOA JANV-JNOO, ZXCR CRA BCUVT
PUV TWBXF, ZRXOA CRA HUONV JANVB ZAEC UE CRAXV RXEQ OASB NEQ BRUZAQ UPP
CRAXV BCAHB. EAKAV N OXCCOA CAN-HNVCL UP ZRXCA LUWES ONQL PUIAB; KNBC,
FUOQ, NEQ ATHCL ZAVA CRA RNOOB UP CRA BEUZ MWAAE. CRA EUVCRAVE-OXSRCB
BRUEA ZXCR BWFR HVAFXBXUE CRNC UEA FUWOQ CAOO AINFCOL ZRAE CRAL ZAVA
NC CRAXV RXSRABC UV OUZABC QASVAA UP JVXSRCEABB. XE CRA TXQQOA UP CRA
ATHCL, AEQOABB RNOO UP BEUZ, ZNB N PVUYAE ONDA; XC ZNB FVNFDAQ XE N
CRUWBNEQ HXAFAB, JWC ANFR HXAFA ZNB BU OXDA CRA UCRAV, CRNC XC BAATAQ
CRA ZUVD UP N FWEEXES NVCXPXFAV. XE CRA TXQQOA UP CRXB ONDA BNC CRA BEUZ
MWAAE ZRAE BRA ZNB NC RUTA; NEQ CRAE BRA BNXQ BRA ZNB BXCCXES XE CRA
TXVVUV UP WEQAVBCNEQXES, NEQ CRNC CRXB ZNB CRA UEOL UEA NEQ CRA JABC
CRXES XE CRA ZUVOQ.

OXCCOA DNL ZNB MWXCA JOWA, LAB EANVOL JONFD ZXCR FUOQ; JWC RA QXQ EUC
UJBAVKA XC, PUV BRA RNQ DXBBAQ NZNL NOO PAAOXES UP FUOQ PVUT RXB JUQL,
NEQ RXB RANVC ZNB N OWTH UP XFA. RA ZNB QVNSSXES NOUES BUTA HUXECAQ
PONC HXAFAB UP XFA, ZRXFR RA ONXQ CUSACRAV XE NOO HUBBXJOA ZNLB, PUV RA
ZNECAQ CU TNDA BUTACRXES ZXCR CRAT; GWBC NB ZA RNKA OXCCOA PONC HXAFAB
UP ZUUQ CU TNDA SAUTACVXFNO PXSWVAB ZXCR, FNOOAQ CRA FRXEABA HWYYOA.
DNL TNQA NOO BUVCB UP PXSWVAB, CRA TUBC FUTHOXFNCAQ, PUV XC ZNB
NE XFA-HWYYOA PUV CRA WEQAVBCNEQXES. XE RXB ALAB CRA PXSWVAB ZAVA
AICVNUVQXENVXOL JANWCXPWO, NEQ UP CRA WCTUBC XTHUVCNEFA; PUV CRA JXC
UP SONBB ZRXFR ZNB XE RXB ALA FNWBAQ CRXB. RA PUWEQ ZRUOA PXSWVAB ZRXFR
VAHVABAECAQ N ZVXCCAE ZUVQ; JWC RA EAKAV FUWOQ TNENSA CU VAHVABAEC GWBC
CRA ZUVQ RA ZNECAQ--CRNC ZUVQ ZNB “ACAVEXCL”; NEQ CRA BEUZ MWAAE RNQ
BNXQ, “XP LUW FNE QXBFUKAV CRNC PXSWVA, LUW BRNOO JA LUWV UZE TNBCAV,
NEQ X ZXOO TNDA LUW N HVABAEC UP CRA ZRUOA ZUVOQ NEQ N HNXV UP EAZ
BDNCAB.” JWC RA FUWOQ EUC PXEQ XC UWC.

“X NT SUXES EUZ CU ZNVT ONEQB,” BNXQ CRA BEUZ MWAAE. “X TWBC RNKA N OUUD
QUZE XECU CRA JONFD FNOQVUEB.” XC ZNB CRA KUOFNEUAB KABWKXWB NEQ ACEN
CRNC BRA TANEC. “X ZXOO GWBC SXKA CRAT N FUNCXES UP ZRXCA, PUV CRNC XB
NB XC UWSRC CU JA; JABXQAB, XC XB SUUQ PUV CRA UVNESAB NEQ CRA SVNHAB.”
 NEQ CRAE NZNL BRA POAZ, NEQ DNL BNC MWXCA NOUEA XE CRA ATHCL RNOOB UP
XFA CRNC ZAVA TXOAB OUES, NEQ OUUDAQ NC CRA JOUFDB UP XFA, NEQ CRUWSRC
NEQ CRUWSRC CXOO RXB BDWOO ZNB NOTUBC FVNFDAQ. CRAVA RA BNC MWXCA
JAEWTJAQ NEQ TUCXUEOABB; UEA ZUWOQ RNKA XTNSXEAQ RA ZNB PVUYAE CU QANCR.

BWQQAEOL OXCCOA SAVQN BCAHHAQ CRVUWSR CRA SVANC HUVCNO XECU CRA HNONFA.
CRA SNCA ZNB PUVTAQ UP FWCCXES ZXEQB; JWC SAVQN VAHANCAQ RAV AKAEXES
HVNLAV, NEQ CRA ZXEQB ZAVA ONXQ NB CRUWSR CRAL BOAHC; NEQ CRA OXCCOA
TNXQAE AECAVAQ CRA KNBC, ATHCL, FUOQ RNOOB. CRAVA BRA JARAOQ DNL: BRA
VAFUSEXBAQ RXT, POAZ CU ATJVNFA RXT, NEQ FVXAQ UWC, RAV NVTB PXVTOL
RUOQXES RXT CRA ZRXOA, “DNL, BZAAC OXCCOA DNL! RNKA X CRAE PUWEQ LUW NC
ONBC?”

JWC RA BNC MWXCA BCXOO, JAEWTJAQ NEQ FUOQ. CRAE OXCCOA SAVQN BRAQ
JWVEXES CANVB; NEQ CRAL PAOO UE RXB JUBUT, CRAL HAEACVNCAQ CU RXB
RANVC, CRAL CRNZAQ CRA OWTHB UP XFA, NEQ FUEBWTAQ CRA BHOXECAVB UP CRA
OUUDXES-SONBB; RA OUUDAQ NC RAV, NEQ BRA BNES CRA RLTE:

“CRA VUBA XE CRA KNOOAL XB JOUUTXES BU BZAAC, NEQ NESAOB QABFAEQ CRAVA
CRA FRXOQVAE CU SVAAC.”

RAVAWHUE DNL JWVBC XECU CANVB; RA ZAHC BU TWFR CRNC CRA BHOXECAV VUOOAQ
UWC UP RXB ALA, NEQ RA VAFUSEXBAQ RAV, NEQ BRUWCAQ, “SAVQN, BZAAC OXCCOA
SAVQN! ZRAVA RNKA LUW JAAE BU OUES? NEQ ZRAVA RNKA X JAAE?” RA OUUDAQ
VUWEQ RXT. “RUZ FUOQ XC XB RAVA!” BNXQ RA. “RUZ ATHCL NEQ FUOQ!” NEQ RA
RAOQ PNBC JL SAVQN, ZRU ONWSRAQ NEQ ZAHC PUV GUL. XC ZNB BU JANWCXPWO,
CRNC AKAE CRA JOUFDB UP XFA QNEFAQ NJUWC PUV GUL; NEQ ZRAE CRAL ZAVA
CXVAQ NEQ ONXQ CRATBAOKAB QUZE, CRAL PUVTAQ AINFCOL CRA OACCAVB ZRXFR
CRA BEUZ MWAAE RNQ CUOQ RXT CU PXEQ UWC; BU EUZ RA ZNB RXB UZE TNBCAV,
NEQ RA ZUWOQ RNKA CRA ZRUOA ZUVOQ NEQ N HNXV UP EAZ BDNCAB XECU CRA
JNVSNXE.

SAVQN DXBBAQ RXB FRAADB, NEQ CRAL SVAZ MWXCA JOUUTXES; BRA DXBBAQ RXB
ALAB, NEQ CRAL BRUEA OXDA RAV UZE; BRA DXBBAQ RXB RNEQB NEQ PAAC, NEQ RA
ZNB NSNXE ZAOO NEQ TAVVL. CRA BEUZ MWAAE TXSRC FUTA JNFD NB BUUE NB BRA
OXDAQ; CRAVA BCUUQ RXB QXBFRNVSA ZVXCCAE XE VABHOAEQAEC TNBBAB UP XFA.

CRAL CUUD ANFR UCRAV JL CRA RNEQ, NEQ ZNEQAVAQ PUVCR UWC UP CRA ONVSA
RNOO; CRAL CNODAQ UP CRAXV UOQ SVNEQTUCRAV, NEQ UP CRA VUBAB WHUE CRA
VUUP; NEQ ZRAVAKAV CRAL ZAEC, CRA ZXEQB FANBAQ VNSXES, NEQ CRA BWE JWVBC
PUVCR. NEQ ZRAE CRAL VANFRAQ CRA JWBR ZXCR CRA VAQ JAVVXAB, CRAL PUWEQ
CRA VAXEQAAV ZNXCXES PUV CRAT. RA RNQ JVUWSRC NEUCRAV, N LUWES UEA, ZXCR
RXT, ZRUBA WQQAV ZNB PXOOAQ ZXCR TXOD, ZRXFR RA SNKA CU CRA OXCCOA UEAB,
NEQ DXBBAQ CRAXV OXHB. CRAL CRAE FNVVXAQ DNL NEQ SAVQN--PXVBC CU CRA
PXEONEQ ZUTNE, ZRAVA CRAL ZNVTAQ CRATBAOKAB XE CRA ZNVT VUUT, NEQ
OANVEAQ ZRNC CRAL ZAVA CU QU UE CRAXV GUWVEAL RUTA; NEQ CRAL ZAEC CU
CRA ONHONEQ ZUTNE, ZRU TNQA BUTA EAZ FOUCRAB PUV CRAT NEQ VAHNXVAQ CRAXV
BOAQSAB.

CRA VAXEQAAV NEQ CRA LUWES RXEQ OANHAQ NOUES JABXQA CRAT, NEQ
NFFUTHNEXAQ CRAT CU CRA JUWEQNVL UP CRA FUWECVL. RAVA CRA PXVBC
KASACNCXUE HAAHAQ PUVCR; RAVA DNL NEQ SAVQN CUUD OANKA UP CRA ONHONEQ
ZUTNE. “PNVAZAOO! PNVAZAOO!” CRAL NOO BNXQ. NEQ CRA PXVBC SVAAE JWQB
NHHANVAQ, CRA PXVBC OXCCOA JXVQB JASNE CU FRXVVWH; NEQ UWC UP CRA ZUUQ
FNTA, VXQXES UE N TNSEXPXFAEC RUVBA, ZRXFR SAVQN DEAZ (XC ZNB UEA UP CRA
OANQAVB XE CRA SUOQAE FNVVXNSA), N LUWES QNTBAO ZXCR N JVXSRC-VAQ FNH UE
RAV RANQ, NEQ NVTAQ ZXCR HXBCUOB. XC ZNB CRA OXCCOA VUJJAV TNXQAE, ZRU,
CXVAQ UP JAXES NC RUTA, RNQ QACAVTXEAQ CU TNDA N GUWVEAL CU CRA EUVCR;
NEQ NPCAVZNVQB XE NEUCRAV QXVAFCXUE, XP CRNC QXQ EUC HOANBA RAV. BRA
VAFUSEXBAQ SAVQN XTTAQXNCAOL, NEQ SAVQN DEAZ RAV CUU. XC ZNB N GULPWO
TAACXES.

“LUW NVA N PXEA PAOOUZ PUV CVNTHXES NJUWC,” BNXQ BRA CU OXCCOA DNL; “X
BRUWOQ OXDA CU DEUZ, PNXCR, XP LUW QABAVKA CRNC UEA BRUWOQ VWE PVUT UEA
AEQ UP CRA ZUVOQ CU CRA UCRAV PUV LUWV BNDA?”

JWC SAVQN HNCCAQ RAV FRAADB, NEQ XEMWXVAQ PUV CRA HVXEFA NEQ HVXEFABB.

“CRAL NVA SUEA NJVUNQ,” BNXQ CRA UCRAV.

“JWC CRA VNKAE?” NBDAQ OXCCOA SAVQN.

“UR! CRA VNKAE XB QANQ,” BRA NEBZAVAQ. “RXB CNTA BZAACRANVC XB N
ZXQUZ, NEQ ZANVB N JXC UP JONFD ZUVBCAQ VUWEQ RAV OAS; BRA ONTAECB TUBC
HXCAUWBOL, JWC XC'B NOO TAVA CNOD NEQ BCWPP! EUZ CAOO TA ZRNC LUW'KA
JAAE QUXES NEQ RUZ LUW TNENSAQ CU FNCFR RXT.”

NEQ SAVQN NEQ DNL JUCR CUOQ CRAXV BCUVL.

NEQ “BFREXHH-BFRENHH-BFREWVVA-JNBBAOWVVA,” BNXQ CRA VUJJAV TNXQAE; NEQ
BRA CUUD CRA RNEQB UP ANFR, NEQ HVUTXBAQ CRNC XP BRA BRUWOQ BUTA QNL
HNBB CRVUWSR CRA CUZE ZRAVA CRAL OXKAQ, BRA ZUWOQ FUTA NEQ KXBXC CRAT;

OUKAOL BHVXES ZANCRAV, ZXCR NJWEQNEFA UP POUZAVB NEQ UP KAVQWVA. CRA
FRWVFR-JAOOB VNES, NEQ CRA FRXOQVAE VAFUSEXBAQ CRA RXSR CUZAVB, NEQ CRA
ONVSA CUZE; XC ZNB CRNC XE ZRXFR CRAL QZAOC. CRAL AECAVAQ NEQ RNBCAEAQ
WH CU CRAXV SVNEQTUCRAV'B VUUT, ZRAVA AKAVLCRXES ZNB BCNEQXES NB
PUVTAVOL. CRA FOUFD BNXQ “CXFD! CNFD!” NEQ CRA PXESAV TUKAQ VUWEQ; JWC
NB CRAL AECAVAQ, CRAL VATNVDAQ CRNC CRAL ZAVA EUZ SVUZE WH. CRA VUBAB
UE CRA OANQB RWES JOUUTXES XE NC CRA UHAE ZXEQUZ; CRAVA BCUUQ CRA OXCCOA
FRXOQVAE'B FRNXVB, NEQ DNL NEQ SAVQN BNC QUZE UE CRAT, RUOQXES ANFR
UCRAV JL CRA RNEQ; CRAL JUCR RNQ PUVSUCCAE CRA FUOQ ATHCL BHOAEQUV UP
CRA BEUZ MWAAE, NB CRUWSR XC RNQ JAAE N QVANT. CRA SVNEQTUCRAV BNC XE
CRA JVXSRC BWEBRXEA, NEQ VANQ NOUWQ PVUT CRA JXJOA: “WEOABB LA JAFUTA NB
OXCCOA FRXOQVAE, LA FNEEUC AECAV CRA DXESQUT UP RANKAE.”

NEQ DNL NEQ SAVQN OUUDAQ XE ANFR UCRAV'B ALAB, NEQ NOO NC UEFA CRAL
WEQAVBCUUQ CRA UOQ RLTE:

“CRA VUBA XE CRA KNOOAL XB JOUUTXES BU BZAAC, NEQ NESAOB QABFAEQ CRAVA
CRA FRXOQVAE CU SVAAC.”

CRAVA BNC CRA CZU SVUZE-WH HAVBUEB; SVUZE-WH, NEQ LAC FRXOQVAE; FRXOQVAE
NC OANBC XE RANVC; NEQ XC ZNB BWTTAV-CXTA; BWTTAV, SOUVXUWB BWTTAV!




CRA OANH-PVUS

N POAN, N SVNBBRUHHAV, NEQ N OANH-PVUS UEFA ZNECAQ CU BAA ZRXFR FUWOQ
GWTH RXSRABC; NEQ CRAL XEKXCAQ CRA ZRUOA ZUVOQ, NEQ AKAVLJUQL AOBA
JABXQAB ZRU FRUBA CU FUTA CU BAA CRA PABCXKNO. CRVAA PNTUWB GWTHAVB ZAVA
CRAL, NB AKAVLUEA ZUWOQ BNL, ZRAE CRAL NOO TAC CUSACRAV XE CRA VUUT.

“X ZXOO SXKA TL QNWSRCAV CU RXT ZRU GWTHB RXSRABC,” AIFONXTAQ CRA DXES;
“PUV XC XB EUC BU NTWBXES ZRAVA CRAVA XB EU HVXYA CU GWTH PUV.”

CRA POAN ZNB CRA PXVBC CU BCAH PUVZNVQ. RA RNQ AIMWXBXCA TNEEAVB, NEQ
JUZAQ CU CRA FUTHNEL UE NOO BXQAB; PUV RA RNQ EUJOA JOUUQ, NEQ ZNB,
TUVAUKAV, NFFWBCUTAQ CU CRA BUFXACL UP TNE NOUEA; NEQ CRNC TNDAB N SVANC
QXPPAVAEFA.

CRAE FNTA CRA SVNBBRUHHAV. RA ZNB FUEBXQAVNJOL RANKXAV, JWC RA ZNB
ZAOO-TNEEAVAQ, NEQ ZUVA N SVAAE WEXPUVT, ZRXFR RA RNQ JL VXSRC UP JXVCR;
RA BNXQ, TUVAUKAV, CRNC RA JAOUESAQ CU N KAVL NEFXAEC ASLHCXNE PNTXOL,

RNLFUFDB XE CRA TANQUZB BTAOC BU BZAACOL. “CRXB UEA EAKAV PUVSACB!”

“XC XB OUKAOL RAVA XE NWCWTE!” BNXQ CRA OXCCOA TNXQAE. NEQ BWQQAEOL CRA
NCTUBHRAVA SVAZ NB JOWA NSNXE NB JAPUVA; CRA PUVABC SVAZ VAQ, NEQ SVAAE,
NEQ LAOOUZ-FUOUVAQ. CRA QUSB FNTA OANHXES NOUES, NEQ ZRUOA POUFDB UP
ZXOQ-PUZO POAZ UKAV CRA FNXVE, ZRAVA JONFDJAVVL-JWBRAB ZAVA RNESXES
VUWEQ CRA UOQ BCUEAB. CRA BAN ZNB QNVD JOWA, FUKAVAQ ZXCR BRXHB PWOO
UP ZRXCA BNXOB; NEQ XE CRA JNVE UOQ ZUTAE, TNXQAEB, NEQ FRXOQVAE ZAVA
BXCCXES HXFDXES RUHB XECU N ONVSA FNBD; CRA LUWES BNES BUESB, JWC CRA
UOQ CUOQ PNXVL CNOAB UP TUWECNXE-BHVXCAB NEQ BUUCRBNLAVB. EUCRXES FUWOQ
JA TUVA FRNVTXES.

“XC XB QAOXSRCPWO RAVA XE ZXECAV!” BNXQ CRA OXCCOA TNXQAE. NEQ NOO CRA
CVAAB ZAVA FUKAVAQ ZXCR RUNV-PVUBC; CRAL OUUDAQ OXDA ZRXCA FUVNOB; CRA
BEUZ FVNFDOAQ WEQAV PUUC, NB XP UEA RNQ EAZ JUUCB UE; NEQ UEA PNOOXES
BCNV NPCAV CRA UCRAV ZNB BAAE XE CRA BDL. CRA FRVXBCTNB-CVAA ZNB OXSRCAQ
XE CRA VUUT; HVABAECB ZAVA CRAVA, NEQ SUUQ-RWTUV VAXSEAQ. XE CRA FUWECVL
CRA KXUOXE BUWEQAQ XE CRA VUUT UP CRA HANBNEC; CRA EAZOL-JNDAQ FNDAB
ZAVA NCCNFDAQ; AKAE CRA HUUVABC FRXOQ BNXQ, “XC XB VANOOL QAOXSRCPWO
RAVA XE ZXECAV!”

LAB, XC ZNB QAOXSRCPWO; NEQ CRA OXCCOA TNXQAE BRUZAQ CRA JUL AKAVLCRXES;
NEQ CRA AOQAV CVAA BCXOO ZNB PVNSVNEC, NEQ CRA VAQ PONS, ZXCR CRA ZRXCA
FVUBB, ZNB BCXOO ZNKXES: CRA PONS WEQAV ZRXFR CRA UOQ BANTNE XE CRA EAZ
JUUCRB RNQ BNXOAQ. NEQ CRA JUL SVAZ WH CU JA N ONQ, NEQ ZNB CU SU PUVCR
XE CRA ZXQA ZUVOQ-PNV, PNV NZNL CU ZNVT ONEQB, ZRAVA CRA FUPPAA-CVAA
SVUZB; JWC NC RXB QAHNVCWVA CRA OXCCOA TNXQAE CUUD NE AOQAV-JOUBBUT PVUT
RAV JUBUT, NEQ SNKA XC RXT CU DAAH; NEQ XC ZNB HONFAQ JACZAAE CRA OANKAB
UP RXB HVNLAV-JUUD; NEQ ZRAE XE PUVAXSE ONEQB RA UHAEAQ CRA JUUD, XC
ZNB NOZNLB NC CRA HONFA ZRAVA CRA DAAHBNDA-POUZAV ONL; NEQ CRA TUVA RA
OUUDAQ NC XC, CRA PVABRAV XC JAFNTA; RA PAOC NB XC ZAVA, CRA PVNSVNEFA
UP CRA QNEXBR SVUKAB; NEQ PVUT NTUES CRA OANKAB UP CRA POUZAVB RA FUWOQ
QXBCXEFCOL BAA CRA OXCCOA TNXQAE, HAAHXES PUVCR ZXCR RAV JVXSRC JOWA
ALAB--NEQ CRAE BRA ZRXBHAVAQ, “XC XB QAOXSRCPWO RAVA XE BHVXES, BWTTAV,
NWCWTE, NEQ ZXECAV”; NEQ N RWEQVAQ KXBXUEB SOXQAQ JAPUVA RXB TXEQ.

CRWB HNBBAQ TNEL LANVB, NEQ RA ZNB EUZ NE UOQ TNE, NEQ BNC ZXCR RXB UOQ
ZXPA WEQAV CRA JOUUTXES CVAA. CRAL RAOQ ANFR UCRAV JL CRA RNEQ, NB CRA
UOQ SVNEQ-PNCRAV NEQ SVNEQ-TUCRAV LUEQAV XE CRA EAZ JUUCRB QXQ, NEQ CRAL
CNODAQ AINFCOL OXDA CRAT UP UOQ CXTAB, NEQ UP CRA PXPCXACR NEEXKAVBNVL
UP CRAXV ZAQQXES. CRA OXCCOA TNXQAE, ZXCR CRA JOWA ALAB, NEQ ZXCR
AOQAV-JOUBBUTB XE RAV RNXV, BNC XE CRA CVAA, EUQQAQ CU JUCR UP CRAT,
NEQ BNXQ, “CU-QNL XB CRA PXPCXACR NEEXKAVBNVL!” NEQ CRAE BRA CUUD CZU
POUZAVB UWC UP RAV RNXV, NEQ DXBBAQ CRAT. PXVBC, CRAL BRUEA OXDA BXOKAV,
CRAE OXDA SUOQ; NEQ ZRAE CRAL ONXQ CRAT UE CRA RANQB UP CRA UOQ HAUHOA,
ANFR POUZAV JAFNTA N SUOQAE FVUZE. BU CRAVA CRAL JUCR BNC, OXDA N DXES
NEQ N MWAAE, WEQAV CRA PVNSVNEC CVAA, CRNC OUUDAQ AINFCOL OXDA NE AOQAV:
CRA UOQ TNE CUOQ RXB ZXPA CRA BCUVL UP “UOQ ENEEL,” NB XC RNQ JAAE CUOQ
RXT ZRAE N JUL. NEQ XC BAATAQ CU JUCR UP CRAT XC FUECNXEAQ TWFR CRNC
VABATJOAQ CRAXV UZE RXBCUVL; NEQ CRUBA HNVCB CRNC ZAVA OXDA XC HOANBAQ
CRAT JABC.

“CRWB XC XB,” BNXQ CRA OXCCOA TNXQAE XE CRA CVAA, “BUTA FNOO TA 'UOQ
ENEEL,' UCRAVB N 'QVLNQ,' JWC, XE VANOXCL, TL ENTA XB 'VATATJVNEFA';
'CXB X ZRU BXC XE CRA CVAA CRNC SVUZB NEQ SVUZB! X FNE VATATJAV; X FNE
CAOO CRXESB! OAC TA BAA XP LUW RNKA TL POUZAV BCXOO?”

NEQ CRA UOQ TNE UHAEAQ RXB HVNLAV-JUUD. CRAVA ONL CRA AOQAV-JOUBBUT,
NB PVABR NB XP XC RNQ JAAE HONFAQ CRAVA JWC N BRUVC CXTA JAPUVA; NEQ
VATATJVNEFA EUQQAQ, NEQ CRA UOQ HAUHOA, QAFDAQ ZXCR FVUZEB UP SUOQ, BNC
XE CRA POWBR UP CRA AKAEXES BWE. CRAL FOUBAQ CRAXV ALAB, NEQ--NEQ--!
LAB, CRNC'B CRA AEQ UP CRA BCUVL!

CRA OXCCOA JUL ONL XE RXB JAQ; RA QXQ EUC DEUZ XP RA RNQ QVANTAQ UV
EUC, UV XP RA RNQ JAAE OXBCAEXES ZRXOA BUTAUEA CUOQ RXT CRA BCUVL. CRA
CAN-HUC ZNB BCNEQXES UE CRA CNJOA, JWC EU AOQAV CVAA ZNB SVUZXES UWC
UP XC! NEQ CRA UOQ TNE, ZRU RNQ JAAE CNODXES, ZNB GWBC UE CRA HUXEC UP
SUXES UWC NC CRA QUUV, NEQ RA QXQ SU.

“RUZ BHOAEQXQ CRNC ZNB!” BNXQ CRA OXCCOA JUL. “TUCRAV, X RNKA JAAE CU
ZNVT FUWECVXAB.”

“BU X BRUWOQ CRXED,” BNXQ RXB TUCRAV. “ZRAE UEA RNB QVWED CZU SUUQ
FWHPWOB UP AOQAV-POUZAV CAN, 'CXB OXDAOL AEUWSR UEA SUAB XECU ZNVT
FOXTNCAB”; NEQ BRA CWFDAQ RXT WH EXFAOL, OANBC RA BRUWOQ CNDA FUOQ. “LUW
RNKA RNQ N SUUQ BOAAH ZRXOA X RNKA JAAE BXCCXES RAVA, NEQ NVSWXES ZXCR
RXT ZRACRAV XC ZNB N BCUVL UV N PNXVL CNOA.”

“NEQ ZRAVA XB UOQ ENEEL?” NBDAQ CRA OXCCOA JUL.

“XE CRA CAN-HUC,” BNXQ RXB TUCRAV; “NEQ CRAVA BRA TNL VATNXE.”




CRA JAOO

HAUHOA BNXQ “CRA AKAEXES JAOO XB BUWEQXES, CRA BWE XB BACCXES.” PUV N
BCVNESA ZUEQVUWB CUEA ZNB RANVQ XE CRA ENVVUZ BCVAACB UP N ONVSA CUZE.
XC ZNB OXDA CRA BUWEQ UP N FRWVFR-JAOO: JWC XC ZNB UEOL RANVQ PUV N
TUTAEC, PUV CRA VUOOXES UP CRA FNVVXNSAB NEQ CRA KUXFAB UP CRA TWOCXCWQA
TNQA CUU SVANC N EUXBA.

CRUBA HAVBUEB ZRU ZAVA ZNODXES UWCBXQA CRA CUZE, ZRAVA CRA RUWBAB ZAVA
PNVCRAV NHNVC, ZXCR SNVQAEB UV OXCCOA PXAOQB JACZAAE CRAT, FUWOQ BAA
CRA AKAEXES BDL BCXOO JACCAV, NEQ RANVQ CRA BUWEQ UP CRA JAOO TWFR
TUVA QXBCXEFCOL. XC ZNB NB XP CRA CUEAB FNTA PVUT N FRWVFR XE CRA BCXOO
PUVABC; HAUHOA OUUDAQ CRXCRAVZNVQ, NEQ PAOC CRAXV TXEQB NCCWEAQ TUBC
BUOATEOL.

N OUES CXTA HNBBAQ, NEQ HAUHOA BNXQ CU ANFR UCRAV--“X ZUEQAV XP CRAVA
XB N FRWVFR UWC XE CRA ZUUQ? CRA JAOO RNB N CUEA CRNC XB ZUEQVUWB BZAAC;
OAC WB BCVUOO CRXCRAV, NEQ AINTXEA CRA TNCCAV EANVAV.” NEQ CRA VXFR
HAUHOA QVUKA UWC, NEQ CRA HUUV ZNODAQ, JWC CRA ZNL BAATAQ BCVNESAOL
OUES CU CRAT; NEQ ZRAE CRAL FNTA CU N FOWTH UP ZXOOUZB ZRXFR SVAZ UE CRA
BDXVCB UP CRA PUVABC, CRAL BNC QUZE, NEQ OUUDAQ WH NC CRA OUES
JVNEFRAB, NEQ PNEFXAQ CRAL ZAVA EUZ XE CRA QAHCR UP CRA SVAAE ZUUQ. CRA
FUEPAFCXUEAV UP CRA CUZE FNTA UWC, NEQ BAC WH RXB JUUCR CRAVA; NEQ BUUE
NPCAV FNTA NEUCRAV FUEPAFCXUEAV, ZRU RWES N JAOO UKAV RXB BCNEQ, NB
N BXSE UV UVENTAEC, JWC XC RNQ EU FONHHAV, NEQ XC ZNB CNVVAQ UKAV CU
HVABAVKA XC PVUT CRA VNXE. ZRAE NOO CRA HAUHOA VACWVEAQ RUTA, CRAL BNXQ
XC RNQ JAAE KAVL VUTNECXF, NEQ CRNC XC ZNB MWXCA N QXPPAVAEC BUVC UP
CRXES CU N HXF-EXF UV CAN-HNVCL. CRAVA ZAVA CRVAA HAVBUEB ZRU NBBAVCAQ
CRAL RNQ HAEACVNCAQ CU CRA AEQ UP CRA PUVABC, NEQ CRNC CRAL RNQ NOZNLB
RANVQ CRA ZUEQAVPWO BUWEQB UP CRA JAOO, JWC XC RNQ BAATAQ CU CRAT NB XP
XC RNQ FUTA PVUT CRA CUZE. UEA ZVUCA N ZRUOA HUAT NJUWC XC, NEQ BNXQ CRA
JAOO BUWEQAQ OXDA CRA KUXFA UP N TUCRAV CU N SUUQ QANV FRXOQ, NEQ
CRNC EU TAOUQL ZNB BZAACAV CRNE CRA CUEAB UP CRA JAOO. CRA DXES UP CRA
FUWECVL ZNB NOBU UJBAVKNEC UP XC, NEQ KUZAQ CRNC RA ZRU FUWOQ QXBFUKAV
ZRAEFA CRA BUWEQB HVUFAAQAQ, BRUWOQ RNKA CRA CXCOA UP “WEXKAVBNO
JAOO-VXESAV,” AKAE XP XC ZAVA EUC VANOOL N JAOO.

TNEL HAVBUEB EUZ ZAEC CU CRA ZUUQ, PUV CRA BNDA UP SACCXES CRA HONFA,
JWC UEA UEOL VACWVEAQ ZXCR N BUVC UP AIHONENCXUE; PUV EUJUQL ZAEC PNV
AEUWSR, CRNC UEA EUC PWVCRAV CRNE CRA UCRAVB. RUZAKAV, RA BNXQ CRNC
CRA BUWEQ HVUFAAQAQ PVUT N KAVL ONVSA UZO, XE N RUOOUZ CVAA; N BUVC UP
OANVEAQ UZO, CRNC FUECXEWNOOL DEUFDAQ XCB RANQ NSNXEBC CRA JVNEFRAB. JWC
ZRACRAV CRA BUWEQ FNTA PVUT RXB RANQ UV PVUT CRA RUOOUZ CVAA, CRNC EU
UEA FUWOQ BNL ZXCR FAVCNXECL. BU EUZ RA SUC CRA HONFA UP “WEXKAVBNO
JAOO-VXESAV,” NEQ ZVUCA LANVOL N BRUVC CVANCXBA “UE CRA UZO”; JWC
AKAVLJUQL ZNB GWBC NB ZXBA NB JAPUVA.

XC ZNB CRA QNL UP FUEPXVTNCXUE. CRA FOAVSLTNE RNQ BHUDAE BU CUWFRXESOL,
CRA FRXOQVAE ZRU ZAVA FUEPXVTAQ RNQ JAAE SVANCOL TUKAQ; XC ZNB
NE AKAECPWO QNL PUV CRAT; PVUT FRXOQVAE CRAL JAFUTA NOO NC UEFA
SVUZE-WH-HAVBUEB; XC ZNB NB XP CRAXV XEPNEC BUWOB ZAVA EUZ CU POL NOO
NC UEFA XECU HAVBUEB ZXCR TUVA WEQAVBCNEQXES. CRA BWE ZNB BRXEXES
SOUVXUWBOL; CRA FRXOQVAE CRNC RNQ JAAE FUEPXVTAQ ZAEC UWC UP CRA CUZE;
NEQ PVUT CRA ZUUQ ZNB JUVEA CUZNVQB CRAT CRA BUWEQB UP CRA WEDEUZE JAOO
ZXCR ZUEQAVPWO QXBCXEFCEABB. CRAL NOO XTTAQXNCAOL PAOC N ZXBR CU SU
CRXCRAV; NOO AIFAHC CRVAA. UEA UP CRAT RNQ CU SU RUTA CU CVL UE N
JNOO-QVABB; PUV XC ZNB GWBC CRA QVABB NEQ CRA JNOO ZRXFR RNQ FNWBAQ RAV
CU JA FUEPXVTAQ CRXB CXTA, PUV UCRAVZXBA BRA ZUWOQ EUC RNKA FUTA;
CRA UCRAV ZNB N HUUV JUL, ZRU RNQ JUVVUZAQ RXB FUNC NEQ JUUCB CU JA
FUEPXVTAQ XE PVUT CRA XEEDAAHAV'B BUE, NEQ RA ZNB CU SXKA CRAT JNFD JL
N FAVCNXE RUWV; CRA CRXVQ BNXQ CRNC RA EAKAV ZAEC CU N BCVNESA HONFA
XP RXB HNVAECB ZAVA EUC ZXCR RXT--CRNC RA RNQ NOZNLB JAAE N SUUQ JUL
RXCRAVCU, NEQ ZUWOQ BCXOO JA BU EUZ CRNC RA ZNB FUEPXVTAQ, NEQ CRNC UEA
UWSRC EUC CU ONWSR NC RXT PUV XC: CRA UCRAVB, RUZAKAV, QXQ TNDA PWE UP
RXT, NPCAV NOO.

CRAVA ZAVA CRVAA, CRAVAPUVA, CRNC QXQ EUC SU; CRA UCRAVB RNBCAEAQ UE.
CRA BWE BRUEA, CRA JXVQB BNES, NEQ CRA FRXOQVAE BNES CUU, NEQ ANFR RAOQ
CRA UCRAV JL CRA RNEQ; PUV NB LAC CRAL RNQ EUEA UP CRAT NEL RXSR UPPXFA,
NEQ ZAVA NOO UP AMWNO VNED XE CRA ALA UP SUQ.

JWC CZU UP CRA LUWESABC BUUE SVAZ CXVAQ, NEQ JUCR VACWVEAQ CU CUZE; CZU
OXCCOA SXVOB BNC QUZE, NEQ CZXEAQ SNVONEQB, BU CRAL QXQ EUC SU AXCRAV;
NEQ ZRAE CRA UCRAVB VANFRAQ CRA ZXOOUZ-CVAA, ZRAVA CRA FUEPAFCXUEAV ZNB,
CRAL BNXQ, “EUZ ZA NVA CRAVA! XE VANOXCL CRA JAOO QUAB EUC AIXBC; XC XB
UEOL N PNEFL CRNC HAUHOA RNKA CNDAE XECU CRAXV RANQB!”

NC CRA BNTA TUTAEC CRA JAOO BUWEQAQ QAAH XE CRA ZUUQ, BU FOANV NEQ
BUOATEOL CRNC PXKA UV BXI QACAVTXEAQ CU HAEACVNCA BUTAZRNC PWVCRAV. XC
ZNB BU CRXFD, NEQ CRA PUOXNSA BU QAEBA, CRNC XC ZNB MWXCA PNCXSWXES
CU HVUFAAQ. ZUUQVUUP NEQ NEATUEXAB SVAZ NOTUBC CUU RXSR; JOUUTXES
FUEKUOKWOWBAB NEQ JONFDJAVVL-JWBRAB RWES XE OUES SNVONEQB PVUT CVAA CU
CVAA, ZRAVA CRA EXSRCXESNOA BNES NEQ CRA BWEJANTB ZAVA HONLXES: XC ZNB
KAVL JANWCXPWO, JWC XC ZNB EU HONFA PUV SXVOB CU SU; CRAXV FOUCRAB ZUWOQ
SAC BU CUVE. ONVSA JOUFDB UP BCUEA ONL CRAVA, UKAVSVUZE ZXCR TUBB UP
AKAVL FUOUV; CRA PVABR BHVXES JWJJOAQ PUVCR, NEQ TNQA N BCVNESA SWVSOXES
BUWEQ.

“CRNC BWVAOL FNEEUC JA CRA JAOO,” BNXQ UEA UP CRA FRXOQVAE, OLXES QUZE
NEQ OXBCAEXES. “CRXB TWBC JA OUUDAQ CU.” BU RA VATNXEAQ, NEQ OAC CRA
UCRAVB SU UE ZXCRUWC RXT.

CRAL NPCAVZNVQB FNTA CU N OXCCOA RUWBA, TNQA UP JVNEFRAB NEQ CRA JNVD UP
CVAAB; N ONVSA ZXOQ NHHOA-CVAA JAEC UKAV XC, NB XP XC ZUWOQ BRUZAV QUZE
NOO XCB JOABBXESB UE CRA VUUP, ZRAVA VUBAB ZAVA JOUUTXES. CRA OUES BCATB
CZXEAQ VUWEQ CRA SNJOA, UE ZRXFR CRAVA RWES N BTNOO JAOO.

ZNB XC CRNC ZRXFR HAUHOA RNQ RANVQ? LAB, AKAVLJUQL ZNB WENEXTUWB UE CRA
BWJGAFC, AIFAHC UEA, ZRU BNXQ CRNC CRA JAOO ZNB CUU BTNOO NEQ CUU PXEA
CU JA RANVQ NC BU SVANC N QXBCNEFA, NEQ JABXQAB XC ZNB KAVL QXPPAVAEC
CUEAB CU CRUBA CRNC FUWOQ TUKA N RWTNE RANVC XE BWFR N TNEEAV. XC ZNB N
DXES'B BUE ZRU BHUDA; ZRAVAUE CRA UCRAVB BNXQ, “BWFR HAUHOA NOZNLB ZNEC
CU JA ZXBAV CRNE AKAVLJUQL AOBA.”

CRAL EUZ OAC RXT SU UE NOUEA; NEQ NB RA ZAEC, RXB JVANBC ZNB PXOOAQ TUVA
NEQ TUVA ZXCR CRA PUVABC BUOXCWQA; JWC RA BCXOO RANVQ CRA OXCCOA JAOO
ZXCR ZRXFR CRA UCRAVB ZAVA BU BNCXBPXAQ, NEQ EUZ NEQ CRAE, ZRAE CRA
ZXEQ JOAZ, RA FUWOQ NOBU RANV CRA HAUHOA BXESXES ZRU ZAVA BXCCXES NC CAN
ZRAVA CRA FUEPAFCXUEAV RNQ RXB CAEC; JWC CRA QAAH BUWEQ UP CRA JAOO VUBA
OUWQAV; XC ZNB NOTUBC NB XP NE UVSNE ZAVA NFFUTHNELXES XC, NEQ CRA CUEAB
FNTA PVUT CRA OAPC RNEQ, CRA BXQA ZRAVA CRA RANVC XB HONFAQ. N VWBCOXES
ZNB RANVQ XE CRA JWBRAB, NEQ N OXCCOA JUL BCUUQ JAPUVA CRA DXES'B BUE, N
JUL XE ZUUQAE BRUAB, NEQ ZXCR BU BRUVC N GNFDAC CRNC UEA FUWOQ BAA ZRNC
OUES ZVXBCB RA RNQ. JUCR DEAZ ANFR UCRAV: CRA JUL ZNB CRNC UEA NTUES
CRA FRXOQVAE ZRU FUWOQ EUC FUTA JAFNWBA RA RNQ CU SU RUTA NEQ VACWVE RXB
GNFDAC NEQ JUUCB CU CRA XEEDAAHAV'B BUE. CRXB RA RNQ QUEA, NEQ ZNB EUZ
SUXES UE XE ZUUQAE BRUAB NEQ XE RXB RWTJOA QVABB, PUV CRA JAOO BUWEQAQ
ZXCR BU QAAH N CUEA, NEQ ZXCR BWFR BCVNESA HUZAV, CRNC HVUFAAQ RA TWBC.

“ZRL, CRAE, ZA FNE SU CUSACRAV,” BNXQ CRA DXES'B BUE. JWC CRA HUUV
FRXOQ CRNC RNQ JAAE FUEPXVTAQ ZNB MWXCA NBRNTAQ; RA OUUDAQ NC RXB ZUUQAE
BRUAB, HWOOAQ NC CRA BRUVC BOAAKAB UP RXB GNFDAC, NEQ BNXQ CRNC RA ZNB
NPVNXQ RA FUWOQ EUC ZNOD BU PNBC; JABXQAB, RA CRUWSRC CRNC CRA JAOO TWBC
JA OUUDAQ PUV CU CRA VXSRC; PUV CRNC ZNB CRA HONFA ZRAVA NOO BUVCB UP
JANWCXPWO CRXESB ZAVA CU JA PUWEQ.

“JWC CRAVA ZA BRNOO EUC TAAC,” BNXQ CRA DXES'B BUE, EUQQXES NC CRA BNTA
CXTA CU CRA HUUV JUL, ZRU ZAEC XECU CRA QNVDABC, CRXFDABC HNVC UP CRA
ZUUQ, ZRAVA CRUVEB CUVA RXB RWTJOA QVABB, NEQ BFVNCFRAQ RXB PNFA NEQ
RNEQB NEQ PAAC CXOO CRAL JOAQ. CRA DXES'B BUE SUC BUTA BFVNCFRAB CUU;
JWC CRA BWE BRUEA UE RXB HNCR, NEQ XC XB RXT CRNC ZA ZXOO PUOOUZ, PUV RA
ZNB NE AIFAOOAEC NEQ VABUOWCA LUWCR.

“X TWBC NEQ ZXOO PXEQ CRA JAOO,” BNXQ RA, “AKAE XP X NT UJOXSAQ CU SU CU
CRA AEQ UP CRA ZUVOQ.”

CRA WSOL NHAB BNC WHUE CRA CVAAB, NEQ SVXEEAQ. “BRNOO ZA CRVNBR RXT?”
 BNXQ CRAL. “BRNOO ZA CRVNBR RXT? RA XB CRA BUE UP N DXES!”

JWC UE RA ZAEC, ZXCRUWC JAXES QXBRANVCAEAQ, QAAHAV NEQ QAAHAV XECU CRA
ZUUQ, ZRAVA CRA TUBC ZUEQAVPWO POUZAVB ZAVA SVUZXES. CRAVA BCUUQ ZRXCA
OXOXAB ZXCR JOUUQ-VAQ BCNTXEN, BDLJOWA CWOXHB, ZRXFR BRUEA NB CRAL ZNKAQ
XE CRA ZXEQB, NEQ NHHOA-CVAAB, CRA NHHOAB UP ZRXFR OUUDAQ AINFCOL OXDA
ONVSA BUNHJWJJOAB: BU UEOL CRXED RUZ CRA CVAAB TWBC RNKA BHNVDOAQ XE CRA
BWEBRXEA! NVUWEQ CRA EXFABC SVAAE TANQB, ZRAVA CRA QAAV ZAVA HONLXES XE
CRA SVNBB, SVAZ TNSEXPXFAEC UNDB NEQ JAAFRAB; NEQ XP CRA JNVD UP UEA UP
CRA CVAAB ZNB FVNFDAQ, CRAVA SVNBB NEQ OUES FVAAHXES HONECB SVAZ XE
CRA FVAKXFAB. NEQ CRAVA ZAVA ONVSA FNOT ONDAB CRAVA CUU, XE ZRXFR ZRXCA
BZNEB ZAVA BZXTTXES, NEQ JANC CRA NXV ZXCR CRAXV ZXESB. CRA DXES'B BUE
UPCAE BCUUQ BCXOO NEQ OXBCAEAQ. RA CRUWSRC CRA JAOO BUWEQAQ PVUT CRA
QAHCRB UP CRABA BCXOO ONDAB; JWC CRAE RA VATNVDAQ NSNXE CRNC CRA CUEA
HVUFAAQAQ EUC PVUT CRAVA, JWC PNVCRAV UPP, PVUT UWC CRA QAHCRB UP CRA
PUVABC.

CRA BWE EUZ BAC: CRA NCTUBHRAVA SOUZAQ OXDA PXVA. XC ZNB BCXOO XE CRA
ZUUQB, BU KAVL BCXOO; NEQ RA PAOO UE RXB DEAAB, BWES RXB AKAEXES RLTE,
NEQ BNXQ: “X FNEEUC PXEQ ZRNC X BAAD; CRA BWE XB SUXES QUZE, NEQ EXSRC
XB FUTXES--CRA QNVD, QNVD EXSRC. LAC HAVRNHB X TNL JA NJOA UEFA TUVA
CU BAA CRA VUWEQ VAQ BWE JAPUVA RA AECXVAOL QXBNHHANVB. X ZXOO FOXTJ WH
LUEQAV VUFD.”

NEQ RA BAXYAQ RUOQ UP CRA FVAAHXES-HONECB, NEQ CRA VUUCB UP
CVAAB--FOXTJAQ WH CRA TUXBC BCUEAB ZRAVA CRA ZNCAV-BENDAB ZAVA ZVXCRXES
NEQ CRA CUNQB ZAVA FVUNDXES--NEQ RA SNXEAQ CRA BWTTXC JAPUVA CRA BWE
RNQ MWXCA SUEA QUZE. RUZ TNSEXPXFAEC ZNB CRA BXSRC PVUT CRXB RAXSRC! CRA
BAN--CRA SVANC, CRA SOUVXUWB BAN, CRNC QNBRAQ XCB OUES ZNKAB NSNXEBC CRA
FUNBC--ZNB BCVACFRAQ UWC JAPUVA RXT. NEQ LUEQAV, ZRAVA BAN NEQ BDL TAAC,
BCUUQ CRA BWE, OXDA N ONVSA BRXEXES NOCNV, NOO TAOCAQ CUSACRAV XE CRA
TUBC SOUZXES FUOUVB. NEQ CRA ZUUQ NEQ CRA BAN BNES N BUES UP VAGUXFXES,
NEQ RXB RANVC BNES ZXCR CRA VABC: NOO ENCWVA ZNB N KNBC RUOL FRWVFR,
XE ZRXFR CRA CVAAB NEQ CRA JWULNEC FOUWQB ZAVA CRA HXOONVB, POUZAVB NEQ
SVNBB CRA KAOKAC FNVHACXES, NEQ RANKAE XCBAOP CRA ONVSA FWHUON. CRA VAQ
FUOUVB NJUKA PNQAQ NZNL NB CRA BWE KNEXBRAQ, JWC N TXOOXUE BCNVB ZAVA
OXSRCAQ, N TXOOXUE ONTHB BRUEA; NEQ CRA DXES'B BUE BHVANQ UWC RXB NVTB
CUZNVQB RANKAE, NEQ ZUUQ, NEQ BAN; ZRAE NC CRA BNTA TUTAEC, FUTXES JL
N HNCR CU CRA VXSRC, NHHANVAQ, XE RXB ZUUQAE BRUAB NEQ GNFDAC, CRA HUUV
JUL ZRU RNQ JAAE FUEPXVTAQ ZXCR RXT. RA RNQ PUOOUZAQ RXB UZE HNCR, NEQ
RNQ VANFRAQ CRA BHUC GWBC NB BUUE NB CRA BUE UP CRA DXES RNQ QUEA. CRAL
VNE CUZNVQB ANFR UCRAV, NEQ BCUUQ CUSACRAV RNEQ XE RNEQ XE CRA KNBC
FRWVFR UP ENCWVA NEQ UP HUACVL, ZRXOA UKAV CRAT BUWEQAQ CRA XEKXBXJOA
RUOL JAOO: JOABBAQ BHXVXCB POUNCAQ NVUWEQ CRAT, NEQ OXPCAQ WH CRAXV
KUXFAB XE N VAGUXFXES RNOOAOWGNR!




CRA UOQ RUWBA

XE CRA BCVAAC, WH CRAVA, ZNB NE UOQ, N KAVL UOQ RUWBA--XC ZNB NOTUBC
CRVAA RWEQVAQ LANVB UOQ, PUV CRNC TXSRC JA DEUZE JL VANQXES CRA SVANC
JANT UE ZRXFR CRA QNCA UP CRA LANV ZNB FNVKAQ: CUSACRAV ZXCR CWOXHB NEQ
RUH-JXEQB CRAVA ZAVA ZRUOA KAVBAB BHAOOAQ NB XE PUVTAV CXTAB, NEQ UKAV
AKAVL ZXEQUZ ZNB N QXBCUVCAQ PNFA FWC UWC XE CRA JANT. CRA UEA BCUVL
BCUUQ PUVZNVQ N SVANC ZNL UKAV CRA UCRAV; NEQ QXVAFCOL WEQAV CRA ANKAB
ZNB N OANQAE BHUWC ZXCR N QVNSUE'B RANQ; CRA VNXE-ZNCAV BRUWOQ RNKA VWE
UWC UP CRA TUWCR, JWC XC VNE UWC UP CRA JAOOL, PUV CRAVA ZNB N RUOA XE
CRA BHUWC.

NOO CRA UCRAV RUWBAB XE CRA BCVAAC ZAVA BU EAZ NEQ BU EANC, ZXCR ONVSA
ZXEQUZ HNEAB NEQ BTUUCR ZNOOB, UEA FUWOQ ANBXOL BAA CRNC CRAL ZUWOQ RNKA
EUCRXES CU QU ZXCR CRA UOQ RUWBA: CRAL FAVCNXEOL CRUWSRC, “RUZ OUES XB
CRNC UOQ QAFNLAQ CRXES CU BCNEQ RAVA NB N BHAFCNFOA XE CRA BCVAAC? NEQ
CRAE CRA HVUGAFCXES ZXEQUZB BCNEQ BU PNV UWC, CRNC EU UEA FNE BAA PVUT
UWV ZXEQUZB ZRNC RNHHAEB XE CRNC QXVAFCXUE! CRA BCAHB NVA NB JVUNQ NB
CRUBA UP N HNONFA, NEQ NB RXSR NB CU N FRWVFR CUZAV. CRA XVUE VNXOXESB
OUUD GWBC OXDA CRA QUUV CU NE UOQ PNTXOL KNWOC, NEQ CRAE CRAL RNKA JVNBB
CUHB--CRNC'B BU BCWHXQ!”

UE CRA UCRAV BXQA UP CRA BCVAAC ZAVA NOBU EAZ NEQ EANC RUWBAB, NEQ CRAL
CRUWSRC GWBC NB CRA UCRAVB QXQ; JWC NC CRA ZXEQUZ UHHUBXCA CRA UOQ RUWBA
CRAVA BNC N OXCCOA JUL ZXCR PVABR VUBL FRAADB NEQ JVXSRC JANTXES ALAB:
RA FAVCNXEOL OXDAQ CRA UOQ RUWBA JABC, NEQ CRNC JUCR XE BWEBRXEA NEQ
TUUEBRXEA. NEQ ZRAE RA OUUDAQ NFVUBB NC CRA ZNOO ZRAVA CRA TUVCNV
RNQ PNOOAE UWC, RA FUWOQ BXC NEQ PXEQ UWC CRAVA CRA BCVNESABC PXSWVAB
XTNSXENJOA; AINFCOL NB CRA BCVAAC RNQ NHHANVAQ JAPUVA, ZXCR BCAHB,
HVUGAFCXES ZXEQUZB, NEQ HUXECAQ SNJOAB; RA FUWOQ BAA BUOQXAVB ZXCR
RNOJAVQB, NEQ BHUWCB ZRAVA CRA ZNCAV VNE, OXDA QVNSUEB NEQ BAVHAECB.
CRNC ZNB N RUWBA CU OUUD NC; NEQ CRAVA OXKAQ NE UOQ TNE, ZRU ZUVA HOWBR
JVAAFRAB; NEQ RA RNQ N FUNC ZXCR ONVSA JVNBB JWCCUEB, NEQ N ZXS CRNC UEA
FUWOQ BAA ZNB N VANO ZXS. AKAVL TUVEXES CRAVA FNTA NE UOQ PAOOUZ CU RXT
ZRU HWC RXB VUUTB XE UVQAV, NEQ ZAEC UE AVVNEQB; UCRAVZXBA, CRA UOQ TNE
XE CRA HOWBR JVAAFRAB ZNB MWXCA NOUEA XE CRA UOQ RUWBA. EUZ NEQ CRAE RA
FNTA CU CRA ZXEQUZ NEQ OUUDAQ UWC, NEQ CRA OXCCOA JUL EUQQAQ CU RXT,
NEQ CRA UOQ TNE EUQQAQ NSNXE, NEQ BU CRAL JAFNTA NFMWNXECNEFAB, NEQ CRAE
CRAL ZAVA PVXAEQB, NOCRUWSR CRAL RNQ EAKAV BHUDAE CU ANFR UCRAV--JWC
CRNC TNQA EU QXPPAVAEFA. CRA OXCCOA JUL RANVQ RXB HNVAECB BNL, “CRA UOQ
TNE UHHUBXCA XB KAVL ZAOO UPP, JWC RA XB BU KAVL, KAVL OUEAOL!”

CRA BWEQNL PUOOUZXES, CRA OXCCOA JUL CUUD BUTACRXES, NEQ ZVNHHAQ XC WH
XE N HXAFA UP HNHAV, ZAEC QUZEBCNXVB, NEQ BCUUQ XE CRA QUUVZNL; NEQ ZRAE
CRA TNE ZRU ZAEC UE AVVNEQB FNTA HNBC, RA BNXQ CU RXT--

“X BNL, TNBCAV! ZXOO LUW SXKA CRXB CU CRA UOQ TNE UKAV CRA ZNL PVUT TA?
X RNKA CZU HAZCAV BUOQXAVB--CRXB XB UEA UP CRAT, NEQ RA BRNOO RNKA XC,
PUV X DEUZ RA XB BU KAVL, KAVL OUEAOL.”

NEQ CRA UOQ AVVNEQ TNE OUUDAQ MWXCA HOANBAQ, EUQQAQ, NEQ CUUD CRA HAZCAV

KXBXC; NEQ BU RA SUC HAVTXBBXUE UP RXB HNVAECB, NEQ CRAE ZAEC UKAV CU
CRA UOQ RUWBA.

NEQ CRA JVNBB JNOOB UE CRA XVUE VNXOXESB BRUEA TWFR JVXSRCAV CRNE AKAV;
UEA ZUWOQ RNKA CRUWSRC CRAL ZAVA HUOXBRAQ UE NFFUWEC UP CRA KXBXC; NEQ

TXSRC, CRAXV FRAADB NHHANVAQ BU TWFR VUWEQAV CRNE JAPUVA. LAB, CRAL

UHAEAQ.

CRA ZRUOA HNBBNSA ZNB RWES ZXCR HUVCVNXCB UP DEXSRCB XE NVTUV, NEQ

OUES FVAKXFAB, JWC SVNBB SVAZ CRAVA NEQ OANKAB UWC UP CRAT NOCUSACRAV,

NEQ CRAE CRAL AECAVAQ N FRNTJAV ZRAVA CRA ZNOOB ZAVA FUKAVAQ ZXCR RUS'B
OANCRAV, NEQ HVXECAQ ZXCR SUOQ POUZAVB.

   “CRA SXOQXES QAFNLB,
   JWC RUS'B OANCRAV BCNLB!”

BNXQ CRA ZNOOB.

NEQ CRAVA BCUUQ ANBL-FRNXVB, ZXCR BWFR RXSR JNFDB, NEQ BU FNVKAQ UWC,

“CRNEDAA! CRNEDAA!” UV “FVNEDL! FVNEDL!” BUWEQAQ PVUT NOO CRA PWVEXCWVA;

WEQAV CRA HXFCWVA, XE N SONYAQ PVNTA, CRAVA RWES N JUWMWAC UP ZXCRAVAQ

“UR!” BNXQ RA. “CRA UOQ CRUWSRCB, ZXCR ZRNC CRAL TNL JVXES ZXCR CRAT,
FUTA NEQ KXBXC TA, NEQ EUZ LUW NOBU FUTA! X NT KAVL ZAOO UPP!”

CRAE RA CUUD N JUUD ZXCR HXFCWVAB XE XC QUZE PVUT CRA BRAOP; CRAVA ZAVA

CRA UOQ TNE EUZ ZAEC XECU CRA UCRAV VUUT CU PACFR HVABAVKAB, NHHOAB, NEQ

“JWC LUW TWBC!” BNXQ CRA OXCCOA JUL.

CRAE XE FNTA CRA UOQ TNE ZXCR CRA TUBC HOANBAQ NEQ RNHHL PNFA, CRA TUBC

CRA OXCCOA JUL VACWVEAQ RUTA RNHHL NEQ HOANBAQ, NEQ ZAADB NEQ QNLB

CRA FNVKAQ CVWTHACAVB JOAZ, “CVNCAVNCVN! CRAVA XB CRA OXCCOA JUL!

OXDA NEUCRAV.

PVUT CRA QVNZAVB.

“X BNZ LUW NOO UKAV CRAVA NC RUTA BU QXBCXEFCOL, NB XP LUW VANOOL ZAVA
RAVA; XC ZNB NSNXE CRNC BWEQNL TUVEXES; NOO LUW FRXOQVAE BCUUQ JAPUVA

QAKUWCOL ZXCR PUOQAQ RNEQB; NEQ PNCRAV NEQ TUCRAV ZAVA GWBC NB HXUWB;
NEQ CRAE CRA QUUV ZNB UHAEAQ, NEQ OXCCOA BXBCAV TNVL, ZRU XB EUC CZU
LANVB UOQ LAC, NEQ ZRU NOZNLB QNEFAB ZRAE BRA RANVB TWBXF UV BXESXES, UP
ZRNCAKAV DXEQ XC TNL JA, ZNB HWC XECU CRA VUUT--CRUWSR BRA UWSRC EUC CU
RNKA JAAE CRAVA--NEQ CRAE BRA JASNE CU QNEFA, JWC FUWOQ EUC DAAH CXTA,
JAFNWBA CRA CUEAB ZAVA BU OUES; NEQ CRAE BRA BCUUQ, PXVBC UE CRA UEA

“CAOO TA XP LUW BCXOO BXES UE BWEQNLB? CAOO TA BUTACRXES NJUWC OXCCOA

“LUW NVA SXKAE NZNL NB N HVABAEC!” BNXQ CRA OXCCOA JUL. “LUW TWBC
VATNXE. FNE LUW EUC WEQAVBCNEQ CRNC?”

CRA UOQ TNE EUZ FNTA ZXCR N QVNZAV, XE ZRXFR CRAVA ZNB TWFR CU JA BAAE,

CRNC QNL HNBBAQ, NEQ CRA OXCCOA JUL ZAEC RUTA, NEQ CRNC ZAAD HNBBAQ,

UEA NC RUTA--EUV ZNB CRAVA NEL UEA NC RUTA--CRA UOQ TNE ZNB QANQ!

XE CRA AKAEXES CRAVA ZNB N RANVBA BAAE JAPUVA CRA QUUV, NEQ RA ZNB JUVEA
XECU XC XE RXB FUPPXE: RA ZNB EUZ CU SU UWC XECU CRA FUWECVL, CU OXA XE

QVXKAE NZNL.

BUTA QNLB NPCAVZNVQB CRAVA ZNB NE NWFCXUE NC CRA UOQ RUWBA, NEQ CRA

JVUDAV'B NSNXE; NEQ CRAVA XC RWES, PUV EU UEA DEAZ RAV TUVA--EU UEA
FNVAQ NJUWC CRA UOQ HXFCWVA.

XE CRA BHVXES CRAL HWOOAQ CRA RUWBA QUZE, PUV, NB HAUHOA BNXQ, XC ZNB
N VWXE. UEA FUWOQ BAA PVUT CRA BCVAAC VXSRC XECU CRA VUUT ZXCR CRA
RUS'B-OANCRAV RNESXES, ZRXFR ZNB BONBRAQ NEQ CUVE; NEQ CRA SVAAE SVNBB

NEQ CRAE XC ZNB HWC CU VXSRCB.

“CRNC ZNB N VAOXAP,” BNXQ CRA EAXSRJUVXES RUWBAB.

N PXEA RUWBA ZNB JWXOC CRAVA, ZXCR ONVSA ZXEQUZB, NEQ BTUUCR ZRXCA
ZNOOB; JWC JAPUVA XC, ZRAVA CRA UOQ RUWBA RNQ XE PNFC BCUUQ, ZNB N
OXCCOA SNVQAE ONXQ UWC, NEQ N ZXOQ SVNHAKXEA VNE WH CRA ZNOO UP CRA
EAXSRJUVXES RUWBA. JAPUVA CRA SNVQAE CRAVA ZNB N ONVSA XVUE VNXOXES
ZXCR NE XVUE QUUV, XC OUUDAQ MWXCA BHOAEQXQ, NEQ HAUHOA BCUUQ BCXOO NEQ
HAAHAQ XE, NEQ CRA BHNVVUZB RWES JL BFUVAB XE CRA KXEA, NEQ FRNCCAVAQ
NZNL NC ANFR UCRAV NB ZAOO NB CRAL FUWOQ, JWC XC ZNB EUC NJUWC CRA UOQ
RUWBA, PUV CRAL FUWOQ EUC VATATJAV XC, BU TNEL LANVB RNQ HNBBAQ--BU TNEL
CRNC CRA OXCCOA JUL RNQ SVUZE WH CU N ZRUOA TNE, LAB, N FOAKAV TNE, NEQ
N HOANBWVA CU RXB HNVAECB; NEQ RA RNQ GWBC JAAE TNVVXAQ, NEQ, CUSACRAV
ZXCR RXB OXCCOA ZXPA, RNQ FUTA CU OXKA XE CRA RUWBA RAVA, ZRAVA CRA
SNVQAE ZNB; NEQ RA BCUUQ JL RAV CRAVA ZRXOBC BRA HONECAQ N PXAOQ-POUZAV
CRNC BRA PUWEQ BU HVACCL; BRA HONECAQ XC ZXCR RAV OXCCOA RNEQ, NEQ
HVABBAQ CRA ANVCR NVUWEQ XC ZXCR RAV PXESAVB. UR! ZRNC ZNB CRNC? BRA
RNQ BCWFD RAVBAOP. CRAVA BNC BUTACRXES HUXECAQ, BCVNXSRC UWC UP CRA BUPC
TUWOQ.

XC ZNB--LAB, SWABB! XC ZNB CRA HAZCAV BUOQXAV, RA CRNC ZNB OUBC WH NC
CRA UOQ TNE'B, NEQ RNQ CWTJOAQ NEQ CWVEAQ NJUWC NTUESBC CRA CXTJAV NEQ
CRA VWJJXBR, NEQ RNQ NC ONBC ONXQ PUV TNEL LANVB XE CRA SVUWEQ.

CRA LUWES ZXPA ZXHAQ CRA QXVC UPP CRA BUOQXAV, PXVBC ZXCR N SVAAE OANP,
NEQ CRAE ZXCR RAV PXEA RNEQDAVFRXAP--XC RNQ BWFR N QAOXSRCPWO BTAOO,
CRNC XC ZNB CU CRA HAZCAV BUOQXAV GWBC NB XP RA RNQ NZNDAQ PVUT N
CVNEFA.

“OAC TA BAA RXT,” BNXQ CRA LUWES TNE. RA ONWSRAQ, NEQ CRAE BRUUD RXB
RANQ. “ENL, XC FNEEUC JA RA; JWC RA VATXEQB TA UP N BCUVL NJUWC N HAZCAV
BUOQXAV ZRXFR X RNQ ZRAE X ZNB N OXCCOA JUL!” NEQ CRAE RA CUOQ RXB ZXPA

UP RXB LUWES ZXPA, UE NFFUWEC UP CRA UOQ RUWBA NEQ CRA UOQ TNE.

“XC TNL HUBBXJOL JA, RUZAKAV, CRNC XC XB CRA BNTA HAZCAV BUOQXAV!” BNXQ
BRA. “X ZXOO CNDA FNVA UP XC, NEQ VATATJAV NOO CRNC LUW RNKA CUOQ TA;
JWC LUW TWBC BRUZ TA CRA UOQ TNE'B SVNKA!”

“JWC X QU EUC DEUZ XC,” BNXQ RA, “NEQ EU UEA DEUZB XC! NOO RXB PVXAEQB
ZAVA QANQ, EU UEA CUUD FNVA UP XC, NEQ X ZNB CRAE N OXCCOA JUL!”

“RUZ KAVL, KAVL OUEAOL RA TWBC RNKA JAAE!” BNXQ BRA.

“KAVL, KAVL OUEAOL!” BNXQ CRA HAZCAV BUOQXAV. “JWC XC XB QAOXSRCPWO EUC
CU JA PUVSUCCAE!”

“QAOXSRCPWO!” BRUWCAQ BUTACRXES FOUBA JL; JWC EU UEA, AIFAHC CRA HAZCAV
BUOQXAV, BNZ CRNC XC ZNB N HXAFA UP CRA RUS'B-OANCRAV RNESXESB; XC RNQ

UHXEXUE, NEQ XC SNKA XC:

   “CRA SXOQXES QAFNLB,
   JWC RUS'B OANCRAV BCNLB!”

CRXB CRA HAZCAV BUOQXAV QXQ EUC JAOXAKA.




CRA RNHHL PNTXOL

VANOOL, CRA ONVSABC SVAAE OANP XE CRXB FUWECVL XB N QUFD-OANP; XP UEA

QUFD-OANKAB, NEQ CRAVAPUVA JWVQUFD BAAQB ZAVA BUZE.

EUZ, CRAVA ZNB NE UOQ TNEUV-RUWBA, ZRAVA CRAL EU OUESAV NCA BENXOB, CRAL

BENXOB.

QXBR.

UEA QNL CRAVA ZNB N RANKL BCUVT UP VNXE.

“ZAOO, CRAE, OAC RAV FUTA CU RXT!” BNXQ CRA UOQ UEAB. “RA RNB N ZRUOA
PUVABC UP JWVQUFDB, BRA RNB UEOL N JWBR!”

NEQ BU CRAL ZAEC NEQ PACFRAQ OXCCOA TXBB BENXO. XC ZNB N ZRUOA ZAAD

CRA BCUVL UP N TUCRAV

N TUCRAV BNC CRAVA ZXCR RAV OXCCOA FRXOQ. BRA ZNB BU QUZEFNBC, BU
NPVNXQ CRNC XC BRUWOQ QXA! XC ZNB BU HNOA, CRA BTNOO ALAB RNQ FOUBAQ
CRATBAOKAB, NEQ XC QVAZ XCB JVANCR BU BUPCOL, EUZ NEQ CRAE, ZXCR N
QAAH VABHXVNCXUE, NB XP XC BXSRAQ; NEQ CRA TUCRAV OUUDAQ BCXOO TUVA
BUVVUZPWOOL UE CRA OXCCOA FVANCWVA.

CRAE N DEUFDXES ZNB RANVQ NC CRA QUUV, NEQ XE FNTA N HUUV UOQ TNE
ZVNHHAQ WH NB XE N ONVSA RUVBA-FOUCR, PUV XC ZNVTB UEA, NEQ RA EAAQAQ
XC, NB XC ZNB CRA FUOQ ZXECAV BANBUE! AKAVLCRXES UWC-UP-QUUVB ZNB
FUKAVAQ ZXCR XFA NEQ BEUZ, NEQ CRA ZXEQ JOAZ BU CRNC XC FWC CRA PNFA.

NB CRA UOQ TNE CVATJOAQ ZXCR FUOQ, NEQ CRA OXCCOA FRXOQ BOAHC N TUTAEC,
CRA TUCRAV ZAEC NEQ HUWVAQ BUTA NOA XECU N HUC NEQ BAC XC UE CRA BCUKA,
CRNC XC TXSRC JA ZNVT PUV RXT; CRA UOQ TNE BNC NEQ VUFDAQ CRA FVNQOA,
NEQ CRA TUCRAV BNC QUZE UE N FRNXV FOUBA JL RXT, NEQ OUUDAQ NC RAV
OXCCOA BXFD FRXOQ CRNC QVAZ XCB JVANCR BU QAAH, NEQ VNXBAQ XCB OXCCOA
RNEQ.

“QU LUW EUC CRXED CRNC X BRNOO BNKA RXT?” BNXQ BRA. “UWV OUVQ ZXOO EUC
CNDA RXT PVUT TA!”

NEQ CRA UOQ TNE--XC ZNB QANCR RXTBAOP--RA EUQQAQ BU BCVNESAOL, XC FUWOQ
GWBC NB ZAOO BXSEXPL LAB NB EU. NEQ CRA TUCRAV OUUDAQ QUZE XE RAV ONH,

JWC UEOL PUV N TXEWCA, ZRAE BRA BCNVCAQ WH NEQ CVATJOAQ ZXCR FUOQ.

“ZRNC XB CRNC?” BNXQ BRA, NEQ OUUDAQ UE NOO BXQAB; JWC CRA UOQ TNE ZNB
SUEA, NEQ RAV OXCCOA FRXOQ ZNB SUEA--RA RNQ CNDAE XC ZXCR RXT; NEQ CRA
UOQ FOUFD XE CRA FUVEAV JWVVAQ, NEQ JWVVAQ, CRA SVANC OANQAE ZAXSRC VNE
QUZE CU CRA POUUV, JWTH! NEQ CRAE CRA FOUFD NOBU BCUUQ BCXOO.

JWC CRA HUUV TUCRAV VNE UWC UP CRA RUWBA NEQ FVXAQ NOUWQ PUV RAV FRXOQ.

UWC CRAVA, XE CRA TXQBC UP CRA BEUZ, CRAVA BNC N ZUTNE XE OUES, JONFD
FOUCRAB; NEQ BRA BNXQ, “QANCR RNB JAAE XE CRL FRNTJAV, NEQ X BNZ RXT

EAKAV JVXESB JNFD ZRNC RA CNDAB!”

“UR, UEOL CAOO TA ZRXFR ZNL RA ZAEC!” BNXQ CRA TUCRAV. “CAOO TA CRA ZNL,
NEQ X BRNOO PXEQ RXT!”

X NT PUEQ UP CRAT. X RNKA RANVQ CRAT JAPUVA; X NT EXSRC; X BNZ CRL CANVB
ZRXOBC CRUW BNES'BC CRAT!”

“X ZXOO BXES CRAT NOO, NOO!” BNXQ CRA TUCRAV. “JWC QU EUC BCUH TA EUZ--X
TNL UKAVCNDA RXT--X TNL PXEQ TL FRXOQ!”

JWC EXSRC BCUUQ BCXOO NEQ TWCA. CRAE CRA TUCRAV ZVWES RAV RNEQB, BNES

CRA VUNQB FVUBBAQ ANFR UCRAV XE CRA QAHCRB UP CRA PUVABC, NEQ BRA EU
OUESAV DEAZ ZRXCRAV BRA BRUWOQ SU! CRAE CRAVA BCUUQ N CRUVE-JWBR;

“LAB,” BNXQ CRA CRUVE-JWBR; “JWC X ZXOO EUC CAOO CRAA ZRXFR ZNL RA CUUD,
WEOABB CRUW ZXOC PXVBC ZNVT TA WH NC CRL RANVC. X NT PVAAYXES CU QANCR;

NEQ BRA HVABBAQ CRA CRUVE-JWBR CU RAV JVANBC, BU PXVTOL, CRNC XC TXSRC

BRA CRAE FNTA CU N ONVSA ONDA, ZRAVA CRAVA ZNB EAXCRAV BRXH EUV JUNC.
CRA ONDA ZNB EUC PVUYAE BWPPXFXAECOL CU JANV RAV; EAXCRAV ZNB XC UHAE,

JWXOC WH; JWC CRA HUUV TUCRAV FUWOQ EUC BAA XC; BRA RNQ ZAHC RAV ALAB
UWC.

“ZRAVA BRNOO X PXEQ QANCR, ZRU CUUD NZNL TL OXCCOA FRXOQ?” BNXQ BRA.

“RA RNB EUC FUTA RAVA LAC!” BNXQ CRA UOQ SVNKA ZUTNE, ZRU ZNB NHHUXECAQ
CU OUUD NPCAV QANCR'B SVANC SVAAERUWBA! “RUZ RNKA LUW JAAE NJOA CU PXEQ
CRA ZNL RXCRAV? NEQ ZRU RNB RAOHAQ LUW?”

“UWV OUVQ RNB RAOHAQ TA,” BNXQ BRA. “RA XB TAVFXPWO, NEQ LUW ZXOO NOBU
JA BU! ZRAVA BRNOO X PXEQ TL OXCCOA FRXOQ?”

“ENL, X DEUZ EUC,” BNXQ CRA ZUTNE, “NEQ LUW FNEEUC BAA! TNEL POUZAVB NEQ
CVAAB RNKA ZXCRAVAQ CRXB EXSRC; QANCR ZXOO BUUE FUTA NEQ HONEC CRAT UKAV
NSNXE! LUW FAVCNXEOL DEUZ CRNC AKAVL HAVBUE RNB RXB UV RAV OXPA'B CVAA
UV POUZAV, GWBC NB AKAVLUEA RNHHAEB CU JA BACCOAQ; CRAL OUUD OXDA UCRAV
HONECB, JWC CRAL RNKA HWOBNCXUEB UP CRA RANVC. FRXOQVAE'B RANVCB FNE
NOBU JANC; SU NPCAV LUWVB, HAVRNHB LUW TNL DEUZ LUWV FRXOQ'B; JWC ZRNC
ZXOO LUW SXKA TA XP X CAOO LUW ZRNC LUW BRNOO QU TUVA?”

“X RNKA EUCRXES CU SXKA,” BNXQ CRA NPPOXFCAQ TUCRAV, “JWC X ZXOO SU CU
CRA ZUVOQ'B AEQ PUV LUW!”

“ENL, X RNKA EUCRXES CU QU CRAVA!” BNXQ CRA ZUTNE. “JWC LUW FNE SXKA
TA LUWV OUES JONFD RNXV; LUW DEUZ LUWVBAOP CRNC XC XB PXEA, NEQ CRNC
X OXDA! LUW BRNOO RNKA TL ZRXCA RNXV XEBCANQ, NEQ CRNC'B NOZNLB
BUTACRXES!”

“QU LUW QATNEQ EUCRXES AOBA?” BNXQ BRA. “CRNC X ZXOO SONQOL SXKA LUW!”
 NEQ BRA SNKA RAV RAV PXEA JONFD RNXV, NEQ SUC CRA UOQ ZUTNE'B BEUZ-ZRXCA
RNXV XEBCANQ.

BU CRAL ZAEC XECU QANCR'B SVANC SVAAERUWBA, ZRAVA POUZAVB NEQ CVAAB
SVAZ BCVNESAOL XECU UEA NEUCRAV. CRAVA BCUUQ PXEA RLNFXECRB WEQAV SONBB
JAOOB, NEQ CRAVA BCUUQ BCVUES-BCATTAQ HAUEXAB; CRAVA SVAZ ZNCAV HONECB,
BUTA BU PVABR, UCRAVB RNOP BXFD, CRA ZNCAV-BENDAB ONL QUZE UE CRAT,
NEQ JONFD FVNJB HXEFRAQ CRAXV BCNODB. CRAVA BCUUQ JANWCXPWO HNOT-CVAAB,
UNDB, NEQ HONECNXEB; CRAVA BCUUQ HNVBOAL NEQ POUZAVXES CRLTA: AKAVL CVAA
NEQ AKAVL POUZAV RNQ XCB ENTA; ANFR UP CRAT ZNB N RWTNE OXPA, CRA RWTNE
PVNTA BCXOO OXKAQ--UEA XE FRXEN, NEQ NEUCRAV XE SVAAEONEQ--VUWEQ NJUWC
XE CRA ZUVOQ. CRAVA ZAVA ONVSA CVAAB XE BTNOO HUCB, BU CRNC CRAL BCUUQ
BU BCWECAQ XE SVUZCR, NEQ VANQL CU JWVBC CRA HUCB; XE UCRAV HONFAB,
CRAVA ZNB N OXCCOA QWOO POUZAV XE VXFR TUWOQ, ZXCR TUBB VUWEQ NJUWC XC,
NEQ XC ZNB BU HACCAQ NEQ EWVBAQ. JWC CRA QXBCVABBAQ TUCRAV JAEC QUZE
UKAV NOO CRA BTNOOABC HONECB, NEQ RANVQ ZXCRXE CRAT RUZ CRA RWTNE RANVC
JANC; NEQ NTUESBC TXOOXUEB BRA DEAZ RAV FRXOQ'B.

“CRAVA XC XB!” FVXAQ BRA, NEQ BCVACFRAQ RAV RNEQB UWC UKAV N OXCCOA JOWA
FVUFWB, CRNC RWES MWXCA BXFDOL UE UEA BXQA.

“QUE'C CUWFR CRA POUZAV!” BNXQ CRA UOQ ZUTNE. “JWC HONFA LUWVBAOP RAVA,
NEQ ZRAE QANCR FUTAB--X AIHAFC RXT AKAVL TUTAEC--QU EUC OAC RXT HOWFD
CRA POUZAV WH, JWC CRVANCAE RXT CRNC LUW ZXOO QU CRA BNTA ZXCR CRA
UCRAVB. CRAE RA ZXOO JA NPVNXQ! RA XB VABHUEBXJOA PUV CRAT CU UWV OUVQ,
NEQ EU UEA QNVAB CU HOWFD CRAT WH JAPUVA RA SXKAB OANKA.”

NOO NC UEFA NE XFL FUOQ VWBRAQ CRVUWSR CRA SVANC RNOO, NEQ CRA JOXEQ
TUCRAV FUWOQ PAAO CRNC XC ZNB QANCR CRNC FNTA.

“RUZ RNBC CRUW JAAE NJOA CU PXEQ CRL ZNL RXCRAV?” RA NBDAQ. “RUZ FUWOQBC
CRUW FUTA MWXFDAV CRNE X?”

“X NT N TUCRAV,” BNXQ BRA.

NEQ QANCR BCVACFRAQ UWC RXB OUES RNEQ CUZNVQB CRA PXEA OXCCOA POUZAV,
JWC BRA RAOQ RAV RNEQB PNBC NVUWEQ RXB, BU CXSRC, NEQ LAC NPVNXQ CRNC
BRA BRUWOQ CUWFR UEA UP CRA OANKAB. CRAE QANCR JOAZ UE RAV RNEQB, NEQ
BRA PAOC CRNC XC ZNB FUOQAV CRNE CRA FUOQ ZXEQ, NEQ RAV RNEQB PAOO QUZE
HUZAVOABB.

“CRUW FNEBC EUC QU NELCRXES NSNXEBC TA!” BNXQ QANCR.

“JWC UWV OUVQ FNE!” BNXQ BRA.

“X UEOL QU RXB JXQQXES!” BNXQ QANCR. “X NT RXB SNVQAEAV, X CNDA NOO RXB
POUZAVB NEQ CVAAB, NEQ HONEC CRAT UWC XE CRA SVANC SNVQAE UP HNVNQXBA,
XE CRA WEDEUZE ONEQ; JWC RUZ CRAL SVUZ CRAVA, NEQ RUZ XC XB CRAVA X QNVA
EUC CAOO CRAA.”

“SXKA TA JNFD TL FRXOQ!” BNXQ CRA TUCRAV, NEQ BRA ZAHC NEQ HVNLAQ. NC

QABHNXV.”

“CUWFR CRAT EUC!” BNXQ QANCR. “CRUW BNL'BC CRNC CRUW NVC BU WERNHHL, NEQ
EUZ CRUW ZXOC TNDA NEUCRAV TUCRAV AMWNOOL WERNHHL.”

“NEUCRAV TUCRAV!” BNXQ CRA HUUV ZUTNE, NEQ QXVAFCOL OAC SU RAV RUOQ UP
JUCR CRA POUZAVB.

“CRAVA, CRUW RNBC CRXEA ALAB,” BNXQ QANCR; “X PXBRAQ CRAT WH PVUT CRA
ONDA, CRAL BRUEA BU JVXSRC; X DEAZ EUC CRAL ZAVA CRXEA. CNDA CRAT NSNXE,
CRAL NVA EUZ JVXSRCAV CRNE JAPUVA; EUZ OUUD QUZE XECU CRA QAAH ZAOO
FOUBA JL; X BRNOO CAOO CRAA CRA ENTAB UP CRA CZU POUZAVB CRUW ZUWOQBC

RWTNE AIXBCAEFA: NEQ BAA ZRNC CRUW ZNBC NJUWC CU QXBCWVJ NEQ QABCVUL.”

NEQ BRA OUUDAQ QUZE XECU CRA ZAOO; NEQ XC ZNB N RNHHXEABB CU BAA RUZ CRA
UEA JAFNTA N JOABBXES CU CRA ZUVOQ, CU BAA RUZ TWFR RNHHXEABB NEQ GUL
ZAVA PAOC AKAVLZRAVA. NEQ BRA BNZ CRA UCRAV'B OXPA, NEQ XC ZNB BUVVUZ
NEQ QXBCVABB, RUVVUV, NEQ ZVACFRAQEABB.

“JUCR UP CRAT NVA SUQ'B ZXOO!” BNXQ QANCR.

“ZRXFR UP CRAT XB TXBPUVCWEA'B POUZAV NEQ ZRXFR XB CRNC UP RNHHXEABB?”
 NBDAQ BRA.

“CRNC X ZXOO EUC CAOO CRAA,” BNXQ QANCR; “JWC CRXB CRUW BRNOC DEUZ PVUT
TA, CRNC CRA UEA POUZAV ZNB CRL UZE FRXOQ! XC ZNB CRL FRXOQ'B PNCA CRUW
BNZ'BC--CRL UZE FRXOQ'B PWCWVA OXPA!”

CRAE CRA TUCRAV BFVANTAQ ZXCR CAVVUV, “ZRXFR UP CRAT ZNB TL FRXOQ? CAOO
XC TA! BNKA CRA XEEUFAEC! BNKA TL FRXOQ PVUT NOO CRNC TXBAVL! VNCRAV
CNDA XC NZNL! CNDA XC XECU SUQ'B DXESQUT! PUVSAC TL CANVB, PUVSAC TL
HVNLAVB, NEQ NOO CRNC X RNKA QUEA!”

“X QU EUC WEQAVBCNEQ CRAA!” BNXQ QANCR. “ZXOC CRUW RNKA CRL FRXOQ NSNXE,
UV BRNOO X SU ZXCR XC CRAVA, ZRAVA CRUW QUBC EUC DEUZ!”

CRAE CRA TUCRAV ZVWES RAV RNEQB, PAOO UE RAV DEAAB, NEQ HVNLAQ CU UWV
OUVQ: “UR, RANV TA EUC ZRAE X HVNL NSNXEBC CRL ZXOO, ZRXFR XB CRA JABC!
RANV TA EUC! RANV TA EUC!”

NEQ BRA JUZAQ RAV RANQ QUZE XE RAV ONH, NEQ QANCR CUUD RAV FRXOQ NEQ

CRA PNOBA FUOONV

CRAVA ZNB UEFA N PXEA SAECOATNE, NOO UP ZRUBA TUKANJOAB ZAVA N JUUC-GNFD

XC ZNB BU UOQ, CRNC XC JASNE CU CRXED UP TNVVXNSA; NEQ XC RNHHAEAQ CRNC
XC FNTA CU JA ZNBRAQ XE FUTHNEL ZXCR N SNVCAV.

“ENL!” BNXQ CRA FUOONV. “X EAKAV QXQ BAA NELCRXES BU BOAEQAV NEQ BU
PXEA, BU BUPC NEQ BU EANC. TNL X EUC NBD LUWV ENTA?”

“CRNC X BRNOO EUC CAOO LUW!” BNXQ CRA SNVCAV.

“ZRAVA QU LUW OXKA?” NBDAQ CRA FUOONV.

JWC CRA SNVCAV ZNB BU JNBRPWO, BU TUQABC, NEQ CRUWSRC XC ZNB N BCVNESA

ONQL.”

UFFNBXUE AEUWSR.”

“QUE'C FUTA BU EANV TA, X JAS UP LUW!” BNXQ CRA SNVCAV. “LUW OUUD BU
TWFR OXDA CRUBA TAE-PUODB.”

“X NT NOBU N PXEA SAECOATNE,” BNXQ CRA FUOONV. “X RNKA N JUUCGNFD NEQ N
RNXV-FUTJ.”

JWC CRNC ZNB EUC CVWA, PUV XC ZNB RXB TNBCAV ZRU RNQ CRAT: JWC RA
JUNBCAQ.

“QUE'C FUTA BU EANV TA,” BNXQ CRA SNVCAV: “X NT EUC NFFWBCUTAQ CU XC.”

“VNS!” BNXQ CRA JUI-XVUE; NEQ ZAEC HVUWQOL UKAV CRA FUOONV: PUV BRA

CRA FUOONV ZNB N OXCCOA GNSSAQ NC CRA AQSA, NEQ BU FNTA CRA OUES

XTXCNCA LUW.”

“X DEUZ XC,” BNXQ CRA BFXBBUVB.

“LUW QABAVKA CU JA N JNVUEABB,” BNXQ CRA FUOONV. “NOO CRNC X RNKA XB N
PXEA SAECOATNE, N JUUC-GNFD, NEQ N RNXV-FUTJ. XP X UEOL RNQ CRA JNVUEL!”

“QU LUW BAAD TL RNEQ?” BNXQ CRA BFXBBUVB; PUV BRA ZNB NESVL; NEQ ZXCRUWC
TUVA NQU, BRA FWC RXT, NEQ CRAE RA ZNB FUEQATEAQ.

“X BRNOO EUZ JA UJOXSAQ CU NBD CRA RNXV-FUTJ. XC XB BWVHVXBXES RUZ ZAOO

“LAB, UP FUWVBA! LUW TNL JA BWVA UP CRNC,” BNXQ CRA RNXV-FUTJ. “X NT
JACVUCRAQ--CU CRA JUUC-GNFD!”

“JACVUCRAQ!” AIFONXTAQ CRA FUOONV. EUZ CRAVA ZNB EU UCRAV CU FUWVC, NEQ

N OUES CXTA HNBBAQ NZNL, CRAE CRA FUOONV FNTA XECU CRA VNS FRABC NC CRA
HNHAV TXOO; CRAVA ZNB N ONVSA FUTHNEL UP VNSB, CRA PXEA JL CRATBAOKAB,

“X RNKA RNQ BWFR NE XTTAEBA EWTJAV UP BZAACRANVCB!” BNXQ CRA FUOONV.
“X FUWOQ EUC JA XE HANFA! XC XB CVWA, X ZNB NOZNLB N PXEA BCNVFRAQ-WH
SAECOATNE! X RNQ JUCR N JUUC-GNFD NEQ N RNXV-FUTJ, ZRXFR X EAKAV WBAQ!
LUW BRUWOQ RNKA BAAE TA CRAE, LUW BRUWOQ RNKA BAAE TA ZRAE X ONL QUZE!
X BRNOO EAKAV PUVSAC TL PXVBC OUKA--BRA ZNB N SXVQOA, BU PXEA, BU BUPC,
NEQ BU FRNVTXES, BRA CRVAZ RAVBAOP XECU N CWJ UP ZNCAV PUV TL BNDA!
CRAVA ZNB NOBU N ZXQUZ, ZRU JAFNTA SOUZXES RUC, JWC X OAPC RAV BCNEQXES
CXOO BRA SUC JONFD NSNXE; CRAVA ZNB NOBU CRA PXVBC UHAVN QNEFAV, BRA
SNKA TA CRNC FWC ZRXFR X EUZ SU ZXCR, BRA ZNB BU PAVUFXUWB! TL
UZE RNXV-FUTJ ZNB XE OUKA ZXCR TA, BRA OUBC NOO RAV CAACR PVUT CRA
RANVC-NFRA; LAB, X RNKA OXKAQ CU BAA TWFR UP CRNC BUVC UP CRXES; JWC X
NT AICVATAOL BUVVL PUV CRA SNVCAV--X TANE CRA SXVQOA--CRNC ZAEC XECU CRA
ZNCAV-CWJ. X RNKA TWFR UE TL FUEBFXAEFA, X ZNEC CU JAFUTA ZRXCA HNHAV!”

NEQ XC JAFNTA BU, NOO CRA VNSB ZAVA CWVEAQ XECU ZRXCA HNHAV; JWC CRA
FUOONV FNTA CU JA GWBC CRXB KAVL HXAFA UP ZRXCA HNHAV ZA RAVA BAA,
NEQ UE ZRXFR CRA BCUVL XB HVXECAQ; NEQ CRNC ZNB JAFNWBA XC JUNBCAQ BU
CAVVXJOL NPCAVZNVQB UP ZRNC RNQ EAKAV RNHHAEAQ CU XC. XC ZUWOQ JA ZAOO
PUV WB CU JAZNVA, CRNC ZA TNL EUC NFC XE N BXTXONV TNEEAV, PUV ZA FNE
EAKAV DEUZ XP ZA TNL EUC, XE CRA FUWVBA UP CXTA, NOBU FUTA XECU CRA
VNS FRABC, NEQ JA TNQA XECU ZRXCA HNHAV, NEQ CRAE RNKA UWV ZRUOA OXPA'B
RXBCUVL HVXECAQ UE XC, AKAE CRA TUBC BAFVAC, NEQ JA UJOXSAQ CU VWE NJUWC
NEQ CAOO XC UWVBAOKAB, GWBC OXDA CRXB FUOONV.




CRA BRNQUZ

XC XB XE CRA RUC ONEQB CRNC CRA BWE JWVEB, BWVA AEUWSR! CRAVA CRA HAUHOA
JAFUTA MWXCA N TNRUSNEL JVUZE, NL, NEQ XE CRA RUCCABC ONEQB CRAL NVA
JWVEC CU EASVUAB. JWC EUZ XC ZNB UEOL CU CRA RUC ONEQB CRNC N OANVEAQ
TNE RNQ FUTA PVUT CRA FUOQ; CRAVA RA CRUWSRC CRNC RA FUWOQ VWE NJUWC
GWBC NB ZRAE NC RUTA, JWC RA BUUE PUWEQ UWC RXB TXBCNDA.

RA, NEQ NOO BAEBXJOA PUODB, ZAVA UJOXSAQ CU BCNL ZXCRXE QUUVB--CRA
ZXEQUZ-BRWCCAVB NEQ QUUVB ZAVA FOUBAQ CRA ZRUOA QNL; XC OUUDAQ NB XP CRA
ZRUOA RUWBA BOAHC, UV CRAVA ZNB EU UEA NC RUTA.

CRA ENVVUZ BCVAAC ZXCR CRA RXSR RUWBAB, ZNB JWXOC BU CRNC CRA BWEBRXEA
TWBC PNOO CRAVA PVUT TUVEXES CXOO AKAEXES--XC ZNB VANOOL EUC CU JA
JUVEA.

CRA OANVEAQ TNE PVUT CRA FUOQ ONEQB--RA ZNB N LUWES TNE, NEQ BAATAQ CU
JA N FOAKAV TNE--BNC XE N SOUZXES UKAE; XC CUUD APPAFC UE RXT, RA JAFNTA
MWXCA TANSVA--AKAE RXB BRNQUZ BRVWED XE, PUV CRA BWE RNQ NOBU NE APPAFC
UE XC. XC ZNB PXVBC CUZNVQB AKAEXES ZRAE CRA BWE ZNB QUZE, CRNC CRAL
JASNE CU PVABRAE WH NSNXE.

XE CRA ZNVT ONEQB AKAVL ZXEQUZ RNB N JNOFUEL, NEQ CRA HAUHOA FNTA UWC UE
NOO CRA JNOFUEXAB XE CRA BCVAAC--PUV UEA TWBC RNKA NXV, AKAE XP UEA JA
NFFWBCUTAQ CU JA TNRUSNEL!* XC ZNB OXKAOL JUCR WH NEQ QUZE CRA
BCVAAC. CNXOUVB, NEQ BRUATNDAVB, NEQ NOO CRA PUODB, TUKAQ UWC XECU CRA
BCVAAC--FRNXVB NEQ CNJOAB ZAVA JVUWSRC PUVCR--NEQ FNEQOAB JWVEC--LAB,
NJUKA N CRUWBNEQ OXSRCB ZAVA JWVEXES--NEQ CRA UEA CNODAQ NEQ CRA UCRAV
BWES; NEQ HAUHOA ZNODAQ NEQ FRWVFR-JAOOB VNES, NEQ NBBAB ZAEC NOUES ZXCR
N QXESOA-QXESOA-QUES! PUV CRAL CUU RNQ JAOOB UE. CRA BCVAAC JULB ZAVA
BFVANTXES NEQ RUUCXES, NEQ BRUWCXES NEQ BRUUCXES, ZXCR QAKXOB NEQ
QACUENCXES JNOOB--NEQ CRAVA FNTA FUVHBA JANVAVB NEQ RUUQ ZANVAVB--PUV
CRAVA ZAVA PWEAVNOB ZXCR HBNOT NEQ RLTE--NEQ CRAE CRA QXE UP FNVVXNSAB
QVXKXES NEQ FUTHNEL NVVXKXES: LAB, XC ZNB, XE CVWCR, OXKAOL AEUWSR QUZE
XE CRA BCVAAC. UEOL XE CRNC BXESOA RUWBA, ZRXFR BCUUQ UHHUBXCA CRNC XE
ZRXFR CRA OANVEAQ PUVAXSEAV OXKAQ, XC ZNB MWXCA BCXOO; NEQ LAC BUTA UEA
OXKAQ CRAVA, PUV CRAVA BCUUQ POUZAVB XE CRA JNOFUEL--CRAL SVAZ BU
ZAOO XE CRA BWE'B RANC! NEQ CRNC CRAL FUWOQ EUC QU WEOABB CRAL ZAVA
ZNCAVAQ--NEQ BUTA UEA TWBC ZNCAV CRAT--CRAVA TWBC JA BUTAJUQL CRAVA.
CRA QUUV UHHUBXCA ZNB NOBU UHAEAQ ONCA XE CRA AKAEXES, JWC XC ZNB QNVD
ZXCRXE, NC OANBC XE CRA PVUEC VUUT; PWVCRAV XE CRAVA ZNB RANVQ CRA BUWEQ
UP TWBXF. CRA OANVEAQ PUVAXSEAV CRUWSRC XC MWXCA TNVKAOOUWB, JWC EUZ--XC
TXSRC JA CRNC RA UEOL XTNSXEAQ XC--PUV RA PUWEQ AKAVLCRXES TNVKAOOUWB
UWC CRAVA, XE CRA ZNVT ONEQB, XP CRAVA RNQ UEOL JAAE EU BWE. CRA
BCVNESAV'B ONEQOUVQ BNXQ CRNC RA QXQE'C DEUZ ZRU RNQ CNDAE CRA RUWBA
UHHUBXCA, UEA BNZ EU HAVBUE NJUWC, NEQ NB CU CRA TWBXF, XC NHHANVAQ
CU RXT CU JA AICVATAOL CXVABUTA. “XC XB NB XP BUTA UEA BNC CRAVA, NEQ
HVNFCXBAQ N HXAFA CRNC RA FUWOQ EUC TNBCAV--NOZNLB CRA BNTA HXAFA. 'X
BRNOO TNBCAV XC!' BNLB RA; JWC LAC RA FNEEUC TNBCAV XC, RUZAKAV OUES RA
HONLB.”

* CRA ZUVQ TNRUSNEL FNE JA WEQAVBCUUQ, XE QNEXBR, NB RNKXES CZU
TANEXESB. XE SAEAVNO, XC TANEB CRA VAQQXBR-JVUZE ZUUQ XCBAOP; JWC XE
GABC, XC BXSEXPXAB “AIFABBXKAOL PXEA,” ZRXFR NVUBA PVUT NE NEAFQUCA UP
ELJUQAV, XE FUHAERNSAE, (CRA BANTAE'B MWNVCAV.) N BNXOUV'B ZXPA, ZRU ZNB
NOZNLB HVUWQ NEQ PXEA, XE RAV ZNL, FNTA CU RAV EAXSRJUV, NEQ FUTHONXEAQ
CRNC BRA RNQ SUC N BHOXECAV XE RAV PXESAV. “ZRNC UP?” NBDAQ CRA
EAXSRJUV'B ZXPA. “XC XB N TNRUSNEL BHOXECAV,” BNXQ CRA UCRAV. “TNRUSNEL!
XC FNEEUC JA OABB ZXCR LUW!” AIFONXTAQ CRA ZUTNE--NEQ CRAEFA CRA
HVUKAVJ, “XC XB BU TNRUSNEL!”--(CRNC XB, BU AIFABBXKAOL PXEA)--XB
QAVXKAQ.


UEA EXSRC CRA BCVNESAV NZUDA--RA BOAHC ZXCR CRA QUUVB UP CRA JNOFUEL
UHAE--CRA FWVCNXE JAPUVA XC ZNB VNXBAQ JL CRA ZXEQ, NEQ RA CRUWSRC
CRNC N BCVNESA OWBCVA FNTA PVUT CRA UHHUBXCA EAXSRJUV'B RUWBA; NOO CRA
POUZAVB BRUEA OXDA PONTAB, XE CRA TUBC JANWCXPWO FUOUVB, NEQ XE CRA
TXQBC UP CRA POUZAVB BCUUQ N BOAEQAV, SVNFAPWO TNXQAE--XC ZNB NB XP BRA
NOBU BRUEA; CRA OXSRC VANOOL RWVC RXB ALAB. RA EUZ UHAEAQ CRAT MWXCA
ZXQA--LAB, RA ZNB MWXCA NZNDA; ZXCR UEA BHVXES RA ZNB UE CRA POUUV; RA
FVAHC SAECOL JARXEQ CRA FWVCNXE, JWC CRA TNXQAE ZNB SUEA; CRA POUZAVB
BRUEA EU OUESAV, JWC CRAVA CRAL BCUUQ, PVABR NEQ JOUUTXES NB AKAV;
CRA QUUV ZNB NGNV, NEQ, PNV ZXCRXE, CRA TWBXF BUWEQAQ BU BUPC NEQ
QAOXSRCPWO, UEA FUWOQ VANOOL TAOC NZNL XE BZAAC CRUWSRCB PVUT XC. LAC
XC ZNB OXDA N HXAFA UP AEFRNECTAEC. NEQ ZRU OXKAQ CRAVA? ZRAVA ZNB CRA
NFCWNO AECVNEFA? CRA ZRUOA UP CRA SVUWEQ-POUUV ZNB N VUZ UP BRUHB, NEQ
CRAVA HAUHOA FUWOQ EUC NOZNLB JA VWEEXES CRVUWSR.

UEA AKAEXES CRA BCVNESAV BNC UWC UE CRA JNOFUEL. CRA OXSRC JWVEC XE CRA
VUUT JARXEQ RXT; NEQ CRWB XC ZNB MWXCA ENCWVNO CRNC RXB BRNQUZ BRUWOQ
PNOO UE RXB UHHUBXCA EAXSRJUV'B ZNOO. LAB! CRAVA XC BNC, QXVAFCOL
UHHUBXCA, JACZAAE CRA POUZAVB UE CRA JNOFUEL; NEQ ZRAE CRA BCVNESAV
TUKAQ, CRA BRNQUZ NOBU TUKAQ: PUV CRNC XC NOZNLB QUAB.

“X CRXED TL BRNQUZ XB CRA UEOL OXKXES CRXES UEA BAAB UKAV CRAVA,” BNXQ
CRA OANVEAQ TNE. “BAA, RUZ EXFAOL XC BXCB JACZAAE CRA POUZAVB. CRA QUUV
BCNEQB RNOP-UHAE: EUZ CRA BRNQUZ BRUWOQ JA FWEEXES, NEQ SU XECU CRA
VUUT, OUUD NJUWC, NEQ CRAE FUTA NEQ CAOO TA ZRNC XC RNQ BAAE. FUTA, EUZ!
JA WBAPWO, NEQ QU TA N BAVKXFA,” BNXQ RA, XE GABC. “RNKA CRA DXEQEABB CU
BCAH XE. EUZ! NVC CRUW SUXES?” NEQ CRAE RA EUQQAQ CU CRA BRNQUZ, NEQ CRA
BRNQUZ EUQQAQ NSNXE. “ZAOO CRAE, SU! JWC QUE'C BCNL NZNL.”

CRA BCVNESAV VUBA, NEQ RXB BRNQUZ UE CRA UHHUBXCA EAXSRJUV'B JNOFUEL
VUBA NOBU; CRA BCVNESAV CWVEAQ VUWEQ NEQ CRA BRNQUZ NOBU CWVEAQ VUWEQ.
LAB! XP NELUEA RNQ HNXQ HNVCXFWONV NCCAECXUE CU XC, CRAL ZUWOQ RNKA
BAAE, MWXCA QXBCXEFCOL, CRNC CRA BRNQUZ ZAEC XE CRVUWSR CRA RNOP-UHAE
JNOFUEL-QUUV UP CRAXV UHHUBXCA EAXSRJUV, GWBC NB CRA BCVNESAV ZAEC XECU
RXB UZE VUUT, NEQ OAC CRA OUES FWVCNXE PNOO QUZE NPCAV RXT.

EAIC TUVEXES, CRA OANVEAQ TNE ZAEC UWC CU QVXED FUPPAA NEQ VANQ CRA
EAZBHNHAVB.

“ZRNC XB CRNC?” BNXQ RA, NB RA FNTA UWC XECU CRA BWEBRXEA. “X RNKA EU
BRNQUZ! BU CRAE, XC RNB NFCWNOOL SUEA ONBC EXSRC, NEQ EUC FUTA NSNXE. XC
XB VANOOL CXVABUTA!”

CRXB NEEULAQ RXT: EUC BU TWFR JAFNWBA CRA BRNQUZ ZNB SUEA, JWC JAFNWBA
RA DEAZ CRAVA ZNB N BCUVL NJUWC N TNE ZXCRUWC N BRNQUZ.* XC ZNB DEUZE
CU AKAVLJUQL NC RUTA, XE CRA FUOQ ONEQB; NEQ XP CRA OANVEAQ TNE EUZ FNTA
CRAVA NEQ CUOQ RXB BCUVL, CRAL ZUWOQ BNL CRNC RA ZNB XTXCNCXES XC, NEQ
CRNC RA RNQ EU EAAQ CU QU. RA ZUWOQ, CRAVAPUVA, EUC CNOD NJUWC XC NC
NOO; NEQ CRNC ZNB ZXBAOL CRUWSRC.

*HACAV BFROATXRO, CRA BRNQUZOABB TNE.


XE CRA AKAEXES RA ZAEC UWC NSNXE UE CRA JNOFUEL. RA RNQ HONFAQ CRA OXSRC
QXVAFCOL JARXEQ RXT, PUV RA DEAZ CRNC CRA BRNQUZ ZUWOQ NOZNLB RNKA XCB
TNBCAV PUV N BFVAAE, JWC RA FUWOQ EUC AECXFA XC. RA TNQA RXTBAOP OXCCOA;
RA TNQA RXTBAOP SVANC: JWC EU BRNQUZ FNTA NSNXE. RA BNXQ, “RAT! RAT!”
 JWC XC ZNB UP EU WBA.

XC ZNB KAINCXUWB; JWC XE CRA ZNVT ONEQB AKAVLCRXES SVUZB BU MWXFDOL; NEQ
NPCAV CRA ONHBA UP AXSRC QNLB RA UJBAVKAQ, CU RXB SVANC GUL, CRNC N EAZ
BRNQUZ FNTA XE CRA BWEBRXEA. XE CRA FUWVBA UP CRVAA ZAADB RA RNQ N KAVL
PNXV BRNQUZ, ZRXFR, ZRAE RA BAC UWC PUV RXB RUTA XE CRA EUVCRAVE ONEQB,
SVAZ TUVA NEQ TUVA XE CRA GUWVEAL, BU CRNC NC ONBC XC ZNB BU OUES NEQ BU
ONVSA, CRNC XC ZNB TUVA CRNE BWPPXFXAEC.

CRA OANVEAQ TNE CRAE FNTA RUTA, NEQ RA ZVUCA JUUDB NJUWC ZRNC ZNB CVWA
XE CRA ZUVOQ, NEQ NJUWC ZRNC ZNB SUUQ NEQ ZRNC ZNB JANWCXPWO; NEQ CRAVA
HNBBAQ QNLB NEQ LANVB--LAB! TNEL LANVB HNBBAQ NZNL.

UEA AKAEXES, NB RA ZNB BXCCXES XE RXB VUUT, CRAVA ZNB N SAECOA DEUFDXES
NC CRA QUUV.

“FUTA XE!” BNXQ RA; JWC EU UEA FNTA XE; BU RA UHAEAQ CRA QUUV, NEQ CRAVA
BCUUQ JAPUVA RXT BWFR NE AICVATAOL OANE TNE, CRNC RA PAOC MWXCA BCVNESA.
NB CU CRA VABC, CRA TNE ZNB KAVL PXEAOL QVABBAQ--RA TWBC JA N SAECOATNE.

“ZRUT RNKA X CRA RUEUV UP BHANDXES?” NBDAQ CRA OANVEAQ TNE.

“LAB! X CRUWSRC NB TWFR,” BNXQ CRA PXEA TNE. “X CRUWSRC LUW ZUWOQ EUC
DEUZ TA. X RNKA SUC BU TWFR JUQL. X RNKA AKAE SUC POABR NEQ FOUCRAB. LUW
FAVCNXEOL EAKAV CRUWSRC UP BAAXES TA BU ZAOO UPP. QU LUW EUC DEUZ LUWV
UOQ BRNQUZ? LUW FAVCNXEOL CRUWSRC X BRUWOQ EAKAV TUVA VACWVE. CRXESB
RNKA SUEA UE ZAOO ZXCR TA BXEFA X ZNB ONBC ZXCR LUW. X RNKA, XE NOO
VABHAFCB, JAFUTA KAVL ZAOO UPP. BRNOO X HWVFRNBA TL PVAAQUT PVUT
BAVKXFA? XP BU, X FNE QU XC”; NEQ CRAE RA VNCCOAQ N ZRUOA JWEFR UP
KNOWNJOA BANOB CRNC RWES CU RXB ZNCFR, NEQ RA BCWFD RXB RNEQ XE CRA
CRXFD SUOQ FRNXE RA ZUVA NVUWEQ RXB EAFD--ENL! RUZ NOO RXB PXESAVB
SOXCCAVAQ ZXCR QXNTUEQ VXESB; NEQ CRAE NOO ZAVA HWVA SATB.

“ENL; X FNEEUC VAFUKAV PVUT TL BWVHVXBA!” BNXQ CRA OANVEAQ TNE. “ZRNC XB
CRA TANEXES UP NOO CRXB?”

“BUTACRXES FUTTUE, XB XC EUC,” BNXQ CRA BRNQUZ. “JWC LUW LUWVBAOP QU EUC
JAOUES CU CRA FUTTUE UVQAV; NEQ X, NB LUW DEUZ ZAOO, RNKA PVUT N FRXOQ
PUOOUZAQ XE LUWV PUUCBCAHB. NB BUUE NB LUW PUWEQ X ZNB FNHNJOA CU SU
UWC NOUEA XE CRA ZUVOQ, X ZAEC TL UZE ZNL. X NT XE CRA TUBC JVXOOXNEC
FXVFWTBCNEFAB, JWC CRAVA FNTA N BUVC UP QABXVA UKAV TA CU BAA LUW UEFA
TUVA JAPUVA LUW QXA; LUW ZXOO QXA, X BWHHUBA? X NOBU ZXBRAQ CU BAA CRXB
ONEQ NSNXE--PUV LUW DEUZ ZA NOZNLB OUKA UWV ENCXKA ONEQ. X DEUZ LUW RNKA
SUC NEUCRAV BRNQUZ NSNXE; RNKA X NELCRXES CU HNL CU XC UV LUW? XP BU,
LUW ZXOO UJOXSA TA JL BNLXES ZRNC XC XB.”

“ENL, XB XC VANOOL CRUW?” BNXQ CRA OANVEAQ TNE. “XC XB TUBC VATNVDNJOA:
X EAKAV XTNSXEAQ CRNC UEA'B UOQ BRNQUZ FUWOQ FUTA NSNXE NB N TNE.”

XE NEL BUVC UP QAJC.”

“RUZ FNEBC CRUW CNOD BU?” BNXQ CRA OANVEAQ TNE. “ZRNC QAJC XB CRAVA CU
CNOD NJUWC? TNDA CRLBAOP NB PVAA NB NELUEA AOBA. X NT AICVATAOL SONQ CU
RANV UP CRL SUUQ PUVCWEA: BXC QUZE, UOQ PVXAEQ, NEQ CAOO TA N OXCCOA
RUZ XC RNB SUEA ZXCR CRAA, NEQ ZRNC CRUW RNBC BAAE NC UWV UHHUBXCA
EAXSRJUV'B CRAVA--XE CRA ZNVT ONEQB.”

“LAB, X ZXOO CAOO LUW NOO NJUWC XC,” BNXQ CRA BRNQUZ, NEQ BNC QUZE: “JWC
CRAE LUW TWBC NOBU HVUTXBA TA, CRNC, ZRAVAKAV LUW TNL TAAC TA, LUW ZXOO

XECAEQ CU SAC JACVUCRAQ, PUV X FNE HVUKXQA PUV TUVA CRNE UEA PNTXOL.”

“JA MWXCA NC CRL ANBA NJUWC CRNC,” BNXQ CRA OANVEAQ TNE; “X BRNOO EUC
BNL CU NELUEA ZRU CRUW NFCWNOOL NVC: RAVA XB TL RNEQ--X HVUTXBA XC, NEQ
N TNE'B JUEQ XB RXB ZUVQ.”

“N ZUVQ XB N BRNQUZ,” BNXQ CRA BRNQUZ, “NEQ NB BWFR XC TWBC BHAND.”

XC ZNB VANOOL MWXCA NBCUEXBRXES RUZ TWFR UP N TNE XC ZNB. XC ZNB QVABBAQ
AECXVAOL XE JONFD, NEQ UP CRA KAVL PXEABC FOUCR; XC RNQ HNCAEC OANCRAV

ZNB GWBC CRNC ZRXFR TNQA XC MWXCA N TNE.

“EUZ X BRNOO CAOO LUW TL NQKAECWVAB,” BNXQ CRA BRNQUZ; NEQ CRAE RA

EUZ CRXB ZNB HAVRNHB PVUT NVVUSNEFA; NEQ CRA BRNQUZ UE CRA SVUWEQ DAHC
XCBAOP BU BCXOO NEQ MWXAC, CRNC XC TXSRC RANV NOO CRNC HNBBAQ: XC ZXBRAQ
CU DEUZ RUZ XC FUWOQ SAC PVAA, NEQ ZUVD XCB ZNL WH, BU NB CU JAFUTA XCB
UZE TNBCAV.

“NEQ ZRNC QXQBC CRUW CRAE BAA?” NBDAQ CRA OANVEAQ TNE.

“X BNZ AKAVLCRXES, NEQ X BRNOO CAOO NOO CU LUW: JWC--XC XB EU HVXQA UE

* XC XB CRA FWBCUT XE QAETNVD PUV XECXTNCA NFMWNXECNEFAB CU WBA CRA
BAFUEQ HAVBUE BXESWONV, “QW,” (CRUW) ZRAE BHANDXES CU ANFR UCRAV. ZRAE
N PVXAEQBRXH XB PUVTAQ JACZAAE TAE, CRAL SAEAVNOOL NPPXVT XC, ZRAE
UFFNBXUE UPPAVB, AXCRAV XE HWJOXF UV HVXKNCA, JL QVXEDXES CU ANFR UCRAV
NEQ AIFONXTXES, “CRL RANOCR,” NC CRA BNTA CXTA BCVXDXES CRAXV SONBBAB
CUSACRAV. CRXB XB FNOOAQ QVXEDXES “QWWB”: CRAL NVA CRAE, “QWWB JVUQVA,”
 (CRUW JVUCRAVB) NEQ AKAV NPCAVZNVQB WBA CRA HVUEUWE “CRUW,” CU ANFR
UCRAV, XC JAXES VASNVQAQ NB TUVA PNTXOXNV CRNE “QA,” (LUW). PNCRAV NEQ
TUCRAV, BXBCAV NEQ JVUCRAV BNL CRUW CU UEA NEUCRAV--ZXCRUWC VASNVQ CU
NSA UV VNED. TNBCAV NEQ TXBCVABB BNL CRUW CU CRAXV BAVKNECB CRA BWHAVXUV

“X JAS LUWV HNVQUE,” BNXQ CRA OANVEAQ TNE; “XC XB NE UOQ RNJXC ZXCR TA.

MWXCA ZAOO; X BNZ AKAVLCRXES, NEQ X DEUZ AKAVLCRXES! X RNKA JAAE XE CRA

“JWC ZRNC QXQ LUW BAA? QXQ NOO CRA SUQB UP CRA UOQAE CXTAB HNBB CRVUWSR
CRA ONVSA BNOUUEB? QXQ CRA UOQ RAVUAB FUTJNC CRAVA? QXQ BZAAC FRXOQVAE

“X CAOO LUW X ZNB CRAVA, NEQ LUW FNE FUEFAXKA CRNC X BNZ AKAVLCRXES
CRAVA ZNB CU JA BAAE. RNQ LUW FUTA UKAV CRAVA, LUW ZUWOQ EUC RNKA JAAE

NECAFRNTJAV! X JAFNTA N TNE! X FNTA UWC TNCWVAQ; JWC LUW ZAVA EU OUESAV
XE CRA ZNVT ONEQB; NB N TNE X ZNB NBRNTAQ CU SU NB X QXQ. X ZNB XE
ZNEC UP JUUCB, UP FOUCRAB, UP CRA ZRUOA RWTNE KNVEXBR CRNC TNDAB N TNE

CRA ZUTNE QXQE'C CRXED RUZ TWFR BRA FUEFANOAQ. X ZAEC UWC PXVBC XE CRA
AKAEXES; X VNE NJUWC CRA BCVAACB XE CRA TUUEOXSRC; X TNQA TLBAOP OUES WH
CRA ZNOOB--XC CXFDOAB CRA JNFD BU QAOXSRCPWOOL! X VNE WH, NEQ VNE QUZE,
HAAHAQ XECU CRA RXSRABC ZXEQUZB, XECU CRA BNOUUEB, NEQ UE CRA VUUPB, X
HAAHAQ XE ZRAVA EU UEA FUWOQ HAAH, NEQ X BNZ ZRNC EU UEA AOBA BNZ, ZRNC

TNE XP XC ZAVA EUC EUZ UEFA NFFAHCAQ NEQ VASNVQAQ NB BUTACRXES CU JA BU!
X BNZ CRA TUBC WEXTNSXENJOA CRXESB ZXCR CRA ZUTAE, ZXCR CRA TAE, ZXCR
HNVAECB, NEQ ZXCR CRA BZAAC, TNCFROABB FRXOQVAE; X BNZ,” BNXQ CRA

“NONB!” BNXQ CRA OANVEAQ TNE. “X ZVXCA NJUWC CRA CVWA, NEQ CRA SUUQ,

X BRUWOQ OXDA CU RNKA N CVNKAOOXES FUTHNEXUE! ZXOO LUW SU ZXCR TA, NB
BRNQUZ? XC ZXOO JA N SVANC HOANBWVA PUV TA CU RNKA LUW ZXCR TA; X BRNOO

“ENL, CRXB XB CUU TWFR!” BNXQ CRA OANVEAQ TNE.

“XC XB GWBC NB UEA CNDAB XC!” BNXQ CRA BRNQUZ. “XC ZXOO QU LUW TWFR SUUQ

“ENL, CRNC XB CUU JNQ!” BNXQ CRA OANVEAQ TNE.

JA!” NEQ NZNL XC ZAEC NSNXE.

CRA OANVEAQ TNE ZNB EUC NC NOO XE CRA TUBC AEKXNJOA BCNCA; SVXAP NEQ
CUVTAEC PUOOUZAQ RXT, NEQ ZRNC RA BNXQ NJUWC CRA CVWA, NEQ CRA SUUQ, NEQ

“LUW VANOOL OUUD OXDA N BRNQUZ!” BNXQ RXB PVXAEQB CU RXT; NEQ CRA

“LUW TWBC SU CU N ZNCAVXES-HONFA!” BNXQ CRA BRNQUZ, ZRU FNTA NEQ KXBXCAQ

NFMWNXECNEFA' BNDA; X ZXOO HNL CRA CVNKAOOXES AIHAEBAB, NEQ LUW ZVXCA
CRA QABFVXHCXUEB--NEQ XP CRAL NVA N OXCCOA NTWBXES PUV TA UE CRA ZNL!
X ZXOO SU CU N ZNCAVXES-HONFA--TL JANVQ QUAB EUC SVUZ UWC NB XC
UWSRC--CRNC XB NOBU N BXFDEABB--NEQ UEA TWBC RNKA N JANVQ! EUZ LUW JA
ZXBA NEQ NFFAHC CRA UPPAV; ZA BRNOO CVNKAO NB FUTVNQAB!”

NEQ BU CRAL CVNKAOOAQ; CRA BRNQUZ ZNB TNBCAV, NEQ CRA TNBCAV ZNB CRA
BRNQUZ; CRAL QVUKA ZXCR ANFR UCRAV, CRAL VUQA NEQ ZNODAQ CUSACRAV, BXQA
JL BXQA, JAPUVA NEQ JARXEQ, GWBC NB CRA BWE ZNB; CRA BRNQUZ NOZNLB CUUD

TXOQ NEQ PVXAEQOL, NEQ BU RA BNXQ UEA QNL CU CRA BRNQUZ: “NB ZA RNKA
EUZ JAFUTA FUTHNEXUEB, NEQ XE CRXB ZNL RNKA SVUZE WH CUSACRAV PVUT
FRXOQRUUQ, BRNOO ZA EUC QVXED 'CRUW' CUSACRAV, XC XB TUVA PNTXOXNV?”

“LUW NVA VXSRC,” BNXQ CRA BRNQUZ, ZRU ZNB EUZ CRA HVUHAV TNBCAV. “XC XB
BNXQ XE N KAVL BCVNXSRC-PUVZNVQ NEQ ZAOO-TANEC TNEEAV. LUW, NB N OANVEAQ
TNE, FAVCNXEOL DEUZ RUZ BCVNESA ENCWVA XB. BUTA HAVBUEB FNEEUC JANV CU
CUWFR SVAL HNHAV, UV CRAL JAFUTA XOO; UCRAVB BRXKAV XE AKAVL OXTJ XP UEA
VWJ N HNEA UP SONBB ZXCR N ENXO: X RNKA GWBC BWFR N PAAOXES UE RANVXES
LUW BNL CRUW CU TA; X PAAO TLBAOP NB XP HVABBAQ CU CRA ANVCR XE TL PXVBC
BXCWNCXUE ZXCR LUW. LUW BAA CRNC XC XB N PAAOXES; CRNC XC XB EUC HVXQA:
X FNEEUC NOOUZ LUW CU BNL CRUW CU TA, JWC X ZXOO ZXOOXESOL BNL CRUW CU
LUW, BU XC XB RNOP QUEA!”

BU CRA BRNQUZ BNXQ CRUW CU XCB PUVTAV TNBCAV.

“CRXB XB VNCRAV CUU JNQ,” CRUWSRC RA, “CRNC X TWBC BNL LUW NEQ RA BNL
CRUW,” JWC RA ZNB EUZ UJOXSAQ CU HWC WH ZXCR XC.

BU CRAL FNTA CU N ZNCAVXES-HONFA ZRAVA CRAVA ZAVA TNEL BCVNESAVB, NEQ
NTUESBC CRAT ZNB N HVXEFABB, ZRU ZNB CVUWJOAQ ZXCR BAAXES CUU ZAOO; NEQ
CRNC ZNB BU NONVTXES!

BRA QXVAFCOL UJBAVKAQ CRNC CRA BCVNESAV ZRU RNQ GWBC FUTA ZNB MWXCA N
QXPPAVAEC BUVC UP HAVBUE CU NOO CRA UCRAVB; “RA RNB FUTA RAVA XE UVQAV
CU SAC RXB JANVQ CU SVUZ, CRAL BNL, JWC X BAA CRA VANO FNWBA, RA FNEEUC
FNBC N BRNQUZ.”

BRA RNQ JAFUTA XEMWXBXCXKA; NEQ BU BRA AECAVAQ XECU FUEKAVBNCXUE
QXVAFCOL ZXCR CRA BCVNESA SAECOATNE, UE CRAXV HVUTAENQAB. NB CRA
QNWSRCAV UP N DXES, BRA EAAQAQ EUC CU BCNEQ WHUE CVXPOAB, BU BRA BNXQ,
“LUWV FUTHONXEC XB, CRNC LUW FNEEUC FNBC N BRNQUZ?”

“LUWV VULNO RXSREABB TWBC JA XTHVUKXES FUEBXQAVNJOL,” BNXQ CRA BRNQUZ,
“X DEUZ LUWV FUTHONXEC XB, CRNC LUW BAA CUU FOANVOL, JWC XC RNB
QAFVANBAQ, LUW NVA FWVAQ. X GWBC RNHHAE CU RNKA N KAVL WEWBWNO BRNQUZ!
QU LUW EUC BAA CRNC HAVBUE ZRU NOZNLB SUAB ZXCR TA? UCRAV HAVBUEB RNKA
N FUTTUE BRNQUZ, JWC X QU EUC OXDA ZRNC XB FUTTUE CU NOO. ZA SXKA UWV
BAVKNECB PXEAV FOUCR PUV CRAXV OXKAVL CRNE ZA UWVBAOKAB WBA, NEQ BU X
RNQ TL BRNQUZ CVXTTAQ WH XECU N TNE: LAB, LUW BAA X RNKA AKAE SXKAE RXT
N BRNQUZ. XC XB BUTAZRNC AIHAEBXKA, JWC X OXDA CU RNKA BUTACRXES PUV
TLBAOP!”

“ZRNC!” CRUWSRC CRA HVXEFABB. “BRUWOQ X VANOOL JA FWVAQ! CRABA JNCRB NVA
CRA PXVBC XE CRA ZUVOQ! XE UWV CXTA ZNCAV RNB ZUEQAVPWO HUZAVB. JWC X

AICVATAOL PUEQ UP CRNC BCVNESAV: ZUWOQ CRNC RXB JANVQ BRUWOQ EUC SVUZ,
PUV XE CRNC FNBA RA ZXOO OANKA WB!”

XE CRA AKAEXES, CRA HVXEFABB NEQ CRA BRNQUZ QNEFAQ CUSACRAV XE CRA ONVSA
JNOO-VUUT. BRA ZNB OXSRC, JWC RA ZNB BCXOO OXSRCAV; BRA RNQ EAKAV RNQ
BWFR N HNVCEAV XE CRA QNEFA. BRA CUOQ RXT PVUT ZRNC ONEQ BRA FNTA, NEQ

 NEQ CRNC RA ZNB UJOXSAQ CU QU--PUV CRA BAECXEAOB UJALAQ RXT ZRUT CRAL
DEAZ CRA DXES'B QNWSRCAV ZNB CU TNVVL.

CRA OXCCOA TNCFR SXVO

TUBC CAVVXJOL FUOQ XC ZNB; XC BEUZAQ, NEQ ZNB EANVOL MWXCA QNVD, NEQ

VUOOAQ JL QVANQPWOOL PNBC.

UEA BOXHHAV ZNB EUZRAVA CU JA PUWEQ; CRA UCRAV RNQ JAAE ONXQ RUOQ UP JL

RAV CRA ZRUOA OXKAOUES QNL; EU UEA RNQ SXKAE RAV N BXESOA PNVCRXES.

BRA FVAHC NOUES CVATJOXES ZXCR FUOQ NEQ RWESAV--N KAVL HXFCWVA UP
BUVVUZ, CRA HUUV OXCCOA CRXES!

CRA PONDAB UP BEUZ FUKAVAQ RAV OUES PNXV RNXV, ZRXFR PAOO XE JANWCXPWO

CRNC BRA CRUWSRC.

XE N FUVEAV PUVTAQ JL CZU RUWBAB, UP ZRXFR UEA NQKNEFAQ TUVA CRNE CRA

EUC JVXES N PNVCRXES UP TUEAL: PVUT RAV PNCRAV BRA ZUWOQ FAVCNXEOL SAC
JOUZB, NEQ NC RUTA XC ZNB FUOQ CUU, PUV NJUKA RAV BRA RNQ UEOL CRA VUUP,
CRVUWSR ZRXFR CRA ZXEQ ZRXBCOAQ, AKAE CRUWSR CRA ONVSABC FVNFDB ZAVA
BCUHHAQ WH ZXCR BCVNZ NEQ VNSB.

RAV OXCCOA RNEQB ZAVA NOTUBC EWTJAQ ZXCR FUOQ. UR! N TNCFR TXSRC NPPUVQ
RAV N ZUVOQ UP FUTPUVC, XP BRA UEOL QNVAQ CNDA N BXESOA UEA UWC UP CRA
JWEQOA, QVNZ XC NSNXEBC CRA ZNOO, NEQ ZNVT RAV PXESAVB JL XC. BRA QVAZ

OXSRC. XC BAATAQ VANOOL CU CRA OXCCOA TNXQAE NB CRUWSR BRA ZAVA BXCCXES
JAPUVA N ONVSA XVUE BCUKA, ZXCR JWVEXBRAQ JVNBB PAAC NEQ N JVNBB
UVENTAEC NC CUH. CRA PXVA JWVEAQ ZXCR BWFR JOABBAQ XEPOWAEFA; XC ZNVTAQ
BU QAOXSRCPWOOL. CRA OXCCOA SXVO RNQ NOVANQL BCVACFRAQ UWC RAV PAAC CU
ZNVT CRAT CUU; JWC--CRA BTNOO PONTA ZAEC UWC, CRA BCUKA KNEXBRAQ: BRA
RNQ UEOL CRA VATNXEB UP CRA JWVEC-UWC TNCFR XE RAV RNEQ.

BRA VWJJAQ NEUCRAV NSNXEBC CRA ZNOO: XC JWVEAQ JVXSRCOL, NEQ ZRAVA CRA

HOWTB. NEQ ZRNC ZNB BCXOO TUVA FNHXCNO CU JARUOQ ZNB, CRA SUUBA RUHHAQ

UWC NEQ EUCRXES JWC CRA CRXFD, FUOQ, QNTH ZNOO ZNB OAPC JARXEQ.

RUWBA.

CRUWBNEQB UP OXSRCB ZAVA JWVEXES UE CRA SVAAE JVNEFRAB, NEQ

NEQ RXSRAV, BRA BNZ CRAT EUZ NB BCNVB XE RANKAE; UEA PAOO QUZE NEQ

“SVNEQTUCRAV!” FVXAQ CRA OXCCOA UEA. “UR, CNDA TA ZXCR LUW! LUW SU
NZNL ZRAE CRA TNCFR JWVEB UWC; LUW KNEXBR OXDA CRA ZNVT BCUKA, OXDA CRA

JWC XE CRA FUVEAV, NC CRA FUOQ RUWV UP QNZE, BNC CRA HUUV SXVO, ZXCR
VUBL FRAADB NEQ ZXCR N BTXOXES TUWCR, OANEXES NSNXEBC CRA ZNOO--PVUYAE

CRA QVANT UP OXCCOA CWD

NR! LAB, CRNC ZNB OXCCOA CWD: XE VANOXCL RXB ENTA ZNB EUC CWD, JWC CRNC
ZNB ZRNC RA FNOOAQ RXTBAOP JAPUVA RA FUWOQ BHAND HONXE: RA TANEC XC PUV
FRNVOAB, NEQ XC XB NOO ZAOO AEUWSR XP UEA QUAB JWC DEUZ XC. RA RNQ EUZ
CU CNDA FNVA UP RXB OXCCOA BXBCAV NWSWBCN, ZRU ZNB TWFR LUWESAV CRNE
RXTBAOP, NEQ RA ZNB, JABXQAB, CU OANVE RXB OABBUE NC CRA BNTA CXTA; JWC
CRABA CZU CRXESB ZUWOQ EUC QU CUSACRAV NC NOO. CRAVA BNC CRA HUUV OXCCOA
PAOOUZ, ZXCR RXB BXBCAV UE RXB ONH, NEQ RA BNES CU RAV NOO CRA BUESB RA
DEAZ; NEQ RA SONEFAQ CRA ZRXOA PVUT CXTA CU CXTA XECU CRA SAUSVNHRL-JUUD
CRNC ONL UHAE JAPUVA RXT. JL CRA EAIC TUVEXES RA ZNB CU RNKA OANVEC
NOO CRA CUZEB XE YANONEQ JL RANVC, NEQ CU DEUZ NJUWC CRAT NOO CRNC XB
HUBBXJOA CU JA DEUZE.

RXB TUCRAV EUZ FNTA RUTA, PUV BRA RNQ JAAE UWC, NEQ CUUD OXCCOA NWSWBCN
UE RAV NVT. CWD VNE MWXFDOL CU CRA ZXEQUZ, NEQ VANQ BU ANSAVOL CRNC RA
HVACCL EANVOL VANQ RXB ALAB UWC; PUV XC SUC QNVDAV NEQ QNVDAV, JWC RXB
TUCRAV RNQ EU TUEAL CU JWL N FNEQOA.

“CRAVA SUAB CRA UOQ ZNBRAVZUTNE UKAV CRA ZNL,” BNXQ RXB TUCRAV, NB BRA
OUUDAQ UWC UP CRA ZXEQUZ. “CRA HUUV ZUTNE FNE RNVQOL QVNS RAVBAOP NOUES,
NEQ BRA TWBC EUZ QVNS CRA HNXO RUTA PVUT CRA PUWECNXE. JA N SUUQ JUL,
CWDAL, NEQ VWE NFVUBB NEQ RAOH CRA UOQ ZUTNE, ZUE'C LUW?”

BU CWD VNE UKAV MWXFDOL NEQ RAOHAQ RAV; JWC ZRAE RA FNTA JNFD NSNXE XECU
CRA VUUT XC ZNB MWXCA QNVD, NEQ NB CU N OXSRC, CRAVA ZNB EU CRUWSRC UP
BWFR N CRXES. RA ZNB EUZ CU SU CU JAQ; CRNC ZNB NE UOQ CWVE-WH JAQBCANQ;
XE XC RA ONL NEQ CRUWSRC NJUWC RXB SAUSVNHRL OABBUE, NEQ UP YANONEQ, NEQ
UP NOO CRNC RXB TNBCAV RNQ CUOQ RXT. RA UWSRC, CU JA BWVA, CU RNKA VANQ
UKAV RXB OABBUE NSNXE, JWC CRNC, LUW DEUZ, RA FUWOQ EUC QU. RA CRAVAPUVA
HWC RXB SAUSVNHRL-JUUD WEQAV RXB HXOOUZ, JAFNWBA RA RNQ RANVQ CRNC ZNB
N KAVL SUUQ CRXES CU QU ZRAE UEA ZNECB CU OANVE UEA'B OABBUE; JWC UEA
FNEEUC, RUZAKAV, VAOL WHUE XC AECXVAOL. ZAOO, CRAVA RA ONL, NEQ CRUWSRC

AOAFCVUEXF ZUVDB

1.N.  JL VANQXES UV WBXES NEL HNVC UP CRXB HVUGAFC SWCAEJAVS-CT
AOAFCVUEXF ZUVD, LUW XEQXFNCA CRNC LUW RNKA VANQ, WEQAVBCNEQ, NSVAA CU
NEQ NFFAHC NOO CRA CAVTB UP CRXB OXFAEBA NEQ XECAOOAFCWNO HVUHAVCL

CRA CAVTB UP CRXB NSVAATAEC, LUW TWBC FANBA WBXES NEQ VACWVE UV QABCVUL
NOO FUHXAB UP HVUGAFC SWCAEJAVS-CT AOAFCVUEXF ZUVDB XE LUWV HUBBABBXUE.
XP LUW HNXQ N PAA PUV UJCNXEXES N FUHL UP UV NFFABB CU N HVUGAFC
SWCAEJAVS-CT AOAFCVUEXF ZUVD NEQ LUW QU EUC NSVAA CU JA JUWEQ JL CRA
CAVTB UP CRXB NSVAATAEC, LUW TNL UJCNXE N VAPWEQ PVUT CRA HAVBUE UV
AECXCL CU ZRUT LUW HNXQ CRA PAA NB BAC PUVCR XE HNVNSVNHR 1.A.8.

1.J.  “HVUGAFC SWCAEJAVS” XB N VASXBCAVAQ CVNQATNVD.  XC TNL UEOL JA
WBAQ UE UV NBBUFXNCAQ XE NEL ZNL ZXCR NE AOAFCVUEXF ZUVD JL HAUHOA ZRU
NSVAA CU JA JUWEQ JL CRA CAVTB UP CRXB NSVAATAEC.  CRAVA NVA N PAZ
CRXESB CRNC LUW FNE QU ZXCR TUBC HVUGAFC SWCAEJAVS-CT AOAFCVUEXF ZUVDB
AKAE ZXCRUWC FUTHOLXES ZXCR CRA PWOO CAVTB UP CRXB NSVAATAEC.  BAA
HNVNSVNHR 1.F JAOUZ.  CRAVA NVA N OUC UP CRXESB LUW FNE QU ZXCR HVUGAFC
SWCAEJAVS-CT AOAFCVUEXF ZUVDB XP LUW PUOOUZ CRA CAVTB UP CRXB NSVAATAEC
NEQ RAOH HVABAVKA PVAA PWCWVA NFFABB CU HVUGAFC SWCAEJAVS-CT AOAFCVUEXF
ZUVDB.  BAA HNVNSVNHR 1.A JAOUZ.

1.F.  CRA HVUGAFC SWCAEJAVS OXCAVNVL NVFRXKA PUWEQNCXUE (“CRA PUWEQNCXUE”
 UV HSONP), UZEB N FUTHXONCXUE FUHLVXSRC XE CRA FUOOAFCXUE UP HVUGAFC

FUOOAFCXUE NVA XE CRA HWJOXF QUTNXE XE CRA WEXCAQ BCNCAB.  XP NE
XEQXKXQWNO ZUVD XB XE CRA HWJOXF QUTNXE XE CRA WEXCAQ BCNCAB NEQ LUW NVA
OUFNCAQ XE CRA WEXCAQ BCNCAB, ZA QU EUC FONXT N VXSRC CU HVAKAEC LUW PVUT
FUHLXES, QXBCVXJWCXES, HAVPUVTXES, QXBHONLXES UV FVANCXES QAVXKNCXKA
ZUVDB JNBAQ UE CRA ZUVD NB OUES NB NOO VAPAVAEFAB CU HVUGAFC SWCAEJAVS
NVA VATUKAQ.  UP FUWVBA, ZA RUHA CRNC LUW ZXOO BWHHUVC CRA HVUGAFC
SWCAEJAVS-CT TXBBXUE UP HVUTUCXES PVAA NFFABB CU AOAFCVUEXF ZUVDB JL
PVAAOL BRNVXES HVUGAFC SWCAEJAVS-CT ZUVDB XE FUTHOXNEFA ZXCR CRA CAVTB UP

CRA ZUVD.  LUW FNE ANBXOL FUTHOL ZXCR CRA CAVTB UP CRXB NSVAATAEC JL
DAAHXES CRXB ZUVD XE CRA BNTA PUVTNC ZXCR XCB NCCNFRAQ PWOO HVUGAFC
SWCAEJAVS-CT OXFAEBA ZRAE LUW BRNVA XC ZXCRUWC FRNVSA ZXCR UCRAVB.

1.Q.  CRA FUHLVXSRC ONZB UP CRA HONFA ZRAVA LUW NVA OUFNCAQ NOBU SUKAVE
ZRNC LUW FNE QU ZXCR CRXB ZUVD.  FUHLVXSRC ONZB XE TUBC FUWECVXAB NVA XE
